001,001 – Praise to the Lord
001,1
001,Praise to the Lord, the Almighty
001,the King of creation!
001,O my soul, praise Him, for He
001,is thy health and salvation!
001,All ye who hear
001,now to His temple draw near;
001,Join ye in glad adoration!
001,2
001,Praise to the Lord, Who o’er all things
001,so wondrously reigneth
001,Shieldeth thee under His wings, yea
001,so gently sustaineth!
001,Hast thou not seen how thy
001,desires e’er have been
001,Granted in what He ordaineth?
001,3
001,Praise to the Lord, who doth prosper
001,thy work and defend thee;
001,Surely His goodness and mercy
001,here daily attend thee.
001,Ponder anew what the Almighty can do
001,If with His love He befriend thee.
002,002 – All Creatures of Our God and King
002,1
002,All creatures of our God and King
002,Lift up your voice and with us sing
002,Alleluia! Alleluia!
002,O burning sun with golden beam
002,And silver moon with softer gleam!
002,Refrain
002,O praise Him! O praise Him!
002,Alleluia! Alleluia! Alleluia!
002,2
002,O rushing wind and breezes soft
002,O clouds that ride the winds aloft
002,O praise Him! Alleluia!
002,O rising morn, in praise rejoice
002,O lights of evening, find a voice!
002,3
002,O flowing waters, pure and clear
002,Make music for your Lord to hear
002,O praise Him! Alleluia!
002,O fire so masterful and bright
002,Providing us with warmth and light.
002,4
002,Let all things their Creator bless
002,And worship Him in humbleness
002,O praise Him! Alleluia!
002,Oh, praise the Father, praise the Son
002,And praise the Spirit, three in One!
003,003 – God Himself Is With Us
003,1
003,God Himself is with us;
003,Let us all adore Him
003,And with awe appear before Him.
003,God is here within us;
003,Soul, in silence fear Him
003,Humbly, fervently draw near Him.
003,Now His own who have known God
003,In worship lowly
003,Yield their spirits wholly.
003,2
003,Come, abide within me;
003,Let my soul, like Mary
003,Be Thine earthly sanctuary.
003,Come, indwelling Spirit
003,With transfigured splendor;
003,Love and honor will I render.
003,Where I go here below
003,Let me bow before Thee
003,Know Thee and adore Thee.
003,3
003,Gladly we surrender
003,Earth’s deceitful treasures
003,Pride of life and sinful pleasures:
003,Gladly, Lord, we offer
003,Thine to be forever
003,Soul and life and each endeavor.
003,Thou alone shall be known
003,Lord of all our being
003,Life’s true way decreeing.
004,004 – Praise, My Soul, the King of Heaven
004,1
004,Praise, my soul, the King of heaven;
004,To his feet thy tribute bring;
004,Ransomed, healed, restored, forgiven
004,Who like thee His praise should sing?
004,Praise Him, praise Him, alleluia!
004,Praise the everlasting King.
004,2
004,Praise him for his grace and favor
004,To our fathers in distress;
004,Praise him still the same forever
004,Slow to chide and swift to bless:
004,Praise Him, praise Him, alleluia!
004,Glorious in His faithfulness.
004,3
004,Tenderly He shields and spares us;
004,Well our feeble frame he knows;
004,In his hands He gently bears us
004,Rescues us from all our foes.
004,Praise Him, praise Him, alleluia!
004,Widely yet his mercy flows.
004,4
004,Angels, help us to adore him;
004,Ye behold him face to face;
004,Sun and moon, bow down before him
004,Dwellers all in time and space.
004,Praise Him, praise Him, alleluia!
004,Praise with us the God of grace.
005,005 – All My Hope on God Is Founded
005,1
005,All my hope on God is founded;
005,He doth still my trust renew.
005,Me through change and chance He guideth
005,Only good and only true.
005,God unknown, He alone
005,Calls my heart to be His own.
005,2
005,Pride of man and earthly glory
005,Sword and crown betray his trust;
005,What with care and toil he buildeth
005,Tower and temple fall to dust.
005,But God’s power, hour by hour
005,Is my temple and my tower.
005,3
005,God’s great goodness aye endureth
005,Deep His wisdom, passing thought;
005,Splendor, light and life attend Him
005,Beauty springeth out of naught.
005,Love doth stand at His hand;
005,Joy doth wait on His command.
005,4
005,Still from man to God eternal
005,Sacrifice of praise be done.
005,High above all praises praising
005,For the gift of Christ His son.
005,Christ doth call one and all:
005,Ye who follow shall not fall.
006,006 – O Worship the Lord
006,1
006,O worship the Lord
006,in the beauty of holiness
006,Bow down before Him
006,His glory proclaim;
006,With gold of obedience
006,and incense of lowliness
006,Kneel and adore Him:
006,the Lord is His name.
006,2
006,Low at His feet
006,lay thy burden of carefulness
006,High on His heart
006,He will bear it for thee
006,Comfort thy sorrows
006,and answer thy prayerfulness
006,Guiding thy steps
006,as may best for thee be.
006,3
006,Fear not to enter
006,His courts in the slenderness
006,Of the poor wealth
006,thou wouldst reckon as thine;
006,Truth in its beauty
006,and love in its tenderness
006,These are the offerings
006,to lay on His shrine.
006,4
006,These, though we bring them
006,in trembling and fearfulness
006,He will accept
006,for the name that is dear;
006,Mornings of joy give
006,for evenings of tearfulness
006,Trust for our trembling
006,and hope for our fear.
007,007 – The Lord in Zion Reigneth
007,1
007,The Lord in Zion reigneth
007,let all the world rejoice
007,And come before His throne of grace
007,with tuneful heart and voice;
007,The Lord in Zion reigneth
007,and there His praise shall ring
007,To Him shall princes bend the knee
007,and kings their glory bring.
007,2
007,The Lord in Zion reigneth
007,and who so great as He?
007,The depths of earth are in His hands;
007,He rules the mighty sea.
007,O crown His Name with honor
007,and let His standard wave
007,Till distant isles beyond the deep
007,shall own His power to save.
007,3
007,The Lord in Zion reigneth
007,these hours to Him belong;
007,O enter now His temple gates
007,and fill His courts with song;
007,Beneath His royal banner
007,let every creature fall
007,Exalt the King of heaven and earth
007,and crown Him Lord of all.
008,008 – We Gather Together
008,1
008,We gather together to ask
008,the Lord’s blessing;
008,He chastens and hastens
008,His will to make known.
008,The wicked oppressing
008,now cease from distressing.
008,Sing praises to His Name;
008,He forgets not His own.
008,2
008,Beside us to guide us
008,our God with us joining
008,Ordaining, maintaining
008,His kingdom divine;
008,So from the beginning
008,the fight we were winning;
008,Thou, Lord, were at our side
008,all glory be Thine!
008,3
008,We all do extol Thee
008,Thou leader triumphant
008,And pray that Thou still
008,our defender wilt be.
008,Let Thy congregation
008,escape tribulation;
008,Thy name be ever praised!
008,O Lord, make us free!
009,009 – Let All the World in Every Corner Sing
009,1
009,Let all the world in every corner sing
009,My God and King!
009,The heavens are not too high
009,His praise may thither fly;
009,The earth is not too low
009,His praises there may grow.
009,Let all the world in every corner sing
009,My God and King!
009,2
009,Let all the world in every corner sing
009,My God and King!
009,The church with psalms must shout
009,No door can keep them out;
009,But, above all, the heart
009,must bear the longest part.
009,Let all the world in every corner sing
009,My God and King!
010,010 – Come, Christians, Join to Sing
010,1
010,Come, Christians, join to sing
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,Loud praise to Christ our King;
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,Let all, with heart and voice
010,Before His throne rejoice;
010,Praise is His gracious choice:
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,2
010,Come, lift your hearts on high;
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,Let praises fill the sky;
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,He is our Guide and Friend;
010,To us He’ll condescend;
010,His love shall never end:
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,3
010,Praise yet our Christ again;
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,Life shall not end the strain;
010,Alleluia! Amen!
010,On heaven’s blissful shore
010,His goodness we’ll adore
010,Singing forevermore
010,Alleluia! Amen!
011,011 – The God of Abraham Praise
011,1
011,The God of Abraham praise
011,Who reigns enthroned above;
011,Ancient of everlasting days
011,And God of love;
011,Jehovah! Great I AM!
011,By earth and heaven confessed;
011,I bow and bless the sacred name
011,Forever blest.
011,2
011,The God of Abraham praise
011,At whose supreme command
011,From earth I rise, and seek the joys
011,At His right hand;
011,I all on earth forsake
011,Its wisdom, fame and power;
011,And Him my only portion make
011,My shield and tower.
011,3
011,The whole triumphant host
011,Give thanks to God on high;
011,“Hail, Father, Son, and Holy Ghost!”
011,They ever cry;
011,Hail, Abraham’s God and mine!
011,I join the heavenly lays;
011,All might and majesty are Thine
011,And endless praise.
012,012 – Joyful, Joyful, We Adore Thee
012,1
012,Joyful, joyful, we adore Thee
012,God of glory, Lord of love;
012,Hearts unfold like flow’rs before Thee
012,Hail Thee as the sun above.
012,Melt the clouds of sin and sadness
012,Drive the dark of doubt away;
012,Giver of immortal gladness
012,Fill us with the light of day!
012,2
012,All Thy works with joy surround Thee
012,Earth and heav’n reflect Thy rays
012,Stars and angels sing around Thee
012,Center of unbroken praise;
012,Field and forest, vale and mountain
012,Bloss’ming meadow, flashing sea
012,Chanting bird and flowing fountain
012,Call us to rejoice in Thee.
012,3
012,Thou art giving and forgiving
012,Ever blessing, ever blest
012,Wellspring of the joy of living
012,Oceandepth of happy rest!
012,Thou the father, Christ our Brother –
012,All who live in love are Thine:
012,Teach us how to love each other
012,Lift us to the joy divine.
013,013 – New Songs of Celebration Render
013,1
013,New songs of celebration render
013,To Him who has great wonders done.
013,Love sits enthroned in ageless splendor:
013,Come, and adore the mighty One.
013,He has made known His great salvation
013,Which all His friends with joy confess:
013,He has revealed to every nation
013,His everlasting righteousness.
013,2
013,Joyfully, heartily resounding
013,Let every instrument and voice
013,Peal out the praise of grace abounding
013,Calling the whole world to rejoice.
013,Trumpets and organs, set in motion
013,Such sounds as make the heavens ring;
013,All things that live in earth and ocean
013,Make music for your mighty King.
013,3
013,Rivers and seas and torrents roaring
013,Honor the Lord with wild acclaim;
013,Mountains and stones look up adoring
013,And find a voice to praise His name.
013,Righteous, commanding, ever glorious
013,Praises be His that never cease:
013,Just is our God, whose truth victorious
013,Establishes the world in peace.

015,015 – My Maker and My King
015,1
015,My Maker and my King
015,To Thee my all I owe;
015,Thy sovereign bounty is the spring
015,Whence all my blessings flow;
015,Thy sovereign bounty is the spring
015,Whence all my blessings flow.
015,2

015,On Thee alone I live;
015,My God, Thy benefits demand
015,More praise than I can give.
015,My God, Thy benefits demand
015,More praise than I can give.
015,3
015,Lord, what can I impart
015,When all is Thine before?
015,Thy love demands a thankful heart;
015,The gift, alas! how poor.
015,Thy love demands a thankful heart;
015,The gift, alas! how poor.
015,4
015,O! let Thy grace inspire
015,My soul with strength divine;
015,Let every word each desire
015,And all my days be Thine.
015,Let every word each desire
015,And all my days be Thine.
016,016 – All People That on Earth Do Well
016,1
016,All people that on earth do dwell
016,sing to the Lord with cheerful voice.
016,Him serve with mirth, his praise forth tell;
016,come ye before him and rejoice.
016,2
016,Know that the Lord is God indeed;
016,without our aid he did us make;
016,we are his folk, he doth us feed
016,and for his sheep he doth us take.
016,3
016,O enter then his gates with praise;
016,approach with joy his courts unto;
016,praise, laud, and bless his name always
016,for it is seemly so to do.
016,4
016,For why! the Lord our God is good;
016,his mercy is forever sure;
016,his truth at all times firmly stood
016,and shall from age to age endure.
017,017 – Lord of All Being, Throned Afar
017,1
017,Lord of all being, throned afar
017,Thy glory flames from sun and star;
017,Center and soul of every sphere
017,Yet to each loving heart how near!
017,Yet to each loving heart how near!
017,2
017,Sun of our life, Thy quickening ray
017,Shed on our path the glow of day;
017,Star of our hope, Thy softened light
017,Cheers the long watches of the night
017,Cheers the long watches of the night.
017,3
017,Our midnight is Thy smile withdrawn;
017,Our noontide is Thy gracious dawn;
017,Our rainbow arch, Thy mercy’s sign;
017,All, save the clouds of sin, are Thine
017,All, save the clouds of sin, are Thine.
017,4
017,Lord of all life, below, above
017,Whose light is truth, whose warmth is love
017,Before Thy ever-blazing throne
017,We ask no luster of our own
017,We ask no luster of our own.
017,5
017,Grant us Thy truth to make us free
017,And kindling hearts that burn for Thee;
017,Till all Thy living altars claim
017,One holy light, one heavenly flame!
017,One holy light, one heavenly flame.
018,018 – O Morning Star, How Fair and Bright
018,1
018,O Morning Star, how fair and bright!
018,You shine with God’s own truth and light
018,Aglow with grace and mercy!
018,Of Jacob’s race, King David’s son
018,Our Lord and Master, You have won
018,Our hearts to serve You only!
018,Lowly, holy!
018,Great and Glorious, all victorious
018,Rich in blessing! Rule and might
018,o’er all possessing!
018,2
018,Lord, when you look on us in love
018,At once there falls from God above
018,A ray of purest pleasure.
018,Your Word and Spirit, flesh and blood
018,Refresh our souls with heav-‘nly food.
018,You are our dearest treasure!
018,Let Your mercy warm and cheer us!
018,O draw near us! For You teach us
018,God’s own love through
018,You has reached us.
018,3
018,Almighty Father, in Your Son
018,You loved us, when not yet begun
018,Was this old earth’s foundation!
018,Your Son has ransomed us in love
018,To live in Him here and above:
018,This is Your great salvation.
018,Alleluia! Christ the living
018,To us giving life forever
018,Keeps us Yours and fails us never!
018,4
018,O let the harps break forth in sound!
018,Our joy be all with music crowned
018,Our voices gaily blending!
018,For Christ goes with us all the way
018,Today, tomorrow, every day!
018,His love is never ending!
018,Sing out! Ring out!
018,Jubilation! Exultation!
018,Tell the story!
018,Great is He, the King of glory!

019,The victory have won.

019,Acclaim the Lord our King!
019,3

019,The world and dwellers there
019,And let the rivers clap their hands
019,The hills their joy declare.
019,4
019,Before the Lord: because He comes
019,To judge the earth come He;
019,He’ll judge the world
019,with righteousness
019,His folk with equity.

020,Ye angels of light;
020,Ye heavens, adore Him
020,By whom ye were made
020,And worship before Him
020,In brightness arrayed.
020,2

020,Praise Him upon earth
020,In tuneful accord:
020,Ye sons of new birth;
020,Praise Him who hath brought
020,you His grace from above
020,Praise Him who hath taught you
020,To sing of His love.
020,3
020,O praise ye the Lord
020,All things that give sound;
020,Each jubilant chord
020,Re-echo around;
020,Loud organs His glory
020,Forth tell in deep tone
020,And sweet harp, the story
020,Of what He hath done.
020,4
020,O praise ye the Lord!
020,Thanksgiving and song
020,To Him be outpoured

020,For love in creation

021,021 – Immortal, Invisible, God Only Wise
021,1
021,Immortal, invisible
021,God only wise
021,In light inaccessible
021,hid from our eyes
021,Most blessed, most glorious
021,the Ancient of Days
021,Almighty, victorious
021,Thy great Name we praise.
021,2
021,Unresting, unhasting
021,and silent as light
021,Nor wanting, nor wasting
021,Thou rulest in might;
021,Thy justice, like mountains
021,high soaring above
021,Thy clouds, which are fountains
021,of goodness and love.
021,3
021,To all, life Thou givest
021,to both great and small;
021,In all life Thou livest
021,the true life of all;
021,We blossom and flourish
021,as leaves on the tree
021,And wither and perish
021,but naught changeth Thee.
021,4
021,Great Father of glory
021,pure Father of light
021,Thine angels adore Thee
021,all veiling their sight;
021,All praise we would render;
021,O help us to see
021,‘Tis only the splendor
021,of light hideth Thee!
022,022 – God Is Our Song
022,1
022,God is our Song, and every singer blest
022,Who praising Him finds energy and rest.
022,All who praise God with unaffected joy
022,Give back to us the widom we destroy
022,Give back to us the widom we destroy.
022,2
022,God is our Song, for Jesus comes to save;
022,While praising Him we offer all we have.
022,New songs we sing, in ventures new unite
022,When Jesus leads us upward into light
022,When Jesus leads us upward into light.
022,3
022,This is our Song no conflict ever drowns;
022,Who praises God our human wrath disowns.
022,Love knows what rich complexities of sound
022,God builds upon a simple common ground
022,God builds upon a simple common ground.
022,4
022,God is our Silence when no songs are sung
022,When ecstasy or sorrow stills the tongue.
022,Glorious the faith which silently obeys
022,Until we find again the voice of praise
022,Until we find again the voice of praise.

023,Where the mountains praise the Lord!
023,3

029,To God all praise and glory!
029,2
029,What God’s almighty power hath made
029,His gracious mercy keepeth;
029,By morning glow or evening shade
029,His watchful eye ne’er sleepeth
029,Within the kingdom of his might
029,Lo! all is just, and all is right:
029,To God all praise and glory!
029,3
029,The Lord is never far away
029,throughout all grief distressing
029,an ever present help and stay
029,our peace and joy and blessing.
029,As with a mother’s tender hand
029,He leads His own, His chosen band:
029,To God all praise and glory!
029,4
029,Then all my gladsome way along
029,I sing aloud thy praises
029,that men may hear the grateful song
029,my voice unwearied raises:
029,Be joyful in the Lord, my heart!
029,both soul and body bear your part!
029,To God all praise and glory.
030,030 – Holy God, We Praise Your Name
030,1
030,Holy God, we praise Your name;
030,Lord of all, we bow before You!
030,All on earth Your scepter claim
030,All in heaven above adore You;
030,Infinite Your vast domain.
030,Everlasting is Your reign.
030,2
030,Hark! the loud celestial hymn
030,Angel choirs above are raising
030,Cherubim and seraphim
030,In unceasing chorus praising;
030,Fill the heavens with sweet accord:
030,Holy, holy, holy, Lord.
030,3
030,Holy Father, Holy Son
030,Holy Spirit, three we name You;
030,While in essence only one
030,Undivided God we claim You;
030,And adoring bend the knee
030,While we own the mystery.
031,031 – Tell Out, My Soul
031,1
031,Tell out my soul, the greatness of the Lord:
031,Unnumbered blessings, give my spirit voice;
031,Tender to me the promise of His Word;
031,In God my Saviour shall my heart rejoice.
031,2
031,Tell out, my soul, the greatness of His name:
031,Make known His might, the deeds His arm has done;
031,His mercy sure, from age to age the same;
031,His holy name, the Lord, the Mighty One.
031,3
031,Tell out, my soul, the greatness of His might:
031,Pow’rs and dominions lay their glory by;
031,Proud hearts and stubborn wills are put to flight
031,The hungry fed, the humble lifted high.
031,4
031,Tell out, my soul, the glories of His word:
031,Firm is His promise, and His mercy sure.
031,Tell out, my soul, the greatness of the Lord
031,To children’s children and forevermore.
032,032 – When in Our Music God is Glorified
032,1
032,When in our music God is glorified
032,And adoration leaves no room for pride
032,It is as though the whole creation cried:
032,Alleluia!
032,2
032,How oft, in making music, we have found
032,A new dimension in the world of sound
032,As worship moved us to a more profound
032,Alleluia!
032,3
032,And did not Jesus sing a psalm that night
032,When utmost evil strove against the light?
032,Then let us sing for whom He won the fight:
032,Alleluia!
032,4
032,Let every instrument be used for praise;
032,Let all rejoice who have a voice to raise;
032,And may God give us faith to sing always:
032,Alleluia!
033,033 – Sing a New Song to the Lord
033,1
033,Sing a new song to the Lord
033,He to whom wonders belong.
033,Rejoice in His triumph and tell of His power.
033,O sing a new song to the Lord.
033,2
033,Now to the ends of the earth
033,See His salvation is shown.
033,And still He remembers His mercy and truth
033,Unchanging in love to His own.
033,3
033,Sing a new song and rejoice.
033,Publish His praises abroad.
033,Let voices in chorus with trumpet and horn
033,Resound for the joy of the Lord.
033,4
033,Join with the hills and the sea
033,Thunders of praise to prolong.
033,In judgement and justice
033,He comes to the earth
033,O sing a new song to the Lord.
034,034 – Wake the Song
034,1
034,Wake the song of joy and gladness;
034,Hither bring your noblest lays;
034,Banish every thought of sadness
034,Pouring forth your highest praise.
034,Sing to Him whose care has brought us
034,Once again with friends to meet
034,And whose loving voice has taught us
034,Of the way to Jesus’ feet.
034,Refrain
034,Wake the song, wake the song
034,The song of joy and gladness
034,Wake the song, wake the song
034,The song of Jubilee.
034,2
034,Joyfully with songs and banners
034,We will greet the festal day;
034,Shout aloud our glad hosannas
034,And our grateful homage pay.
034,We will chant our Savior’s glory
034,while our thoughts we raise above
034,Telling still the old, old, story
034,Precious theme- redeeming love!
034,3
034,Thanks to Thee, O holy Father
034,For the mercies of the year;
034,May each heart, as here we gather
034,Swell with gratitude sincere
034,Thanks to Thee, O loving Savior
034,For redemption through Thy blood.
034,Breathe upon us, Holy Spirit
034,Sweetly draw us near to God.
035,035 – With Songs and Honors
035,1
035,With songs and honors sounding loud
035,Address the Lord on high;
035,Over the heavens He spreads His cloud
035,And waters veil the sky.
035,2
035,He sends His showers of blessing down
035,To cheer the plains below;
035,He makes the grass the mountains crown
035,And corning valleys grow.
035,3
035,His steady counsels change the face
035,Of the declining year;
035,He bids the sun cut short his race
035,And wintry days appear.
035,4
035,He sends His word, and melts the snow;
035,The fields no longer mourn;
035,He calls the warmer gales to blow
035,And bids the spring return.
035,5
035,The changing wind, the flying cloud
035,Obey His mighty word:
035,With songs and honors sounding loud
035,Praise ye the sovereign Lord!
036,036 – O Thou in Whose Presence
036,1
036,O Thou in whose presence my soul takes delight
036,On whom in affliction I call
036,My comfort by day and my song in the night
036,My hope, my salvation, my all!
036,2
036,His voice, as the sound of the dulcimer sweet
036,Is heard through the shadows of death;
036,The cedars of Lebanon bow at His feet
036,The air is perfumed with His breath.
036,3
036,His lips, as a fountain of righteousness flow
036,To water the gardens of grace;
036,From which their salvation the Gentiles shall know
036,And bask in the smiles of His face.
036,4
036,He looks, and ten thousands of angels rejoice
036,And myriads wait for His word;
036,He speaks, and eternity, filled with His voice
036,Re-echoes the praise of the Lord.
037,037 – O Sing, My Soul, Your Makers Praise
037,1
037,O sing my soul, your Maker’s praise
037,In grateful hymns ascending;
037,Whose steadfast love has crowned your days
037,With heav’nly gifts un ending.
037,I sought the Lord, He heard my cry;
037,His holy angels hover nigh
037,The tents of those who love Him.
037,2
037,The Lord is good to those who seek
037,His face in time of sorrow
037,Providing comfort to the weak
037,And grace for each tomorrow.
037,Though grief may tarry for a night
037,The morn shall break in joy and light
037,With blessings from His presence.
037,3
037,The Lord will turn His face in peace
037,When troubled souls draw near Him;
037,His loving kindness shall not cease
037,To those who trust and fear Him.
037,Our God will not forsake His own;
037,Eternal is His heav’nly throne;
037,His kingdom stands forever.
038,038 – Arise, My Soul, Arise!
038,1
038,Arise, my soul, arise!
038,Stretch forth to things eternal
038,And hasten to the feet of your Redeemer God.
038,Though hid from mortal eyes
038,He dwells in light supernal;
038,Yet worship Him in humbleness and call Him Lord.
038,His banquet of love
038,Awaits you above;
038,Yet here He grants a foretaste of the feast
038,to come!
038,Rejoice, my soul, rejoice
038,To heav’n lift up your voice:
038,Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia!
038,2
038,Now hear the harps of heav’n!
038,Oh, hear the song victorious
038,The never-ending anthem sounding
038,through the sky!
038,To mortals is not giv’n
038,To join in strains so glorious;
038,Yet here on earth we too can sing
038,our praises high!
038,He bought with His blood
038,The ransomed of God;
038,To Him be everlasting pow’r and victory.
038,And let the great amen
038,Resound through heav’n again.
038,Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia!
039,039 – Lord, in the Morning
039,1
039,Lord, in the morning Thou shalt hear
039,My voice ascending high;
039,To Thee will I direct my prayer
039,To Thee lift up mine eye-
039,2
039,Up to the hills where Christ is gone
039,To plead for all His saints
039,Presenting at His Father’s throne
039,Our songs and our complaints.
039,3
039,O may Thy Spirit guide my feet
039,In ways of righteousness;
039,Make every path of duty straight
039,And plain before my face.
039,4 The men that love and fear Thy name
039,Shall see their hopes fulfilled;
039,The mighty God will compass them
039,With favor as a shield.
040,040 – The Dawn of Gods Dear Sabbath
040,1
040,The dawn of God’s dear Sabbath
040,Breaks o’er the earth again
040,As some sweet summer morning
040,After a night of pain;
040,It comes as cooling showers
040,To some exhausted land
040,As shade of clustered palm trees
040,‘Mid weary wastes of sand.
040,2
040,Lord, we would bring for offering
040,Though marred with earthly soil
040,A week of earnest labor
040,Of steady, faithful toil
040,Fair fruits of self denial
040,Of strong, deep love to Thee
040,Fostered by Thine own Spirit
040,In true humility.
040,3
040,And we would bring our burden
040,Of sinful thought and deed
040,In Thy pure presence kneeling
040,From bondage to be freed
040,Our heart’s most bitter sorrow
040,For all Thy work undone-
040,So many talents wasted!
040,So few bright laurels won!
040,4
040,And with that sorrow mingling
040,A steadfast faith, and sure
040,And love so deep and fervent
040,For Thee to make it pure
040,In Thy dear presence finding
040,The pardon that we need
040,And then the peace so lasting-
040,Celestial peace indeed.
041,041 – O Splendor of Gods Glory Bright
041,1
041,O splendor of God’s glory bright
041,From light eternal bringing light;
041,O Light of life, light’s living spring
041,True day, all days illumining.
041,2
041,O Thou true Sun, on us Thy glance
041,Let fall in royal radiance;
041,The Spirit’s sanctifying beam
041,Upon our earthly senses stream.
041,3
041,O joyful be the passing day
041,With thoughts as clear as morning’s ray
041,With faith like noontide shining bright
041,Our souls unshadowed by the night.
041,4
041,Dawn’s glory gilds the earth and skies;
041,Let Him, our perfect morn, arise;
041,The Father’s help His children claim
041,And sing the Father’s glorious name. Amen.
042,042 – Now That the Daylight Fills the Sky
042,1
042,Now that the daylight fills the sky
042,We lift our hearts to God on high
042,That He, in all we do or say
042,Would keep us free from harm today;
042,2
042,Would guard our hearts and tongues from strife;
042,From anger’s din would shield our life;
042,From evil sights would turn our eyes
042,And close our ears to vanities;
042,3
042,So we, when this new day is gone
042,And night in turn is drawing on
042,With conscience by the world unstained
042,Shall praise His name for vict’ry gained.
042,4
042,“All praise to You, creator Lord!
042,All praise to You, eternal Word!
042,All praise to You, O Spirit wise!”
042,We sing as daylight fills the skies.
043,043 – When Morning Gilds the Skies
043,1
043,When morning gilds the skies
043,my heart awaking cries
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
043,Alike at work and prayer
043,to Jesus I repair:
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
043,2
043,Whene’er the sweet church bell
043,peals over hill and dell
043,May Jesus Christ praised!
043,O hark to what it sings
043,as joyously it rings
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
043,3
043,The night becomes as day
043,when from the heart we say:
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
043,The powers of darkness fear
043,when this sweet chant they hear:
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
043,4
043,Ye nations of mankind
043,in this your concord find
043,May Jesus Christ praised!
043,Let all the earth around
043,ring joyous with the sound
043,May Jesus Christ praised!
043,5
043,In heaven’s eternal bliss
043,the loveliest strain is this
043,May Jesus Christ praised!
043,Let earth, and sea and sky
043,from depth to height reply
043,May Jesus Christ praised!
043,6
043,Be this, while life is mine
043,my canticle divine:
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
043,Be this th’eternal song
043,through all the ages long
043,May Jesus Christ be praised!
044,044 – Morning Has Broken
044,1
044,Morning has broken like the first morning
044,Blackbird has spoken like the first bird.
044,Praise for the singing!Praise for the morning!
044,Praise for the springing fresh from the Word!
044,2
044,Sweet the rain’s new fall sunlit from heaven
044,Like the first dewfall on the first grass.
044,Praise for the sweetness of the wet garden
044,Sprung in completeness where His feet pass.
044,3
044,Mine is the sunlight! Mine is the morning
044,Born of the one light Eden saw play!
044,Praise with elation, Praise every morning
044,God’s recreation of the new day!
045,045 – Open Now Thy Gates of Beauty
045,1
045,Open now thy gates of beauty
045,Zion, let me enter there
045,Where my soul in joyful duty
045,Waits for God Who answers prayer.
045,Oh, how blessèd is this place
045,Filled with solace, light, and grace!
045,2
045,Gracious God, I come before Thee
045,Come Thou also unto me;
045,Where we find Thee and adore Thee
045,There a heav’n on earth must be.
045,To my heart, oh, enter Thou
045,Let it be Thy temple now!
045,3
045,Here Thy praise is gladly chanted
045,Here Thy seed is duly sown;
045,Let my soul, where it is planted
045,Bring forth precious sheaves alone
045,So that all I hear may be
045,Fruitful unto life in me.
045,4
045,Thou my faith increase and quicken
045,Let me keep Thy gift divine
045,Howsoe’er temptations thicken;
045,May Thy Word still o’er me shine
045,As my guiding star through life
045,As my comfort in my strife.
045,5
045,Speak, O God, and I will hear Thee
045,Let Thy will be done indeed;
045,May I undisturbed draw near Thee
045,While Thou dost Thy people feed.
045,Here of life the fountain flows;
045,Here is balm for all our woes.
046,046 – Abide With Me, Tis Eventide
046,1
046,Abide with me, ’tis eventide!
046,The day is past and gone;
046,The shadows of the evening fall;
046,The night is coming on!
046,Within my heart a welcome guest
046,Within my home abide;
046,Refrain
046,O Savior, stay this night with me;
046,Behold, ’tis eventide!
046,O Savior, stay this night with me;
046,Behold, ’tis eventide.
046,2
046,Abide with me, ’tis eventide!
046,Thy walk today with me
046,Has made my heart within me burn
046,As I communed with Thee.
046,Thy earnest words have filled my soul
046,And kept me near Thy side;
046,3
046,Abide with me, ’tis eventide!
046,And lone will be the night
046,If I cannot commune with Thee
046,Nor find in Thee my light.
046,The darkness of the world, I fear
046,Would in my home abide;
047,047 – God, Who Made the Earth and Heaven
047,1
047,God, who made the earth and heaven,
047,Darkness and light:
047,You the day for work have given
047,For rest the night.
047,May Your angel guards defend us
047,Slumber sweet Your mercy send us
047,Holy dreams and hopes attend us
047,All through the night.
047,2
047,And when morn again shall call us
047,to run life’s way
047,May we still, what-e’er befall us
047,Your will obey.
047,From the pow’r of evil hide us
047,In the narrow pathway guide us
047,Never be Your smile denied us
047,All through the day.
047,3
047,Guard us waking, guard us sleeping
047,And, when we die
047,May we in Your mighty keeping
047,All peaceful lie.
047,When the trumpet call shall wake us
047,Then, O Lord, do not forsake us
047,But to reign in glory take us
047,with You on high.
047,4
047,Holy Father, throned in heaven
047,All holy Son
047,Holy Spirit, freely given
047,Blest Three in One:
047,Grant us grace, we now implore You
047,Till we lay our crowns before You
047,And in worthier strains adore
047,You while ages run.
048,048 – Softly Now the Light of Day
048,1
048,Softly now the light of day
048,Fades upon out sight away:
048,Free from care, from labor free
048,Lord, we would commune with Thee.
048,2
048,Thou, whose allpervading eye
048,Nought escapes, without, within
048,Pardon each infirmity
048,Open fault, and secret sin.
048,3
048,Soon from us the light of day
048,Shall forever pass away;
048,Then, from sin and sorrow free
048,Take us, Lord, to dwell with Thee.
049,049 – Savior, Breathe an Evening Blessing
049,1
049,Savior, breathe an evening blessing
049,Ere repose our spirits seal;
049,Sin and want we come confessing;
049,Thou canst save, and Thou canst heal.
049,2
049,Though the night be dark and dreary
049,Darkness cannot hide from Thee;
049,Thou art He who, never weary
049,Watchest where Thy people be.
049,3
049,Though destruction walk around us.
049,Though the arrow past us fly
049,Angel guards from Thee Surround us
049,We are safe if Thou art nigh.
049,4
049,Should swift death this night o’re-take us
049,And our couch become our tomb
049,May the morn of glory wake us
049,Clad in light and deathless bloom.
050,050 – Abide With Me
050,1
050,Abide with me; fast falls the eventide;
050,The darkness deepens; Lord with me abide!
050,When other helpers fail and comforts flee
050,Help of the helpless, O abide with me.
050,2
050,Swift to its close ebbs out life’s little day;
050,Earth’s joys grow dim; its glories pass away;
050,Change and decay in all around I see;
050,O Thou who changest not, abide with me.
050,3
050,I need Thy presence every passing hour.
050,What but Thy grace can foil the tempter’s power?
050,Who, like Thyself, my guide and stay can be?
050,Through cloud and sunshine, Lord, abide with me.
050,4
050,I fear no foe, with Thee at hand to bless;
050,Ills have no weight, and tears no bitterness.
050,Where is death’s sting? Where, grave, thy victory?
050,I triumph still, if Thou abide with me!
051,051 – Day Is Dying in the West
051,1
051,Day is dying in the west;
051,Heaven is touching earth with rest;
051,Wait and worship while the night
051,Sets the evening lamps alight
051,Through all the sky.
051,Refrain
051,Holy, holy, holy, Lord God of Hosts!
051,Heaven and earth are full of Thee!
051,Heaven and earth are praising Thee
051,O Lord most high!
051,2
051,Lord of life, beneath the dome
051,Of the universe, Thy home
051,Gather us who seek Thy face
051,To the fold of Thy embrace
051,For Thou art nigh.
051,3
051,While the deepening shadows fall
051,Heart of love enfolding all
051,Through the glory and the grace
051,Of the stars that veil Thy face
051,Our hearts ascend.
051,4
051,When forever from our sight
051,Pass the stars, the day, the night
051,Lord of angels, on our eyes
051,Let eternal morning rise
051,And shadows end.
052,052 – Now the Day Is Over
052,1
052,Now the day is over
052,night is drawing nigh
052,Shadows of the evening
052,steal across the sky.
052,2
052,Father, give the weary
052,calm and sweet repose;
052,With Thy tenderest blessing
052,May our eyelids close.
052,3
052,Through the long night watches
052,may thine angels spread
052,Their white wings above me
052,watching round my bed.
053,053 – All Praise to Thee
053,1
053,All praise to thee, my God, this night
053,for all the blessings of the light!
053,Keep me, O keep me, King of kings
053,beneath thine own almighty wings.
053,2
053,Forgive me, Lord, for thy dear Son
053,the ill that I this day have done
053,that with the world, myself, and thee
053,I, ere I sleep, at peace may be.
053,3
053,O may my soul on thee repose
053,and with sweet sleep mine eyelids close
053,sleep that may me more vigorous make
053,to serve my God when I awake.
053,4
053,Praise God, from whom all blessings flow;
053,praise him, all creatures here below;
053,praise him above, ye heavenly host;
053,praise Father, Son, and Holy Ghost.
054,054 – O Gladsome Light
054,1
054,O gladsome light
054,Of God the Father’s face
054,The eternal splendour wearing;
054,Celestial, holy, blest
054,Our Saviour, Jesus Christ
054,Joyful in Thine appearing.
054,2
054,Now e’er day fadeth quite
054,We see the evening light
054,Our wonted hymn outpouring;
054,Father of might unknown
054,Thee His incarnate Son
054,And Holy Spirit adoring.
054,3
054,To Thee of right belongs
054,All praise of holy songs
054,O Son of God, life giver;
054,Thee, therefore, O most high
054,The world doth glorify
054,And shall exalt forever.
055,055 – Jesus, Tender Shepherd, Hear Me
055,1
055,Jesus, tender Shepherd, hear me
055,Bless Thy little lamb tonight;
055,Through the darkness be Thou near me;
055,Watch my sleep till morning light.
055,2
055,All this day Thy hand has led me
055,And I thank Thee for Thy care;
055,Thou hast clothed me, warmed and fed me;
055,Listen to my evening prayer.
056,056 – The Day Thou Gavest
056,1
056,The day Thou gavest, Lord, is ended;
056,the darkness falls at Thy behest;
056,to Thee our morning hymns ascended;
056,Thy praise shall hallow now our rest.
056,2
056,We thank Thee that Thy church, unsleeping
056,while earth rolls onward into light
056,through all the world her watch is keeping
056,and rests not now by day or night.
056,3
056,As o’er each continent and island
056,the dawn leads on another day
056,the voice of prayer is never silent
056,nor die the strains of praise away.
056,4
056,So be it, Lord; Thy throne shall never
056,like earth’s proud empires, pass away.
056,Thy kingdom stands, and grows forever
056,till all Thy creatures own Thy sway.
057,057 – Now All the Woods Are Sleeping
057,1
057,Now all the woods are sleeping
057,And night and stillness creeping
057,O’er city, man, and beast;
057,But thou, my heart, awake thee
057,To pray’r awhile be take thee
057,And praise thy Maker ere thou rest.
057,2
057,My Jesus, stay Thou by me
057,And let no foe come nigh me
057,Safe sheltered by Thy wing;
057,But would the foe alarm me
057,O let him never harm me
057,But still Thine angels round me sing!
057,3
057,My loved ones, rest securely
057,From every peril surely
057,Our God will guard your heads;
057,And happy slumbers send you
057,And bid His hosts attend you
057,And golden armed watch o’er your beds.
058,058 – Hark, the Vesper Hymn Is Stealing
058,1
058,Hark! the vesper hymn is stealing
058,O’er the waters soft and clear;
058,Jubilate, Jubilate, Jubilate
058,Amen.
058,2
058,Nearer yet, and nearer pealing
058,Soft it breaks upon the ear.
058,Jubilate, Jubilate, Jubilate
058,Amen.
059,059 – Great Our Joy as Now We Gather
059,1
059,Great our joy as now we gather
059,Where the Master makes us one:
059,Where we worship God the Father
059,Thro’ the Spirit of His Son.
059,All who search for His church
059,Find it where His will is done.
059,2
059,Precious is the tie that binds us
059,To our God when faith grows cold;
059,Precious all that now reminds us
059,He is still our safe stronghold.
059,Faithful love serves to prove
059,Here the Shepherd has His fold.
059,3
059,May we learn from Christ’s example
059,How to use this house of prayer:
059,He who loved and cleansed His temple
059,Wants us all to worship there.
059,God the Son shuts out none:
059,In His kingdom all may share.
059,4
059,Lord, inspire us with Your vision
059,Of a world which must be won!
059,Glorious is the church’s mission
059,Long endeavoured, scarce begun!
059,Faithful now – this is how
059,God’s eternal will is done.
060,060 – Blessed Jesus at Thy Word
060,1
060,Blessed Jesus, at Thy word
060,We have gathered all to hear Thee;
060,By Thy word our hearts were stirred
060,Now to seek and love and fear Thee.
060,By Thy teachings sweet and holy
060,Let us learn to love Thee solely.
060,2
060,All our knowledge, sense, and sight
060,Lie in deepest darkness shrouded;
060,Till Thy Spirit breaks our night
060,With His beams of truth unclouded.
060,He alone to God canst win us
060,He who works all good within us.
060,3
060,Glorious Lord, Thy self impart!
060,Light of light, from God proceeding.
060,Open Thou our ears and heart
060,Help us, by Thy Spirit’s pleading.
060,Hear the cry Thy people raises!
060,Hear, and bless our prayer and praises!
061,061 – God Is Here!
061,1
061,God is here as we his people
061,meet to offer praise and prayer
061,may we find in fuller measure
061,what it is in Christ we share.
061,Here, as in the world around us
061,all our varied skills and arts
061,wait the coming of his Spirit
061,into open minds and hearts.
061,2
061,Here are symbols to remind us
061,of our lifelong need of grace;
061,here are table, font and pulpit;
061,here the Word has central place.
061,Here in honesty of preaching
061,here in silence, as in speech
061,here in newness and renewal
061,God the Spirit comes to each.
061,3
061,Here our children find a welcome
061,in the Shepherd’s flock and fold.
061,Here, as bread and wine are taken
061,Christ sustains us, as of old.
061,Here the servants of the Servant
061,seek in worship to explore
061,what it means in daily living
061,to believe and to adore.
061,4
061,Lord of all, Church and Kingdom
061,in an age of change and doubt
061,keep us faithful to the Gospel
061,help us work your purpose out.
061,Here, in this day’s dedication
061,all we have to give, receive:
061,we, who cannot live without you
061,we adore you! We believe!
062,062 – How Lovely Is Thy Dwelling Place
062,1
062,How lovely is Thy dwelling place
062,O Lord of hosts to me!
062,The tabenacles of Thy grace
062,How pleasant, Lord, they be!
062,2
062,My thirsty soul longs ardently
062,Yea, faints Thy courts to see;
062,My very heart and flesh cry out
062,O living God, for Thee.
062,3
062,Behold the sparrow findeth out
062,A house where-in to rest;
062,The swallow also, for herself
062,Provided hath a nest.
062,4
062,Ev’n Thine own altars, where she safe
062,Her young ones forth may bring
062,O Thou, almighty Lord of hosts
062,Who art my God and King.
062,5
062,Blest are they in Thy house that dwell
062,They ever give Thee praise.
062,Blest is the man whose strength Thou art
062,In whose heart are Thy ways.
063,063 – O Come, Let Us Sing to the Lord
063,1
063,O come, let us sing to the Lord
063,Come let us every one
063,A joyful noise make to the Rock
063,Of our salvation.
063,2

063,With glad and thankful voice;
063,Let us sing psalms of praise to Him
063,And make a joyful noise.
063,3
063,For God, a great God and great King
063,Above all gods, He is;
063,The depths of earth are in His hand
063,The strength of hills is His.
063,4
063,To Him the ocean vast belongs
063,For He the sea did make;
063,The dry land also from His hands
063,Its form at first did take.
063,5
063,O come, bow down and worship Him
063,And kneeling, humbly pray
063,Come to our Maker and our God
063,And hear His voice today.

074,074 – Like a River Glorious
074,1
074,Like a river glorious
074,is God’s perfect peace
074,Over all victorious
074,in its bright increase;
074,Perfect, yet it floweth
074,fuller every day
074,Perfect, yet it groweth
074,deeper all the way.
074,Refrain
074,Stayed upon Jehovah
074,hearts are fully blessed
074,Finding, as He promised
074,perfect peace and rest.
074,2
074,Hidden in the hollow
074,of His blessed hand
074,Never foe can follow
074,never traitor stand;
074,Not a surge of worry
074,not a shade of care
074,Not a blast of hurry
074,touch the spirit there.
074,3
074,Every joy or trial
074,falleth from above
074,Traced upon our dial
074,by the Sun of Love;
074,We may trust Him fully
074,all for us to do.
074,They who trust Him wholly
074,find Him wholly true.

076,076 – O Love That Wilt Not Let Me Go
076,1
076,O Love that wilt not let me go
076,I rest my weary soul in thee;
076,I give thee back the life I owe
076,that in thine ocean depths
076,its flow may richer, fuller be.
076,2
076,O Light that followest all my way
076,I yield my flickering torch to thee;
076,my heart restores its borrowed ray
076,that in they sunshine’s blaze
076,its day may brighter, fairer be.
076,3
076,O Joy that seekest me through pain
076,I cannot close my heart to thee;
076,I trace the rainbow thru the rain
076,and feel the promise is not vain
076,that morn shall tearless be.
076,4
076,O Cross that liftest up my head
076,I dare not ask to fly from thee;
076,I lay in dust life’s glory dead
076,and from the ground there blossoms
076,red life that shall endless be.

077,3
077,The wildest sea is calm
077,The tempest brings no fear
077,The darkest night is full of light
077,Because Thy love is near.
077,4
077,O love of God most full
077,O love of God most free
077,It warms my heart, it fills my soul
077,With might it strengthens me.

079,1

079,Eternal, and yet ever new;
079,Uncomprehended and unbought
079,Beyond all knowledge and all thought.
079,2

079,Far deeper than man’s deepest hate;
079,Self-fed, self-kindled like the light
079,Changeless, eternal, infinite.
079,3
079,We read thee best in Him who cam
079,To bear for us the cross of shame;
079,Sent by the Father from on high
079,Our life to live, our death to die.
079,4

079,E’en in the darkness of the grave;
079,Still more in resurrection light
079,We read the fullness of thy might.
079,5

079,Through all the perils of our way!
079,Eternal love, in thee we rest

080,080 – O World of God
080,1
080,O world of God, so vast and strange
080,Profound and wonderful and fair
080,Beyond the utmost reach of thought
080,But not beyond a Father’s care!
080,We are not strangers on this earth
080,Whirling amid the suns of space;
080,We are God’s children, this our home
080,With those of every clime and race.
080,2
080,O world of man where life is lived
080,So strangely mingling joy and pain
080,So full of evil and of good
080,So needful that the god shall reign!
080,It is this world that God has loved
080,And goodness was its Maker’s plan
080,The promise of God’s triumph is
080,His coming in a Son of Man.
080,3
080,O world of time’s far-stretching years!
080,There was a day when time stood still
080,A central moment when there rose
080,A cross upon a cruel hill;
080,In pain and death love’s power was seen
080,The mystery of time revealed
080,The wisdom of the ways of God
080,The grace through which man’s hurt is healed.
081,081 – Though I Speak With Tongues
081,1
081,Though I speak with tongues of men and angels
081,Though I have the prophet’s gift
081,Though I hold the keys to hidden knowledge
081,Though my faith can mountains shift;
081,Without love I am no better
081,Without love it’s all for naught;
081,Lord, You spent Your life in loving others:
081,What this means I would be taught.
081,2
081,Love is patient, knows no envy
081,Never gloats when others sin;
081,Love is never glad to see injustice
081,Always wants the truth to win.
081,There’s no end to love’s endurance
081,There’s no test it cannot face;
081,Lord, You spent Your life in loving others:
081,I shall fail without Your grace.
081,3
081,Though there’ll be an end to hidden knowledge
081,Visions, raptures, prophecy:
081,Faith and hope and love shall last forever
081,Love the greatest of the three.
081,Without love I am no better
081,Without love it’s all for naught;
081,Lord, You gave Your life in saving others:
081,What this means I would be taught.

082,2

082,Made us of clay, and formed us men;

082,He brought us to His fold again.
082,3

082,High as the heavens our voices raise;
082,And earth, with her ten thousand tongues
082,Shall fill His courts with sounding praise.
082,4
082,Wide as the world is His command
082,Vast as Eternity His love;
082,Firm as a rock His truth shall stand
082,When rolling years shall cease to move.

087,087 – God Who Spoke in the Beginning
087,1
087,God who spoke in the beginning
087,Forming rock and shaping spar
087,Set all life and growth in motion
087,Earthly world and distant star;
087,He who calls the earth to order
087,Is the ground of what we are.
087,2
087,God who spoke thro’ men and nations
087,Thro’ events long past and gone
087,Showing still today His purpose
087,Speaks supremely through His Son;
087,He who calls the earth to order
087,Gives His word and it is done.
087,3
087,God whose speech becomes incarnate –
087,Christ is servant, Christ is Lord –
087,Calls us to a life of service
087,Heart and will to action stirred;
087,He who uses man’s obedience
087,Has the first and final word.

088,1

088,that made the mountains rise
088,that spread the flowing seas abroad

088,I sing the wisdom that ordained
088,the sun to rule the day;
088,the moon shines full at God’s command
088,and all the stars obey.
088,2

088,who filled the earth with food
088,who formed the creatures thru the Word
088,and then pronounced them good.
088,Lord, how thy wonders are displayed
088,where’er I turn my eye
088,if I survey the ground I tread
088,or gaze upon the sky!
088,3
088,There’s not a plant or flower below
088,but makes thy glories known
088,and clouds arise, and tempests blow
088,by order from thy thrown;
088,while all that borrows life from thee
088,is ever in thy care;
088,and everywhere that we can be
088,thou, God, art present there.

090,Shall make life’s pathway clear!

090,Your face, By whom Your will was done;

090,Till greed and hate shall cease

093,The river running by
093,The sunset and the morning
093,That brighten up the sky.
093,3

093,The pleasant summer sun

093,4

093,And lips that we might tell
093,How great is God Almighty
093,Who has made all things well.
094,094 – Nature With Open Volume Stands
094,1
094,Nature with open volume stands
094,To spread its Maker’s praise abroad;
094,And every labor of His hands
094,Shows something worthy of our God.
094,2
094,But in the grace that rescued us
094,His brightest form of glory shines;
094,‘Tis fairest drawn upon the cross
094,In precious blood and crimson lines.
094,3
094,Here His whole name appears complete.
094,Nor wit can guess, nor reason prove
094,Which of the letters best is writ
094,The pow’r, the wisdom, or the love.
094,4
094,We would forever speak His name
094,In sounds to mortal ears unknown
094,With angels join to praise the Lamb
094,And worship at His Father’s throne.
095,095 – Spring Has Now Unwrapped the Flowers
095,1
095,Spring has now unwrapped the flowers
095,Day is fast reviving
095,Life in all her growing powers
095,Towards the light is striving:
095,Gone the iron touch of cold
095,Winter time and frost time
095,Seedlings, working through the mould
095,Now make up for lost time.
095,2
095,Herb and plant that winter long
095,Slumbered at their leisurek
095,Now be stirring, green and strong
095,Find in growth their pleasure:
095,All the world with beauty fills
095,Gold the green enhacing;
095,Flowers make glee among the hills
095,Set the meadows dancing.
095,3
095,Through each wonder of fair days
095,God Himself expresses;
095,Beauty follows all His ways
095,As the world He blesses:
095,So, as He renews the earth
095,Artist without rival
095,In His grace of glad new birth
095,We must seek revival.
096,096 – The Spacious Firmament
096,1
096,The spacious firmament on high
096,With all the blue, ethereal sky
096,And spangled heavens, a shining frame
096,Their great Original proclaim.
096,Th’unwearied sun from day to day
096,Does his Creator’s power display
096,And publishes to every land
096,The work of an almighty hand
096,2
096,Soon as the evening shades prevail
096,The moon takes up the wondrous tale;
096,And nightly to the listening earth
096,Repeats the story of her birth;
096,While all the stars that round her burn
096,And all the planets in their turn
096,Confirm the tidings as they roll
096,And spread the truth from pole to pole
096,3
096,What though in solemn silence all
096,Move round the dark terrestrial ball?
096,What though no real voice nor sound
096,Amid their radiant orbs be found?
096,In reason’s ear they all rejoice
096,And utter forth a glorious voice
096,Forever singing as they shine
096,“The hand that made us is divine.”

108,108 – Amazing Grace
108,1

108,that saved a wretch like me!
108,I once was lost, but now am found;
108,was blind, but now I see.
108,2

108,and grace my fears relieved;
108,how precious did that grace appear
108,the hour I first believed.
108,3

108,his word my hope secures;

108,as long as life endures.

108,I have already come;

108,and grace will lead me home.
108,5

108,bright shining as the sun
108,we’ve no less days to sing God’s praise
108,than when we first begun.

118,5

121,121 – Go, Tell It On the Mountain

121,Over the hills and everywhere:

121,That Jesus Christ is born!

121,O’er silent flocks by night
121,Behold throughout the heavens
121,There shone a holy light.
121,2

121,When lo! Above the earth

121,3

151,151 – Jesus Walked This Lonesome Valley
151,1
151,Jesus walked this lonesome valley;
151,He had to walk it by Himself.
151,O nobody else could walk it for Him.
151,He had to walk it by Himself.
151,2
151,I must go and stand my trial.
151,I have to stand it by myself.
151,O nobody else could stand it for me.
151,I have to stand it by myself.
151,3
151,Jesus walked this lonesome valley;
151,He had to walk it by Himself.
151,O nobody else could walk it for Him.
151,He had to walk it by Himself.
152,152 – Tell Me the Story of Jesus
152,1
152,Tell me the story of Jesus
152,Write on my heart every word.
152,Tell me the story most precious
152,Sweetest that ever was heard.
152,Tell how the angels in chorus
152,Sang as they welcomed His birth.
152,“Glory to God in the highest!
152,Peace and good tidings to earth.”
152,Refrain
152,Tell me the story of Jesus
152,Write on my heart every word.
152,Tell me the story most precious
152,Sweetest that ever was heard.
152,2
152,Fasting alone in the desert
152,Tell of the days that are past.
152,How for our sins He was tempted
152,Yet was triumphant at last.
152,Tell of the years of His labor
152,Tell of the sorrow He bore.
152,He was despised and afflicted
152,Homeless, rejected and poor.
152,3
152,Tell of the cross where they nailed Him
152,Writhing in anguish and pain.
152,Tell of the grave where they laid Him
152,Tell how He liveth again.
152,Love in that story so tender
152,Clearer than ever I see.
152,Stay, let me weep while you whisper
152,Love paid the ransom for me.
153,153 – Prince of Peace, Control My Will
153,1
153,Prince of Peace, control my will
153,Bid this struggling heart be still;
153,Bid my fears and doubtings cease
153,Hush my spirit into peace.
153,2
153,Thou hast bought me with Thy blood
153,Opened wide the gate to God;
153,Peace, I ask, but peace must be
153,Lord, in being one with Thee.
153,3
153,May Thy will, not mine, be done
153,May Thy will and mine be one;
153,Chase these doubtings from my heart
153,Now Thy perfect peace impart.
154,154 – When I Survey the Wondrous Cross
154,1
154,When I survey the wondrous cross
154,on which the Prince of Glory died;
154,my richest gain I count but loss
154,and pour contempt on all my pride.
154,2
154,Forbid it, Lord, that I should boast
154,save in the death of Christ, my God;
154,all the vain things that charm me most
154,I sacrifice them to his blood.
154,3
154,See, from his head, his hands, his feet
154,sorrow and love flow mingled down.
154,Did e’er such love and sorrow meet
154,or thorns compose so rich a crown.
154,4
154,Were the whole realm of nature mine
154,that were an offering far too small;
154,love so amazing, so divine
154,demands my soul, my life, my all.
155,155 – When I Survey the Wondrous Cross
155,1
155,When I survey the wondrous cross
155,On which the Prince of glory died
155,My richest gain I count but loss
155,And pour contempt on all my pride.
155,2
155,See, from His head, His feet
155,Sorrow and love flow mingled down;
155,Did e’er such love and sorrow meet?
155,Or thorns compose so rich a crown?
155,3
155,Since I, who was undone and lost
155,Have pardon through His name and word;
155,Forbid it, then, that I should boast
155,Save in the cross of Christ my Lord.
155,4
155,Were the whole realm of nature mine
155,That were a tribute far too small;
155,Love so amazing, so divine
155,Demands my life, my soul, my all.
156,156 – O Sacred Head Now Wounded
156,1
156,O sacred Head, now wounded
156,with grief and shame weighed down
156,now scornfully surounded
156,with thorns, thine only crown:
156,how pale thou art with anguish
156,with sore abuse and scorn!
156,How does that visage languish
156,which once was bright as morn!
156,2
156,What thou, my Lord, has suffered
156,was all for sinners’ gain;
156,mine, mine was the transgression
156,but thine the deadly pain.
156,Lo, here I fall, my Savior!
156,‘Tis I deserve thy place;
156,look on me with thy favor
156,vouchsafe to me thy grace.
156,3
156,What language shall I borrow
156,to thank thee, dearest friend
156,for this thy dying sorrow
156,thy pity without end?
156,O make me thine forever;
156,and should I fainting be
156,Lord, let me never, never
156,outlive my love for thee.
157,157 – Go to Dark Gethsemane
157,1
157,Go to dark Gethsemane
157,Ye who feel the tempter’s power
157,Your Redeemer’s conflict see.
157,Watch with him one bitter hour;
157,Turn not from his griefs away;
157,Learn from Jesus Christ to pray.
157,2
157,See Him at the judgment hall
157,Beaten, bound, reviled, arraigned;
157,See Him meekly bearing all;
157,Love to man His soul sustained!
157,Shun not suffering, shame, or loss;
157,Learn from him to bear the cross.
157,3
157,Calvary’s mournful mountain climb;
157,There, adoring at his feet
157,Mark that miracle of time
157,God’s own sacrifice complete.
157,“It is finished!” hear him cry;
157,Learn from Jesus Christ to die.

159,159 – The Old Rugged Cross
159,1
159,On a hill far away
159,stood an old rugged cross
159,the emblem of suffering and shame;
159,and I love that old cross
159,where the dearest and best
159,for a world of lost sinners was slain.
159,Refrain
159,So I’ll cherish the old rugged cross
159,till my trophies at last I lay down;
159,I will cling to the old rugged cross
159,and exchange it some day for a crown.
159,2
159,O that old rugged cross
159,so despised by the world
159,has a wondrous attraction for me;
159,for the dear Lamb of God
159,left his glory above
159,to bear it to dark Calvary.
159,3
159,To that old rugged cross
159,I will ever be true
159,its shame and reproach gladly bear;
159,then he’ll call me some day
159,to my home far away
159,where his glory forever I’ll share.
160,160 – Ride On in Majesty
160,1
160,Ride on! ride on in majesty!
160,Hark, all the tribes hosanna cry;
160,O Savior meek, pursue Thy road
160,With palms and scattered garments strowed.
160,2
160,Ride on! ride on in majesty!
160,In lowly pomp ride on to die;
160,O Christ, Thy triumphs now begin
160,O’er captive death and conquered sin.
160,3
160,Ride on! ride on in majesty!
160,The winged squadrons of the sky
160,Look down with sad and wondering eyes
160,To see the approaching sacrifice.
160,4
160,Ride on! ride on in majesty!
160,In lowly pomp ride on to die;
160,Bow Thy meek head to mortal pain
160,Then take, O God, Thy power and reign.
161,161 – Throned Upon the Awful Tree
161,1
161,Throned upon the awful tree
161,Lamb of God, Your grief we see.
161,Darkness veils Your anguished face;
161,None its lines of woe can trace.
161,None can tell what pangs unknown
161,Hold You silent and alone.
161,2
161,Silent through those three dread hours
161,Wrestling with the evil powers
161,Left alone with human sin
161,Gloom around You and within
161,Till th’appointed time is nigh
161,Till the Lamb of God may die.
161,3
161,Hark, that cry that peals aloud
161,Upward through the whelming cloud!
161,You, the Father’s only Son
161,You, His own anointed one
161,You are asking- can it be?
161,“Why have You forsaken Me?”
161,4
161,Lord, should fear and anguish roll
161,Darkly o’er our sinful soul
161,You, who once were thus bereft
161,That Your own might ne’er be left
161,Teach us by that bitter cry
161,In the gloom to know You nigh.
162,162 – Wondrous Love
162,1
162,What wondrous love is this
162,O my soul, O my soul?
162,What wondrous love is this, O my soul?
162,What wondrous love is this
162,That caused the Lord of bliss
162,To bear the dreadful curse
162,for my soul, for my soul;
162,To bear the dreadful curse
162,for my soul, for my soul;
162,2
162,To God and to the Lamb
162,I will sing, I will sing;
162,To God and to the Lamb, I will sing;
162,To God and to the Lamb
162,Who is the great I am
162,While millions join the theme
162,I will sing, I will sing;
162,While millions join the theme
162,I will sing, I will sing;
162,3
162,And when from death I’m free
162,I’ll sing on, I’ll sing on;
162,And when from death I’m free, I’ll sing on;
162,And when from death I’m free
162,I’ll sing and joyful be
162,And through eternity
162,I’ll sing on, I’ll sing on!
162,And through eternity
162,I’ll sing on.
163,163 – At the Cross
163,1
163,Alas! and did my Savior bleed
163,and did my Sovereign die?
163,Would he devote that sacred head
163,for sinners such as I?
163,Refrain
163,At the cross, at the cross
163,where I first saw the light
163,and the burden of my heart rolled away;
163,it was there by faith I received my sight
163,and now I am happy all the day!
163,2
163,Was it for crimes that I have done
163,he groaned upon the tree?
163,Amazing pity! Grace unknown!
163,And love beyond degree!
163,3
163,But drops of grief can ne’er repay
163,the debt of love I owe:
163,Here, Lord, I give myself away;
163,’tis all that I can do!
164,164 – There Is a Green Hill Far Away
164,1
164,There is a green hill far away
164,Without a city wall
164,Where the dear Lord was crucified
164,Who died to save us all.
164,2
164,We may not know, we cannot tell
164,What pains He had to bear
164,But we believe it was for us
164,He hung and suffered there.
164,3
164,He died that we might be forgiven
164,He died to make us good
164,That we might go at last to heaven
164,Saved by His precious blood.
164,4
164,There was no other good enough
164,To pay the price of sin;
164,He only could unlock the gate
164,Of heaven, and let us in.
164,5
164,O dearly, dearly has He loved!
164,And we must love Him too
164,And trust in His redeeming blood
164,And try His works to do.

165,1

165,See the Man of sorrows now;
165,From the fight returned victorious
165,Every knee to Him shall bow.
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Crowns become the victor’s brow.

165,2

165,Rich the trophies Jesus brings;
165,On the seat of power enthrone Him
165,While the vault of heaven rings.
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Crown the Savior, King of Kings.
165,Crown the Savior, King of Kings.
165,3
165,Sinners in derision crowned Him
165,Mocking thus the Savior’s claim;
165,Saints and angels crowd around Him
165,Own His title, praise His name.
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Spread abroad the victor’s fame!

165,4
165,Hark! those bursts of acclamation!
165,Hark! those loud triumphant chords!
165,Jesus takes the highest station;
165,Oh, what joy the sight affords!
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,Crown Him! Crown Him! Crown Him!
165,King of kings and Lord of lords!
165,King of kings and Lord of lords!
166,166 – Christ the Lord Is Risen Today
166,1
166,Christ the Lord is risen today, Alleluia!
166,Sons of man and angels say, Alleluia!
166,Raise your joys and triumphs high, Alleluia!
166,Sing, ye heavens, and earth reply, Alleluia!
166,2
166,Lives again our glorious King, Alleluia!
166,Where, O death, is now thy sting? Alleluia!
166,Once he died our souls to save, Alleluia!
166,Where’s thy victory, boasting grave? Alleluia!
166,3
166,Love’s redeeming work is done, Alleluia!
166,Fought the fight, the battle won, Alleluia!
166,Death in vain forbids him rise, Alleluia!
166,Christ has opened paradise, Alleluia!
166,4
166,Soar we now where Christ has led, Alleluia!
166,Following our exalted Head, Alleluia!
166,Made like him, like him we rise, Alleluia!
166,Ours the cross, the grave, the skies, Alleluia!
167,167 – Alleluia! Sing to Jesus!
167,1
167,Alleluia! sing to Jesus!
167,His the scepter, His the throne.
167,Alleluia! His the triumph
167,His the victory alone.
167,Hark! the songs of peaceful
167,Zion thunder like a mighty flood.
167,Jesus out of every nation
167,has redeemed us by His blood.
167,2
167,Alleluia! not as orphans
167,are we left in sorrow now;
167,Alleluia! He is near us
167,faith believes, nor questions how;
167,Though the cloud from sight
167,received Him when the forty days were o’er
167,Shall our hearts forget His promise
167,“I am with you evermore”?
167,3
167,Alleluia! bread of angels
167,Thou on earth our food, our stay;
167,Alleluia! here the sinful flee
167,to Thee from day to day:
167,Intercessor, Friend of sinners
167,Earth’s Redeemer, plead for me
167,Where the songs of all the sinless
167,sweep across the crystal sea.
168,168 – And Have the Bright Immensities
168,1
168,And have the bright immensities
168,Received our risen Lord
168,Where light years frame the Pleiades
168,And point Orion’s sword?
168,Do flaming suns His footsteps trace
168,Thro’corridors sublime
168,The Lord of inter stellar space
168,And conqueror of time?
168,2
168,The heav’n that hides Him from our sight
168,Knows neither near nor far;
168,A little candle sheds its light
168,As surely as a star.
168,And where His loving people meet
168,To share the gift divine
168,There stands He with unhurrying feet;
168,There heav’nly splendors shine.
169,169 – Come, You Faithful
169,1
169,Come, you faithful, raise the strain
169,Of triumphant gladness;
169,God has brought His people
169,Now rejoice, Jerusalem
169,And with true affection
169,Welcome in unwearied strains
169,Jesus’resurrection.
169,2
169,‘Tis the spring of souls today;
169,Christ has burst His prison
169,From the frost and gloom of death
169,light and life have risen
169,All the winter of our sins
169,Long and dark, is flying
169,From His ligth, to whom we give
169,Thanks and praise undying.
169,3
169,“Alleluia!” now we cry
169,to our King immortal
169,Who, triumphant, burst the
169,bars of the tomb’s dark portal
169,“Alleluia!” with the Son
169,God the Father praising;
169,“Alleluia!” yet again to
169,the Spirit raising.
170,170 – Come, You Faithful
170,1
170,Come, you faithful, raise the strain
170,Of triumphant gladness;
170,God has brought His Israel
170,Into joy from sadness;
170,Loosed from Pharoah’s bitter yoke
170,Jacob’s sons and daughters;
170,Led them with unmoistened foot
170,Through the Red Sea waters.
170,2
170,‘Tis the spring of souls today;
170,Christ has burst His prison
170,And from three days’sleep in death
170,As a sun has risen;
170,All the winter of our sins
170,Long and dark, is flying
170,From His light, to whom is giv’n
170,Laud and praise undying.
170,3
170,Now the queen of seasons, bright
170,With the day of splendor
170,With the royal feast of feasts
170,Comes its joy to render;
170,Comes to gladden faithful hearts
170,Which with true affection
170,Welcome in unwearied strain
170,Jesus’resurrection.
170,4
170,For today among the twelve
170,Christ appeared, be stowing
170,His deep peace, which evermore
170,Passes human knowing.
170,Neither could the gates of death
170,Nor the tomb’s dark portal
170,Nor the watchers, nor the seal
170,Hold Him as a mortal.
170,5
170,“Alleluia!” now we cry
170,To our King immortal
170,Who, triumphant, burst the bars
170,Of the tomb’s dark portal;
170,“Alleluia” with the Son
170,God the Father praising;
170,“Alleluia!” yet again
170,To the Spirit raising.

171,1
171,Thine is the glory
171,Risen, conquering Son;
171,Endless is the victory
171,thou o’er death hast won.
171,Angels in bright raiment
171,rolled the stone away
171,Kept the folded grave-clothes
171,where Thy body lay.
171,Refrain
171,Thine is the glory
171,Risen, conquering Son;
171,Endless is the victory
171,Thou o’er death hast won.
171,2
171,Lo! Jesus meets us.
171,Risen from the tomb
171,Lovingly He greets us
171,Scatters fear and gloom;
171,Let His Church with gladness
171,hymns of triumph sing
171,For her Lord now liveth;
171,Death has lost its sting.
171,3
171,No more we doubt Thee
171,Glorious Prince of life!
171,Life is nought without Thee;
171,Aid us in our strife;
171,Make us more than conquerors
171,through Thy deathless love
171,Bring us safe through Jordan
171,to Thy home above.
172,172 – The Strife Is Oer
172,Alleluia, alleluia, alleluia!
172,1
172,The strife is o’er, the battle done;
172,Now is the victor’s triumph won!
172,Now be the song of praise begun. Alleluia!
172,2
172,The pow’rs of death have done their worst
172,But Christ their legions has dispersed.
172,Let shouts of holy joy outburst. Alleluia!
172,3
172,The three sad days have quickly sped
172,He rises glorious from the dead.
172,All glory to our risen head! Alleluia!
172,4
172,Lord, by the stripes which wounded You
172,From death’s sting free Your servants too
172,That we may live and sing to You. Alleluia!

173,3

173,4

173,And sing today with one accord

174,174 – Star of Our Hope
174,1
174,Star of our hope! He’ll soon appear
174,The last loud trumpet speaks Him near;
174,Hail Him, all saints, from pole to pole-
174,How welcome to the faithful soul!
174,2
174,From heaven angelic voices sound:
174,Behold the Lord of glory crowned
174,Arrayed in majesty divine
174,And in His highest glories shine.
174,3
174,The grave yields up its precious trust
174,Which long has slumbered in the dust
174,Resplendent forms ascending, fair
174,Now meet the Savior in the air.
174,4
174,Descending with His azure throne
174,He claims the kingdom for His own;
174,The saints rejoice, they shout, they sing
174,And hail Him their triumphant King.
175,175 – Now the Green Blade Rises
175,1
175,Now the green blade rises
175,from the buried grain
175,What that in dark earth
175,many days has lain;
175,Love lives again
175,that with the dead has been;
175,Love is come again
175,like wheat arising green.
175,2
175,In the grave they laid Him
175,love by hatred slain
175,Thinking that He would
175,never wake again
175,Laid in the earth like grain
175,that sleeps unseen;
175,Love is come again
175,like wheat arising green.
175,3
175,Forth He came in triumph
175,like the risen grain
175,He that for three days
175,in the grave had lain;
175,Raised from the dead
175,my living Lord is seen;
175,Love is come again
175,like wheat arising green.
175,4
175,When our hearts are wintry
175,grieving, or in pain
175,Your touch can call us
175,back to life again
175,Field of our hearts that dead
175,and bare have been;
175,Love is come again
175,like wheat arising green.

177,177 – Jesus, Your Blood and Righteousness
177,1
177,Jesus, your blood and righteousness
177,My beauty are, my glorious dress;
177,Mid flaming worlds, in these arrayed
177,With joy shall I lift up my head.
177,2
177,Bold shall I stand in that great day
177,Cleansed and redeemed, no debt to pay;
177,For by your cross absolved I am
177,From sin and guilt, from fear and shame.
177,3
177,Lord, I believe your precious blood
177,Which at the mercy seat of God
177,Pleads for the captives’ liberty
177,Was also shed in love for me.
177,4
177,When from the dust of death I rise
177,To claim my mansion in the skies
177,This then shall be my only plea:
177,Christ Jesus lived and died for me.
178,178 – The Unveiled Christ
178,1
178,Once our blessed Christ of beauty
178,Was veiled off from human views;
178,But through suffering, death, and sorrow
178,He has rent the veil in two.
178,Refrain
178,O behold the Man of Sorrows!
178,O behold Him in plain view!
178,Lo! He is the mighty Conqueror
178,Since her rent the veil in two;
178,Lo! He is the mighty Conqueror
178,Since her rent the veil in two.
178,2
178,Yes, He is with God, the Father
178,Interceding there for you;
178,For He is the Well beloved
178,Since He rent the veil in two.
178,3
178,Holy angels bow before Him
178,Men of earth give praises due;
178,For He is the mighty Conqueror
178,Since He rent the veil in two.
179,179 – The Wonders of Redeeming Love
179,1
179,The wonders of redeeming love
179,Our highest thoughts exceed;
179,The Son of God comes from above
179,For sinful man to bleed.
179,2
179,He gives Himself, His life, His all
179,A sinless sacrifice.
179,For man He drains the cup of gall
179,For man the victim dies.
179,3
179,And now before His Father’s face
179,His precious blood He pleads;
179,For those who seek the throne of grace
179,His love still intercedes.
179,4
179,He knows the frailties of our frame
179,For He has borne our grief;
179,Our great High Priest once felt the same
179,And He can send relief.
179,5
179,His love will not be satisfied
179,Till He in glory sees
179,The faithful ones for whom He died
179,From sin forever free.
