179,Labels: The Wonders of Redeeming Love
180,180 – O Listen to Our Wondrous Story
180,1
180,O listen to our wondrous story
180,Counted once among the lost;
180,Yet One came down from heaven’s glory
180,Saving us at awful cost!
180,Refrain
180,Who saved us from eternal loss?
180,Who but God’s Son upon the cross?
180,What did He do? He died for you!
180,Where is He now? Believe it thou
180,In heaven interceding!
180,In heaven interceding!
180,2
180,No angel could His place have taken
180,Highest of the high tho’ he;
180,The loved One on the cross forsaken
180,Was One of the Godhead three!
180,3
180,Will you surrender to this Savior?
180,To His scepter humbly bow?
180,You, too, shall come to know His favor
180,He will save you, save you now.
181,181 – Does Jesus Care
181,1
181,Does Jesus care when my heart is pained
181,Too deeply for mirth and song;
181,As the burdens press, and the cares distress
181,And the way grows weary and long?
181,Refrain
181,O yes, He cares- I know He cares!
181,His heart is touched with my grief;
181,When the days are weary
181,The long nights dreary
181,I know my Savior cares. (He cares.)
181,2
181,Does Jesus care when my way is dark
181,With a nameless dread and fear?
181,As the daylight fades into deep night shades
181,Does He care enough to be near?
181,3
181,Does Jesus care when I’ve said goodbye
181,To the dearest on earth to me
181,And my sad heart aches till it nearly breaks ­
181,Is it aught to Him? Does He see?
182,182 – Christ Is Alive
182,1
182,Christ is alive!
182,Let Christians sing.
182,His cross stands empty to the sky.
182,Let streets and homes with praises ring.
182,His love in death shall never die.
182,2
182,Christ is alive!
182,No longer bound
182,To distant years in Palestine
182,He comes to claim the here and now
182,And conquer every place and time.
182,3
182,In every insult
182,rift, and war
182,Where color, scorn or wealth divide
182,He suffers still, yet loves the more
182,And lives, though ever crucified.
182,4
182,Christ is alive!
182,Ascended Lord
182,He rules the world His Father made
182,Till, in the end, His love adored
182,Shall be to all on earth displayed.
183,183 – I Will Sing of Jesus Love
183,1
183,I Will sing of Jesus love
183,Sing of Him,who first loved me;
183,for He left bright worlds above
183,And died on Calvary.
183,Refrain
183,I will sing of Jesus love
183,Endless praise my heart shall give;
183,He has died that I might live
183,I will sing His love to me.
183,2
183,O the depths of love divine!
183,Earth or heaven can never know
183,How that sin as dark as mine
183,can be made as white as snow.
183,3
183,Nothing good for Him I’ve done;
183,How could He such love bestow?
183,Lord, I own my heart is won
183,help me now my love to show.
184,184 – Jesus Paid It All
184,1
184,I hear the Savior say
184,“Thy strength indeed is small;
184,Child of weakness, watch and pray
184,Find in Me thine all in all.”
184,Refrain
184,Jesus paid it all
184,All to Him I owe;
184,Sin had left a crimson stain
184,He washed it white as snow.
184,2
184,Lord, now indeed I find
184,Thy power and Thine alone
184,Can change the leper’s spots
184,And melt the heart of stone.
184,3
184,Since nothing good have I
184,Whereby Thy grace to claim
184,I’ll wash my garments white
184,In the blood of Calv’ry’s Lamb.
184,4
184,And when before the throne
184,I stand in Him complete
184,I’ll lay my trophies down
184,All down at Jesus’ feet.
185,185 – Jesus Is All the World to Me
185,1
185,Jesus is all the world to me
185,my life, my joy, my all;
185,he is my strength from day to day
185,without him I would fall.
185,When I am sad, to him I go
185,no other one can cheer me so;
185,when I am sad, he makes me glad
185,he’s my friend.
185,2
185,Jesus is all the world to me
185,my friend in trials sore;
185,I go to him for blessings, and
185,he gives them o’er and o’er.
185,He sends the sunshine and the rain
185,he sends the harvest’s golden grain;
185,sunshine and rain, harvest of grain
185,he’s my friend.
185,3
185,Jesus is all the world to me
185,and true to him I’ll be;
185,O how could I this friend deny
185,when he’s so true to me?
185,Following him I know I’m right
185,he watches o’er me day and night;
185,following him by day and night
185,he’s my friend.
185,4
185,Jesus is all the world to me
185,I want no better friend;
185,I trust him now, I’ll trust him when
185,life’s fleeting days shall end.
185,Beautiful life with such a friend
185,beautiful life that has no end;
185,eternal life, eternal joy
185,he’s my friend.
186,186 – Ive Found a Friend
186,1
186,I’ve found a Friend; oh, such a Friend!
186,He loved me ere I knew Him;
186,He drew me with the cords of love
186,And thus He bound me to Him.
186,And ’round my heart still closely twine
186,Those ties which nought can sever
186,For I am His, and He is mine
186,Forever and forever.
186,2
186,I’ve found a Friend; oh, such a Friend!
186,He bled, He died to save me;
186,And not alone the gift of life
186,But His own self He gave me.
186,Nought that I have my own I call
186,I hold it for the Giver;
186,My heart, my strength, my life my all
186,Are His, and His forever.
186,3
186,I’ve found a Friend; oh, such a Friend!
186,All power to Him is given;
186,To guard me on my upward course
186,And bring me safe to heaven.
186,The eternal glories gleam afar
186,To nerve my faint endeavor;
186,So now to watch, to work, to war
186,And then to rest forever.
186,4
186,I’ve found a Friend; oh, such a Friend!
186,So kind, and true, and tender
186,So wise a counselor and guide
186,So mighty a defender.
186,From Him, who loveth me so well
186,What power my soul can sever?
186,Shall life or death, or earth, or hell?
186,No; I am His forever.
187,187 – Jesus, What a Friend for Sinners
187,1
187,Jesus! what a Friend for sinners!
187,Jesus! Lover of my soul;
187,Friends may fail me, foes assail me
187,He, my Savior, makes me whole.
187,Refrain
187,Hallelujah! what a Savior!
187,Hallelujah! what a Friend!
187,Saving, helping, keeping, loving
187,He is with me to the end.
187,2
187,Jesus! what a Strength in weakness!
187,Let me hide myself in Him.
187,Tempted, tried, and sometimes failing
187,He, my Strength, my victory wins.
187,3
187,Jesus! what a Help in sorrow!
187,While the billows over me roll
187,Even when my heart is breaking
187,He, my Comfort, helps my soul.
187,4
187,Jesus! I do now receive Him
187,[or Jesus! I do now adore Him,]
187,More than all in Him I find.
187,He hath granted me forgiveness
187,I am His, and He is mine.
188,188 – My Song Is Love Unknown
188,1
188,My song is love unknown
188,My Savior’s love to me
188,Love to the loveless shown
188,That they might lovely be.
188,O who am I that for my sake
188,My Lord should take frail flesh and die?
188,2
188,He came from His blest throne
188,Salvation to bestow
188,But men made strange, and none
188,The longed for Christ would know.
188,But O my Friend, my Friend indeed
188,Who at my need His life did spend.
188,3
188,Sometimes they strew His way
188,And His sweet praises sing
188,Resounding all the day
188,Hosannas to their King.
188,Then “Crucify” is all their breath
188,And for His death they thirst and cry.
188,4
188,Why, what hath my Lord done?
188,What makes this rage and spite?
188,He made the lame to run
188,He gave the blind their sight.
188,Sweet injuries! yet they at these
188,Themselves displease, and ‘gainst Him rise.
188,5
188,They rise, and needs will have
188,My dear Lord made away;
188,A murderer they save
188,The Prince of life they slay.
188,Yet cheerful He to suff’ring goes
188,That He His foes from thence might free.
188,6
188,Here might I stay and sing
188,No story so divine:
188,Never was love, dear King
188,Never was grief like Thine!
188,This is my Friend, in whose sweet praise
188,I all my days could gladly spend.
189,189 – All That Thrills My Soul
189,1
189,Who can cheer the heart like Jesus
189,By His presence all divine?
189,True and tender, pure and precious
189,Oh, how blest to call Him mine!
189,Refrain
189,All that thrills my soul is Jesus;
189,He is more than life to me; (to me;)
189,And the fairest of ten thousand
189,In my blessed Lord I see.
189,2
189,Love of Christ so freely given
189,Grace of God beyond degree
189,Mercy higher than the heaven
189,Deeper than the deepest sea.
189,3
189,Every need His hand supplying
189,Every good in Him I see;
189,On His strength divine relying
189,He is All in All to me.
189,4
189,By the crystal flowing river
189,With the ransomed I will sing
189,And forever and forever
189,Praise and glorify the King.
190,190 – Jesus Loves Me
190,1
190,Jesus loves me! this I know
190,For the Bible tells me so;
190,Little ones to Him belong
190,They are weak but He is strong
190,Refrain
190,Yes, Jesus loves me!
190,Yes, Jesus loves me!
190,Yes, Jesus loves me!
190,The Bible tells me so.
190,2
190,Jesus loves me! He wo died
190,Heaven’s gate to open wide:
190,He will wash away my sin
190,Let His little child come in.
190,3
190,Jesus, take this heart of mine
190,Make it pure and wholly thine;
190,On the coross You died for me
190,I will love and live for Thee.
191,191 – Love Divine
191,1
191,Love divine, all loves excelling
191,joy of heaven, to earth come down;
191,fix in us thy humble dwelling;
191,all thy faithful mercies crown!
191,Jesus thou art all compassion
191,pure, unbounded love thou art;
191,visit us with thy salvation;
191,enter every trembling heart.
191,2
191,Breathe, O breathe thy loving Spirit
191,into every troubled breast!
191,Let us all in thee inherit;
191,let us find the promised rest.
191,Take away our bent to sinning;
191,Alpha and Omega be;
191,end of faith, as its beginning
191,set our hearts at liberty.
191,3
191,Come, Almighty to deliver
191,let us all thy grace receive;
191,suddenly return and never
191,nevermore thy temples leave.
191,Thee we would be always blessing
191,serve thee as thy hosts above
191,pray and praise thee without ceasing
191,glory in thy perfect love.
191,4
191,Finish, then, thy new creation;
191,pure and spotless let us be.
191,Let us see thy great salvation
191,perfectly restored in thee;
191,changed from glory into glory
191,till in heaven we take our place
191,till we cast our crowns before thee
191,lost in wonder, love, and praise.
192,192 – O Shepherd Divine
192,1
192,O Shepherd divine, I know Thou art mine;
192,Thy search in the night was for me.
192,This bleak world is cold, but warm is Thy fold;
192,My Shepherd, I follow Thee.
192,Thy beautiful lamp shineth bright o’er my way
192,Thy glorious light unto Thy perfect day.
192,Thro’ pastures serene
192,Thro’ valleys of green
192,My Shepherd, I follow Thee.
192,2
192,O Shepherd divine, I know Thou art mine;
192,Thy great heart was broken for me.
192,Thy grace and Thy law I picture in awe;
192,They kissed upon Calvary.
192,Ah! Life that was given to ransom my soul
192,Ah! Heart that was broken to make sinners whole
192,This world is but loss
192,In view of Thy cross
192,My Shepherd, I follow Thee.
192,3
192,O Shepherd divine, I know Thou art mine;
192,I hear Thee say, “Follow thou Me.”
192,Thy message today illumines my way;
192,The Spirit of Prophecy.
192,I thrill at Thy marvellous love to Thy sheep
192,The way Thou dost lead to the still waters deep
192,One staff and one rod
192,One fold and one God;
192,My Shepherd, I follow Thee.
193,193 – Savior, Teach Me
193,1
193,Saviour, teach me day by day
193,Love’s sweet lesson to obey
193,Sweeter lesson cannot be
193,Loving Him who first loved me.
193,2
193,With a child’s glad heart of love
193,At Thy bidding may I move
193,Prompt to serve and follow Thee
193,Loving Him who first loved me.
193,3
193,Teach me I am not my own
193,I am Thine, and Thine alone;
193,Thine to keep, to rule, to save
193,From all sin that would enslave.
193,4
193,Love in loving finds employ
193,In obedience all her joy;
193,Ever new that joy will be
193,Loving Him who first loved me.
193,5
193,Teach me thus Thy steps to trace
193,Strong to follow in Thy grace.
193,Learning how to love from Thee
193,Loving Him who first loved me.
194,194 – Sing We of the Modern City
194,1
194,Sing we of the modern city
194,Scene alike of joy and stress;
194,Sing we of its nameless people
194,In their urban wilderness.
194,Into endless rows of houses
194,Life is set a millionfold
194,Life expressed in human beings
194,Daily born and growing old.
194,2
194,In the city full of people
194,World of speed and hectic days
194,In the ever-changing setting
194,Of the latest trend and craze
194,Christ is present, and among us;
194,In the crowd we see Him stand.
194,In the bustle of the city
194,Jesus Christ is every man.
194,3
194,God is not remote in heaven
194,But on earth to share our shame
194,Changing graph and mass and number
194,Into persons with a name.
194,Christ has shown, beyond statistics
194,Human life with glory crowned
194,By His timeless presence proving
194,People matter, people count!
195,195 – Showers of Blessing
195,1
195,“There shall be showers of blessing;”
195,This is the promise of love;
195,There shall be seasons refreshing
195,Sent from the Savior above.
195,Refrain
195,Showers of blessing
195,Showers of blessing we need;
195,Mercy drops round us are falling
195,But for the showers we plead.
195,2
195,“There shall be showers of blessing;”
195,Precious reviving again;
195,Over the hills and the valleys
195,Sound of abundance of rain.
195,3
195,“There shall be showers of blessing;”
195,Send them upon us, O Lord;
195,Grant to us now a refreshing;
195,Come, and now honor Thy word.
195,4
195,“There shall be showers of blessing;”
195,O that today they might fall
195,Now as to God were confessing
195,Now as on Jesus we call!
196,196 – Tell Me the Old, Old Story
196,1
196,Tell me the old, old story
196,of unseen things above
196,Of Jesus and His glory
196,of Jesus and His love.
196,Tell me the story simply
196,as to a little child
196,For I am weak and weary
196,and helpless and defiled.
196,Refrain
196,Tell me the old, old story
196,tell me the old, old story
196,Tell me the old, old story
196,of Jesus and His love.
196,2
196,Tell me the story softly
196,with earnest tones and grave;
196,Remember I’m the sinner
196,whom Jesus came to save.
196,Tell me the story always
196,if you would really be
196,In any time of trouble
196,a comforter to me.
196,3
196,Tell me the same old story
196,when you have cause to fear
196,That this world’s empty glory
196,is costing me too dear.
196,Yes, and when that world’s glory
196,is dawning on my soul
196,Tell me the old, old story:
196,“Christ Jesus makes thee whole.”
197,197 – The King of Love My Shepherd Is
197,1
197,The King of love my Shepherd is
197,Whose goodness faileth never;
197,I nothing lack if I am His
197,And He is mine forever.
197,2
197,Where streams of living water flow
197,My ransomed soul He leadeth
197,And, where the verdant pastures grow
197,With food celestial feedeth.
197,3
197,Perverse and foolish, oft I strayed
197,But yet in love He sought me
197,And on His shoulder gently laid
197,And home, rejoicing, brought me.
197,4
197,And so through all the length of days
197,Thy goodness faileth never;
197,Good Shepherd! I would sing Thy praise
197,Within Thy house forever.
198,198 – And Can It Be
198,1
198,And can it be that I should gain
198,an interest in the Savior’s blood!
198,Died he for me? who caused his pain!
198,For me? who him to death pursued?
198,Amazing love! How can it be
198,that thou, my God, shouldst die for me?
198,Refrain
198,Amazing love! How can it be
198,that thou, my God, shouldst die for me?
198,2
198,He left his Father’s throne above
198,so free, so infinite his grace!;
198,emptied himself of all but love
198,and bled for Adam’s helpless race.
198,‘Tis mercy all, immense and free
198,for O my God, it found out me!
198,3
198,Long my imprisoned sprit lay
198,fast bound in sin and nature’s night;
198,thine eye diffused a quickening ray;
198,I woke, the dungeon flamed with light;
198,my chains fell off, my heart was free
198,I rose, went forth, and followed thee.
198,4
198,No condemnation now I dread;
198,Jesus, and all in him, is mine;
198,alive in him, my living Head
198,and clothed in righteousnes divine
198,bold I approach th’ eternal throne
198,and claim the crown, through Christ my own.
199,199 – The Head That Once Was Crowned
199,1
199,The head that once was crowned with thorns
199,Is crowned with glory now;
199,A royal diadem adorns
199,The mighty victor’s brow.
199,2
199,The highest place that heaven affords
199,Is His, is His by right;
199,The King of kings, and Lord of lords
199,And heaven’s eternal light.
199,3
199,The joy of all who dwell above
199,The joy of all below
199,To whom He manifests His love
199,And grants His name to know.
199,4
199,To them the cross, with all its shame
199,With all its grace is given;
199,Their name an everlasting name
199,Their joy the joy of heaven.
199,5
199,To them the cross, with all its shame
199,With all its grace is given;
199,Their name an everlasting name
199,Their joy the joy of heaven.

200,1
200,The Lord is coming, let this be
200,The herald note of jubilee;
200,And when we meet and when we part
200,The salutation from the heart.
200,Refrain
200,The Lord is coming, let this be
200,The herald note of jubilee
200,The herald note of jubilee.
200,2
200,The Lord is coming, sound it forth
200,From east to west, from south to north;
200,Speed on! Speed on the tidings glad
200,That none who love Him may be sad.
200,Refrain
200,The Lord is coming, let this be
200,The herald note of jubilee
200,The herald note of jubilee.
200,3
200,The Lord is coming, swift and sure
200,And all His judgements shall endure
200,And none can hope to escape His wrath
200,Who walk not in the narrow path.
200,Refrain
200,The Lord is coming, let this be
200,The herald note of jubilee
200,The herald note of jubilee.
200,4
200,This earth, with her ten thousand wrongs
200,Will soon be tuned to nobler songs;
200,Our praise shall then, in realms of light
200,With all His universe unite.
200,Refrain
200,The Lord is coming, let this be
200,The herald note of jubilee
200,The herald note of jubilee.
201,201 – Christ Is Coming
201,1
201,Christ is coming! let creation
201,Bid her groans and travail cease;
201,Let the glorious proclamation
201,Hope restore and faith increase;
201,Christ is coming! Christ is coming!
201,Come, Thou blessed Prince of Peace!
201,(Prince of Peace!)
201,Come, Thou blessed Prince of Peace!
201,2
201,Earth can now but tell the story
201,Of Thy bitter cross and pain;
201,She shall yet behold Thy glory
201,When Thou comest back to reign;
201,Christ is coming! Christ is coming!
201,Let each heart repeat the strain.
201,(repeat the strain)
201,Let each heart repeat the strain.
201,3
201,With that “blessed hope” before us
201,Let no harp remain unstrung;
201,Let the mighty advent chorus
201,Onward roll from tongue to tongue:
201,Christ is coming! Christ is coming!
201,Come, Lord Jesus, quickly come!
201,(quickly come!)
201,Come, Lord Jesus, quickly come!
202,202 – Hail Him the King of Glory
202,1
202,Tell it to every kindred and nation
202,Tell it far and near;
202,Earth’s darkest night will fade with the dawning
202,Jesus will soon appear.
202,Refrain
202,Hail Him the King of glory
202,Once the Lamb for sinners slain;
202,Tell, tell the wondrous story
202,“Jesus comes to reign.”
202,2
202,Nations again in strife and commotion
202,Warnings by the way;
202,Signs in the heavens, unerring omens
202,Herald the glorious day.
202,3
202,Children of God look up with rejoicing;
202,Shout and sing His praise;
202,Blessèd are they who, waiting and watching
202,Look for the dawning rays.

203,Refrain

203,Christ is risen!
203,Christ will come again!
203,2

203,When doubt and grief assails
203,Our Christian fortitude
203,And only grace avails.

203,Christ is risen!
203,Christ will come again!
203,3
203,This is the threefold truth
203,Which, if we hold it fast
203,Changes the world and us
203,And brings us home at last.
203,Refrain

203,Christ is risen!
203,Christ will come again!
204,204 – Come, Thou Long Expected Jesus
204,1
204,Come, thou long expected Jesus!
204,born to set thy people free;
204,from our fears and sins release us
204,let us find our rest in thee.
204,Israel’s strength and consolation
204,hope of all the earth thou art;
204,dear desire of every nation
204,joy of every longing heart.
204,2
204,Born thy people to deliver
204,born a child and yet a King
204,born to reign in us forever
204,now thy gracious kingdom bring.
204,By thine own eternal spirit
204,rule in all our hearts alone;
204,by thine all sufficient merit
204,raise us to thy glorious throne.
205,205 – Gleams of the Golden Morning
205,1
205,The golden morning is fast approaching;
205,Jesus soon will come
205,To take his faithful and happy children
205,to their promised home
205,Refrain
205,O, we see the gleams of the golden morning
205,piercing thro’ this night of gloom!
205,O, see the gleams of the golden morning
205,that will burst the tomb.
205,2
205,The gospel summons will soon be carried
205,to the nations round;
205,The Bridegroom then will cease to tarry
205,and the trumpet sound.
205,3
205,Attended by all the shining angels
205,Down the flaming sky
205,the Judge will come, and will take his people
205,where they will not die.
205,4
205,The lov’d of earth who have long been parted
205,Meet in that glad day;
205,The tears of those who are broken hearted
205,shall be wiped away.
206,206 – Face to Face
206,1
206,Face to face with Christ my Savior
206,Face to face, what will it be
206,When with rapture I behold Him
206,Jesus Christ, who died for me?
206,Refrain
206,Face to face shall I behold Him
206,Far beyond the starry sky;
206,Face to face in all His glory
206,I shall see Him by and by!
206,2
206,Only faintly now I see Him
206,With the darkening veil between
206,But a blessed day is coming
206,When His glory shall be seen.
206,3
206,What rejoicing in His presence
206,When are banished grief and pain;
206,When the crooked ways are straightened
206,And the dark things shall be plain!
206,4
206,Face to face! oh, blissful moment!
206,Face to face to see and know;
206,Face to face with my Redeemer
206,Jesus Christ, who loves me so.
207,207 – It May Be at Morn
207,1
207,It may be at morn, when the day is awaking
207,When sunlight through darkness and shadow is breaking
207,That Jesus will come in the fullness of glory
207,To receive from the world His own.
207,Refrain
207,O Lord Jesus, how long, how long
207,Ere we shout the glad song?
207,Christ returneth, Hallelujah!
207,Hallelujah! Amen, Hallelujah! Amen.
207,2
207,It may be at midday, it may be at twilight
207,It may be, perchance, that the blackness of midnight
207,Will burst into light in the blaze of His glory
207,When Jesus receives His own.
207,3
207,O joy! O delight! should we go without dying
207,No sickness, no sadness, no dread, and no crying
207,Caught up through the clouds with our Lord into glory
207,When Jesus receives His own.
208,208 – Therell Be No Dark Valley
208,1

209,209 – That Glorious Day Is Coming
209,1
209,That glorious day is coming
209,The hour is hastening on;
209,Its radiant light is nearing
209,Far brighter than the sun;
209,In yonder clouds of heaven
209,The Saviour will appear
209,And gather all His chosen
209,To meet Him in the air.
209,The saints, then all victorious
209,Will go to meet their Lord;
209,An earth both bright and glorious
209,Will then be their reward;
209,And God Himself there reigning
209,Will wipe all tears away;
209,Nor clouds nor night remaining
209,But one eternal day.
209,2
209,O Christian, keep from sleeping
209,And let your love abound;
209,Be watchful, prayerful, faithful
209,The trumpet soon will sound!
209,O sinner, hear the warning!
209,To Jesus quickly fly!
209,Then you, in that blest morning
209,May meet Him in the sky!
210,210 – Wake, Awake for the Night Is Flying
210,1
210,Wake, awake, for night is flying
210,The watchmen on the heights are crying
210,Awake, Jerusalem, arise!
210,Midnight’s solemn hour is tolling
210,His chariot wheels are nearer rolling
210,He comes; prepare, ye virgins wise.
210,Rise up with willing feet
210,Go forth, the Bridegroom meet; Alleluia!
210,Bear through the night your well-trimmed light
210,Speed forth to join the marriage rite.
210,2
210,Zion hears the watchmen singing
210,Her heart with deep delight is springing
210,She wakes, she rises from her gloom;
210,Forth her Bridegroom comes, all-glorious
210,In grace arrayed, by truth victorious;
210,Her Star is risen, her Light is come!
210,All hail, incarnate Lord
210,Our crown, and our reward! Alleluia!
210,We haste along, in pomp and song
210,And gladsome join the marriage throng.
210,3
210,Lamb of God, the heavens adore Thee
210,And men and angels sing before Thee
210,With harp and cymbal’s clearest tone.
210,By the pearly gates in wonder
210,We stand, and swell the voice of thunder
210,That echoes round Thy dazzling throne.
210,No vision ever brought
210,No ear hath ever caught
210,Such bliss and joy;
210,We raise the song, we swell the throng
210,To praise Thee ages all along.

211,1

211,Swell the triumph of His train:

211,Jesus comes, and comes to reign.
211,2

211,Robed in dreadful majesty!
211,Those who set at nought and sold Him
211,Pierced, and nailed Him to the tree
211,Deeply wailing, Deeply wailing
211,Shall the true Mesiah see!
211,3

211,Heaven and earth shall flee away;
211,All who hate Him, must, confounded
211,Hear the summons of that day-
211,“Come to judgment! Come to judgment!
211,Come to judgment! Come away!”
211,4
211,Yea, amen! let all adore Thee
211,High on Thy eternal throne!
211,Savior, take the power and glory
211,Make Thy righteous sentence known;
211,O come quickly, O come quickly
211,Claim the kingdom for Thine own!

223,1
223,Crown him with many crowns
223,the Lamb upon his throne
223,Hark! how the heavenly anthem drowns
223,all music but its own.
223,Awake, my soul, and sing
223,of him who died for thee
223,and hail him as thy matchless King
223,through all eternity.
223,2
223,Crown him the Lord of love!
223,behold his hands and side
223,those wounds, yet visible above
223,in beauty glorified;
223,No angel in the sky
223,Can fully bear that sight
223,But downward bend his wondering eye
223,At mysteries so great.
223,3
223,Crown him the Lord of peace!
223,whose power a scepter sways
223,from pole to pole, that wars may cease
223,and all be prayer and praise.
223,His reign shall know no end
223,and round his pierced feet
223,fair flowers of paradise extend
223,their fragrance ever sweet.
223,4
223,Crown him the Lord of years;
223,The potentate of time
223,Creator of the rolling spheres
223,Ineffably sublime!
223,All hail, Redeemer, hail!
223,For thou hast died for me;
223,thy praise shall never, never fail
223,throughout eternity.
224,224 – Seek Ye First the Kingdom
224,1
224,Seek ye first the kingdom
224,‘Tis your Father’s will.
224,So the voice of Jesus
224,bids us follow still.
224,Savior, we would hear Thee
224,Follow, find, and see;
224,And in life’s adventure
224,Thy disciples be.
224,2
224,As for hidden treasure
224,Or for matchless pearl
224,When at last discovered
224,some will sell their all;
224,So, when breaks the vision
224,of that kingdom fair
224,Ours shall be its riches
224,And its beauty rare.
224,3
224,As the silent leaven
224,works its secret way
224,Or as grows the seed grain
224,through the night and day;
224,Lord, so be the increase
224,peaceable but sure
224,Of Thy word within us
224,And Thy kingdom’s power.
224,4
224,As the tender seedling
224,grows up tall and strong
224,And the birds of heaven
224,to its branches throng;
224,So shall all God’s children
224,from the east and west
224,Gather to His kingdom
224,In its shadow rest.
224,5
224,Humblest shall be greatest
224,poor in spirit reign;
224,Home shall come the childlike
224,born through Thee again;
224,Eager hearts arrive there
224,on the pilgrim’s road
224,Hail! The kingdom glorious
224,of the living God!
225,225 – God Is Working His Purpose Out
225,1
225,God is working His purpose out
225,As year succeeds to year;
225,God is working His purpose out
225,And the time is drawing near;
225,Nearer and nearer draws the time
225,The time that shall surely be
225,When the earth shall be filled
225,with the glory of God
225,As the waters cover the sea.
225,2
225,From utmost east to utmost west
225,Where’er man’s foot hath trod
225,By the mouth of many messengers
225,Goes forth the voice of God;
225,Give ear to me, ye continents
225,Ye isles, give ear to me
225,That the earth shall be filled
225,with the glory of God
225,As the waters cover the sea.
225,3
225,March we forth in the strength of God
225,With the banner of Christ unfurled
225,That the light of the glorious gospel of truth
225,May shine throughout the world:
225,Fight we the fight with sorrow and sin
225,To set their captives free
225,That the earth shall be filled
225,with the glory of God
225,As the waters cover the sea.
225,4
225,All we can do is nothing worth
225,Unless God blesses the deed;
225,Vainly we hope for the harvest tide
225,Till God gives life to the seed;
225,Yet nearer and nearer draws the time
225,The time that shall surely be
225,When the earth shall be filled
225,with the glory of God
225,As the waters cover the sea.

227,227 – Jesus Shall Reign
227,1
227,Jesus shall reign where’er the sun
227,Does his successive journeys run;
227,His kingdom stretch from shore to shore
227,Till moons shall wax and wane no more.
227,2
227,People and realms of ev’ry tongue
227,Dwell on His love with sweetest song
227,And infant voices shall proclaim
227,Their early blessings on His name.
227,3
227,Blessings abound wherever He reigns;
227,The prisoner leaps to lose his chains;
227,The weary find eternal rest
227,And all who suffer want are blessed.
227,4
227,Let every creature rise and bring
227,Honors peculiar to our King;
227,Angels descend with songs again
227,And earth repeat the loud amen!

231,231 – Blest Be the King
231,1
231,Blest be the King whose coming
231,Is in the name of God!
231,For Him let doors be opened
231,No hearts against Him barred!
231,Not robed in royal splendor
231,In power and pomp comes He;
231,But clad as are the poorest
231,Such His humility.
231,2
231,Blest be the King whose coming
231,Is in the name of God!
231,By those who truly listen
231,His voice is truly heard;
231,Pity the proud and haughty
231,Who have not learned to heed
231,The Christ who is the promise
231,Who has atonement made.
231,3
231,Blest be the King whose coming
231,Is in the name of God!
231,He only to the humble
231,Reveals the face of God.
231,All power is His, all glory!
231,All things are in His hand
231,All ages and all peoples
231,‘Till time itself shall end.
231,4
231,Blest be the King whose coming
231,Is in the name of God!
231,He offers to the burdened
231,The rest and grace they need.
231,Gentle is He and humble!
231,And light his Yoke shall be
231,For He would have us bear it
231,So He can made us free!

232,sprang at once to sight
232,All the angel faces
232,All the hosts of light
232,Thrones and dominations
232,stars upon their way

232,To receive a name

232,He is God the Savior

232,There let Him subdue

232,in its light and power.

232,shall return again

233,233 – Christ, Whose Glory Fills the Skies
233,1
233,Christ, whose glory fills the skies
233,Christ, the true, the only light
233,Sun of Righteousness, arise
233,triumph o’er the shades of night;
233,Dayspring from on high, be near;
233,Daystar, in my heart appear.
233,2
233,Dark and cheerless is the morn
233,unaccompanied by thee;
233,joyless is the day’s return
233,till thy mercy’s beams I see;
233,till they inward light impart
233,cheer my eyes and warm my heart.
233,3
233,Visit then this soul of mine;
233,pierce the gloom of sin and grief;
233,fill me, Radiancy divine
233,scatter all my unbelief;
233,more and more thyself display
233,shining to the perfect day.

234,He became our brother
234,if we have seen Him
234,we have seen the Father:
234,Glory to God on high!
234,2
234,Christ is the world’s peace
234,Christ and none other;
234,no one can serve Him
234,and despise another.
234,Who else unites us
234,one in God the Father?
234,Glory to God on high!
234,3
234,Christ is the world’s life
234,Christ and none other;
234,sold once for silver
234,murdered here, our brother
234,He, who redeems us
234,reigns with God the Father:
234,Glory to God on high!
234,4
234,Give God the glory
234,God and none other;
234,give God the glory
234,Spirit, Son and Father;
234,give God the glory
234,God-with-us our brother:
234,Glory to God on high!
235,235 – Christ Is Made the Sure Foundation
235,1
235,Christ is made the sure foundation
235,Christ the head and cornerstone
235,chosen of the Lord, and precious
235,binding all the Church in one;
235,holy Zion’s help for ever
235,and her confidence alone.
235,2
235,All that dedicated city
235,dearly loved of God on high
235,in exultant jubilation
235,pours perpetual melody;
235,God the One in Three adoring
235,in glad hymns eternally.
235,3
235,To this temple, where we call thee
235,come, O Lord of Hosts, today;
235,with thy wonted loving-kindness
235,hear thy servants as they pray
235,and thy fullest benediction
235,shed within its walls alway.
235,4

235,what they ask of thee of gain;
235,what they gain from thee, for ever
235,with the blessed to retain
235,and hereafter in thy glory
235,evermore with thee to reign.
235,5
235,Laud and honor to the Father
235,laud and honor to the Son
235,laud and honor to the Spirit
235,ever Three, and ever One
235,con-substantial, co-eternal

236,236 – I Love Thee
236,1
236,I love Thee, I love Thee
236,I love Thee, my Lord;
236,I love Thee, my Savior
236,I love Thee, my God.
236,I love Thee, I love Thee
236,and that Thou dost know;
236,But how much I love Thee
236,my actions will show.
236,2
236,I’m happy, I’m happy
236,O, wondrous account!
236,My joys are immortal
236,I stand on the mount!
236,I gaze on my treasure
236,and long to be there
236,With Jesus and angels
236,and kindred so dear.
236,3
236,O Jesus, my Savior
236,with Thee I am blest
236,My life and salvation
236,my joy and my rest:
236,Thy name be my theme
236,and Thy love be my song;
236,Thy grace shall inspire
236,both my heart and my tongue.
236,4
236,O, who’s like my Savior?
236,He’s Salem’s bright King;
236,He smiles, and He loves me
236,and helps me to sing.
236,I’ll praise Him, I’ll praise Him
236,with notes loud and clear
236,While rivers of pleasure
236,my spirit do cheer.
237,237 – In the Cross of Christ I Glory
237,1
237,In the cross of Christ I glory
237,towering o’er the wrecks of time;
237,all the light of sacred story
237,gathers round its head sublime.
237,2
237,When the woes of life o’ertake me
237,hopes deceive, and fears annoy
237,never shall the cross forsake me.
237,Lo! it glows with peace and joy.
237,3
237,When the sun of bliss is beaming
237,light and love upon my way
237,from the cross the radiance streaming
237,adds more luster to the day.
237,4
237,Bane and blessing, pain and pleasure
237,by the cross are sanctified;
237,peace is there that knows no measure
237,joys that through all time abide.
238,238 – How Sweet the Name!
238,1
238,How sweet the name of Jesus sounds
238,In a believer’s ear!
238,It soothes his sorrows, heals his wounds
238,And drives away his fear.
238,2
238,It makes the wounded spirit whole
238,And calms the troubled breast;
238,“Tis manna to the hungry soul
238,And to the weary, rest.
238,3
238,Dear name, the rock on which I build
238,My shield and hiding place
238,My neverfailing treasury, filled
238,With boundless stores of grace.
238,4
238,Jesus! my Shepherd, Guardian, Friend
238,My Prophet, Priest, and King!
238,My Lord, my life, my way, my end!
238,Accept the praise I bring.
238,5
238,Weak is the effort of my heart
238,And cold my warmest thought;
238,But when I see Thee as Thou art
238,I’ll praise Thee as I ought.

239,Nought I ask beside Thee.
239,2

239,foes who would molest me
239,Cannot reach me here.
239,Though the earth be shaking
239,Every heart be quaking
239,Jesus calms our fear.
239,Sin and hell in conflict fell
239,With their bitter storms assail me
239,Jesus will not fail me.
239,3

239,For the Lord of gladness
239,Jesus, enters in.
239,Those who love the Father
239,Though the storms may gather
239,still have peace within;
239,Yea, whatever we here must bear
239,Still in Thee lies purest pleasure
239,Jesus, priceless Treasure!

241,The Savior of mankind.

255,255 – I Cannot Tell Why
255,1
255,I cannot tell why
255,He whom angels worship
255,Should set His love
255,upon the souls of men
255,Or why as Shepherd
255,He should seek the wanderers
255,To bring them back
255,they know not how nor when.
255,But this I know
255,that He was born of Mary
255,When Bethlehem’s manger
255,was His only home
255,And that He lived
255,at Nazareth and labored;
255,And so the Savior
255,Savior of the world, has come.
255,2
255,I cannot tell how
255,silently He suffered
255,As with His peace
255,He graced this place of tears
255,Nor how His heart
255,upon the cross was broken
255,The crown of pain
255,to three and thirty years.
255,But this I know
255,He heals the broken hearted
255,And stays our sin
255,and calms our lurking fear
255,And lifts the burden
255,from the heavy laden;
255,For still the Savior
255,Savior of the world, is here.
255,3
255,I cannot tell how
255,He will win the nations
255,How He will claim
255,His earthly heritage
255,How satisfy the
255,needs and aspirations
255,Of east and west
255,of sinner and of sage.
255,But this I know
255,all flesh shall see His glory
255,And He shall reap
255,the harvest He has sown
255,And some glad day His
255,sun will shine in splendor
255,When He the Savior
255,Savior, of the world, is known.
255,4
255,I cannot tell how
255,all lands shall worship
255,When at His biding
255,every storm is stilled
255,Or who can say how
255,great the jubilation
255,When all our hearts
255,with love for Him are filled.
255,But this I know the skies
255,shall sound His praises
255,Ten thousand thousand
255,human voices sing
255,And earth to heaven
255,and heaven to earth will answer
255,At last the Savior
255,Savior of the world, is King!

261,Amid the gloom of ancient night
261,They hailed the dawning Word
261,And in the coming of the light
261,Proclaimed the coming Lord.
261,2
261,The prophets passed; at length there came
261,To sojourn and abide
261,The Word incarnate, to whose name
261,The prophets testified;
261,And He, the twilight overpast
261,Himself, the Light of light
261,As man with man, revealed at last
261,The Father to our sight.
261,3
261,Eternal Spirit, who dost speak
261,To mind and conscience still
261,That we in this our day, may seek
261,To do our Father’s will
261,To us the word of life impart
261,Of Christ, the living way;
261,Give us the quiet, humble heart
261,To hear and to obey.

264,Which bade their souls to heaven aspire
264,Calm in distress, in danger bold!
264,2

264,In Abram’s breast, and sealed Him Thine?
264,Which made Paul’s heart with sorrow melt
264,And glow with energy divine?
264,3
264,That spirit which from age to age
264,Proclaimed Thy love, and taught Thy ways?
264,Brightened Isaiah’s vivid page
264,And breathed in David’s hallowed lays?
264,4

264,As when Elijah felt its power?
264,When glory beamed from Moses’ brow
264,Or Job endured the trying hour?
264,5

264,Renew Thy work, Thy grace restore;
264,And while to Thee our hearts we raise
264,On us Thy Holy Spirit pour.

346,May those who teach grow
346,in knowledge and patience
346,Guiding to wisdom
346,the young and the old
346,Training for worship
346,and witness and service
346,Foes to all falsehood
346,in truthfulness bold.
346,5
346,Lord, ever give to us
346,gifts in due measure
346,Each needing other
346,and all having worth;
346,So to the Father
346,the Son, and the Spirit
346,Glory be shown by
346,the church here on earth.
347,347 – Built on the Rock
347,1
347,Built on the Rock the Church shall stand
347,Even when steeples are falling;
347,Crumbled have spires in every land
347,Bells still are chiming and calling
347,Calling the young and old to rest
347,Calling the souls of those distressed
347,Longing for life everlasting.
347,2
347,Not in our temples made with hands
347,God, the Almighty, is dwelling;
347,High in the heav’ns His temple stands
347,All earthly temples excelling.
347,Yet He who dwells in heav’n above
347,Deigns to abide with us in love
347,Making our bodies His temple.
347,3
347,We are God’s house of living stones
347,Built for His own habitation;
347,He fills our hearts, His humble thrones
347,Granting us life and salvation.
347,Were two or three to seek His face
347,He in their midst would show His grace
347,Blessings upon them bestowing.
347,4
347,Yet in this house, an earthly frame
347,Jesus His children is blessing;
347,Hither we come to praise His name
347,Faith in our Savior confessing.
347,Jesus to us His Spirit sent
347,Making with us His covenant
347,Granting His children the kingdom.
347,5
347,Thro‘ all the passing years, O Lord
347,Grant that, when church bells are ringing
347,Many may come to hear God’s Word
347,Where He this promise is bringing:
347,I know My own, My own know Me:
347,You, not the world, My face shall see;
347,My peace I leave with you. Amen.
348,348 – The Church Has One Foundation
348,1
348,The church’s one foundation
348,is Jesus Christ her Lord;
348,she is his new creation
348,by water and the Word.
348,From heaven he came and sought her
348,to be his holy bride;
348,with his own blood he bought her
348,and for her life he died.
348,2
348,Elect from every nation
348,yet one o’er all the earth;
348,her charter of salvation
348,one Lord, one faith, one birth;
348,one holy name she blesses
348,partakes one holy food
348,and to one hope she presses
348,with every grace endued.
348,3
348,Though with a scornful wonder
348,we see her sore oppressed
348,by schisms rent asunder
348,by heresies distressed
348,yet saints their watch are keeping;
348,their cry goes up, “How long?”
348,And soon the night of weeping
348,shall be the morn of song.
348,4
348,‘Mid toil and tribulation
348,and tumult of her war
348,she waits the consummation
348,of peace forevermore;
348,till, with the vision glorious
348,her longing eyes are blest
348,and the great church victorious
348,shall be the church at rest.
349,349 – God is Love
349,1
349,Here in Christ we gather,
349,love of Christ our calling.
349,Christ, our love, is with us,
349,gladness be His greeting.
349,Let us fear Him, yes, and
349,love Him, God eternal.
349,Loving Him, let each love
349,Christ in all his brethren.
349,Refrain
349,God is love, and where true love is
349,God Himself is there.
349,2
349,When we Christians gather,
349,members of one body
349,Let there be in us no
349,discord but one spirit.
349,Banished now be anger,
349,strife, and every quarrel.
349,Christ, our God,
349,be always present here among us.
349,3
349,Grant us love’s fulfillment,
349,joy with all the blessed
349,When we see Your face,
349,O Savior, in its glory.
349,Shine on us,
349,O purest Light of all creation
349,Be our bliss while endless
349,ages sing Your praises.
350,350 – Blest Be the Tie That Binds
350,1
350,Blest be the tie that binds
350,our hearts in Christian love;
350,the fellowship of kindred minds
350,is like to that above.
350,2
350,Before our Father’s throne
350,we pour our ardent prayers;
350,our fears, our hopes, our aims are one
350,our comforts and our cares.
350,3
350,We share each other’s woes
350,our mutual burdens bear;
350,and often for each other flows
350,the sympathizing tear.
350,4
350,When we asunder part
350,it gives us inward pain;
350,but we shall still be joined in heart
350,and hope to meet again.

352,352 – This Is My Will
352,1
352,This is My will, My one command
352,That love should dwell among you all.
352,This is My will that you should love
352,As I have shown that I love you.
352,2
352,No greater love a man can have
352,Than that he die to save his friends.
352,You are My friends if you obey
352,What I command that you should do.
352,3
352,You chose not Me, but I chose you
352,That you should go and bear much fruit.
352,I chose you out that you in Me
352,Should bear much fruit that will abide.
352,4
352,All that I ask My Father, dear
352,For My name’s sake you shall receive.
352,This is My will, My one command
352,That love should dwell in each, in all.

375,Work for the night is coming
375,Under the sunset skies;
375,While their bright tints are glowing
375,Work for daylight flies.
375,Work till the last beam fadeth
375,Fadeth to shine no more;
375,Work while the night is dark’ning
375,When man’s work is o’er.
376,376 – All Things Are Thine
376,1
376,All things are Thine; no gift have we
376,Lord of all gifts, to offer Thee;
376,And hence with grateful hearts today
376,Thine own before Thy feet we lay.
376,2
376,Thy will was in the builder’s thought;
376,Thy hand unseen amidst us wrought;
376,Thro’ mortal motive, scheme and plan
376,Thy wise, eternal purpose ran.
376,3
376,No lack Thy perfect fullness knew;
376,For human needs and longings grew
376,This house of prayer- this home of rest.
376,Here may Thy saints be often blessed.
376,4
376,In weakness and in want we call
376,On Thee, for whom the heav’ns are small;
376,Thy glory is Thy children’s good
376,Thy joy Thy tender Fatherhood.
376,5
376,O Father! deign these walls to bless;
376,Make this the abode of righteousness
376,And let these doors a gateway be
376,To lead us from ourselves to Thee!

378,And ye shall prove My gospel true
378,By all the works that I have done
378,By all the wonders ye shall do.
378,3

378,I’m with you till the world shall end;
378,All power is vested in My hands;
378,I can destroy, and I defend.”
378,4

378,On a bright cloud to heaven He rode;
378,They to the farthest nations spread
378,The grace of their ascended Lord.

386,386 – The Sacred Anthem
386,1

386,Across the fields of praise
386,When earth’s first Sabbath made complete
386,All creatures and all days.
386,2

386,Woman and man together share
386,The blessed Sabbath mood;
386,And in that green and golden world
386,Know all God’s works are good.
386,3
386,But now in our diminished lives
386,We sing a blemished song;
386,The earth is worn and disarrayed
386,And all our work goes wrong.
386,4

386,And rest within God’s rest.

386,6

386,Around God’s shining throne.

437,437 – Im Going Home
437,1
437,My heav’nly home is bright and fair
437,Nor pain nor death can enter there;
437,It’s glitt’ring tow’rs the sun outshine
437,That heav’nly mansion shall me mine.
437,Refrain
437,I’m going home, I’m going home
437,I’m going home to die no more;
437,To die no more; to die no more-
437,I’m going home to die no more.
437,2
437,My Father’s house is built on high
437,Far, far above the starry sky;
437,When from this earthly prison free
437,That heav’nly mansion mine shall be.
437,3
437,Let others seek a home below
437,Which flames devour or waves oe’r flow;
437,Be mine a happier lot to own
437,A heav’nly mansion near the throne.

438,In a few more days.
438,3

438,You will see the saints arising
438,You will see the saints arising
438,In a few more days.
438,4
438,Angels bear them to the Savior
438,Angels bear them to the Savior
438,Angels bear them to the Savior
438,In a few more days.
438,5
438,Then we’ll shout, our suff’ring over
438,Then we’ll shout, our suff’ring over
438,Then we’ll shout, our suff’ring over
438,In a few more days.
439,439 – How Far From Home
439,1
439,How far from? I asked, as on
439,I bent my steps-the watchman spake:
439,“the long, dark night is almost gone
439,The morning soon will break.
439,Then weep no more, but speed thy flight
439,With Hope’s bright star guiding ray
439,Till thou shalt reach the realms of light
439,In everlasting days.”
439,2
439,I asked the warrior on the field;
439,This was his soul-inspiring song:
439,“With courage, bold, the sword I’ll wield
439,The battle is not long.
439,Then weep no more, but well endure
439,The conflict, till thy work is done;
439,For this we know, the prize is sure
439,When victory is won.”
439,3
439,I asked again; earth, sea, and sun
439,Seemed, with one voice, to make reply:
439,“Time’s wasting sands are nearly run
439,Eternity is nigh.
439,Then weep no more-with warning tones
439,Portentous signs are thickening round
439,The whole creation, waiting, groans
439,To hear the trumpet sound.”
439,4
439,Not far from home! O blessed thought!
439,The traveler’s lonely heart to cheer;
439,Which oft a healing balm has brought
439,And dried the mourner’s tear.
439,Then weep no more, since we shall meet
439,Where weary footsteps never roam-
439,Our trails past, our joys complete
439,Safe in our Father’s home.
440,440 – How Cheering Is the Christians Hope
440,1
440,How cheering is the Christian’s hope
440,While toiling here below!
440,It bouys us up while this passing through
440,This wilderness of woe
440,2
440,It bouys us up while this passing through
440,This wilderness of woe
440,It bouys us up while passing through
440,This wilderness of woe.
440,3
440,It points us to a land of rest
440,Where saints with Christ will reign;
440,Where we shall meet the loved of earth
440,And never part again.
440,4
440,Fly, lingering moments, fly, O, fly
440,Dear Savior, quickly come!
440,We long to see Thee as Thou art
440,And reach that blissful home.
441,441 – I Saw One Weary
441,1
441,I saw one weary, sad, and torn
441,With eager steps press on the way
441,Who long the hallowed cross had born
441,Still looking for the promised day;
441,While many a line of grief and care
441,Upon his brow was furrowed there;
441,I asked what buoyed his spirits up
441,“O this” said he-“the blessed hope.”
441,2
441,And one I saw, with sword and shield
441,Who boldly braved the world’s cold frown
441,And fought, unyielding, on the field
441,To win an everlasting crown.
441,Though worn with toil, oppressed by foes
441,No murmur from his heart arose;
441,I asked what buoyed his spirits up
441,“O this!” said he-“the blessed hope.”
441,3
441,And there was one who left behind
441,The cherished friends of early years
441,And honor, pleasure, wealth re-signed
441,To tread the path bedewed with tears.
441,Through trials deep and conflict sore
441,Yet still a smile of joy he wore;
441,O! what can bouy the spirit up?
441,‘Tis this alone-the blessed hope.
441,4
441,While pilgrims here we journey on
441,In this dark vale of sin and gloom
441,Through tribulation, hate, and scorn
441,Or through the portals of the tomb
441,Till our returning King shall come
441,To tkae His exile captives home
441,O! what can bouy the spirits up?
441,‘Tis this alone– the blessed hope.
442,442 – How Sweet Are the Tidings
442,1
442,How sweet are the tidings
442,that greet the pilgrim’s ear
442,As he wanders in exile from home!
442,Soon, soon will the Savior
442,in glory appear
442,And soon will the kingdom come.
442,Refrain
442,He’s coming, coming, coming soon I know
442,Coming back to this earth again;
442,And the weary pilgrims will to glory go
442,When the Savior comes to reign.
442,2
442,The mossy old graves
442,where the pilgrims sleep
442,Shall be open as wide as before
442,And the millions that sleep
442,in the mighty deep
442,Shall live on this earth once more.
442,3
442,There we’ll meet ne’er
442,to part in our happy
442,Eden home, Sweet songs
442,of redemption we’ll sing;
442,From the north, from the south
442,all the ransomed shall come
442,And worship our heavenly King.
442,4
442,Hallelujah, Amen!
442,Hallelujah again!
442,Soon, if faithful
442,we all shall be there;
442,O, be watchful, be hopeful
442,be joyful till then, And a crown
442,of bright glory we’ll wear.
443,443 – Therell Be No Sorrow There
443,1
443,There’ll be no night in heaven
443,In that blest world above;
443,No anxious toil, no weary hours;
443,For labor there is love.
443,Refrain
443,There’ll be no sorrow there
443,There’ll be no sorrow there;
443,In heaven above, where all is love
443,There’ll be no sorrow there.
443,2
443,There’ll be no grief in heaven;
443,For life is one glad day
443,And tears are those of former things
443,Which all have passed away.
443,3
443,There’ll be no sin in heaven;
443,Behold that blessed throng
443,All holy in there spotless robes
443,All holy in their song.
444,444 – Im a Pilgrim
444,1
444,I’m a pilgrim, and I’m a stranger;
444,I can tarry, I can tarry but a night;
444,Do not detain me, for I am going
444,To where the fountains are ever flowing.
444,Refrain
444,I’m a pilgrim, and I’m a stranger;
444,I can tarry, I can tarry but a night.
444,2
444,There the glory is ever shining!
444,O, my longing heart, my longing heart is there;
444,Here in this country so dark and dreary
444,I long have wandered forlorn and weary.
444,3
444,There’s the city to which I journey;
444,My Redeemer, my Redeemer is its light!
444,There is no sorrow, nor any sighing
444,Nor any tears there, or any dying.
445,445 – Im But a Stranger Here
445,1
445,I’m but a stranger here
445,Heav’n is my home;
445,Earth is a desert drear
445,Heav’n is my home.
445,Danger and sorrow stand
445,Round me on every hand;
445,Heav’n is my fatherland
445,Heav’n is my home.
445,2
445,What though the tempest rage
445,Heav’n is my home;
445,Short is my pilgrimage
445,Heav’n is my home;
445,And time’s wild wintry blast
445,Soon shall be over past;
445,I shall reach home at last
445,Heav’n is my home.
445,3
445,There at my Savior’s side
445,Heav’n is my home;
445,I shall be glorified
445,Heav’n is my home;
445,There are the good and blest
445,Those I love most and best;
445,And there I, too, shall rest
445,Heav’n is my home.

447,447 – Long Upon the Mountains
447,1
447,Long upon the mountains weary
447,Have the scattered flocks been torn;
447,Dark the dessert paths, and dreary;
447,Grievous trials have they borne.
447,Now the gathering call is sounding
447,Solemn in its warning voice;
447,Union, faith, and love, abounding
447,Bid the little flock rejoice.
447,2
447,Now the light of truth they’re seeking
447,In its onward track pursue;
447,All the ten commandments keeping
447,They are holy, just, and true.
447,On the words of lire they’re feeding
447,Precious to their taste so sweet;
447,All their Master’s percepts heeding
447,Bowing humbly to His feet.
447,3
447,In that light of light and beauty
447,In that golden city fair
447,Soon its pearly gates they’ll enter
447,And of all its glories share.
447,There, divine the soul’s expansions;
447,Free from sin, and death, and pain;
447,Tear will never dim those mansions
447,Where the souls immortal reign.
447,4
447,Soon He comes! With clouds descending;
447,All His saints, entombed arise;
447,The redeemed, in anthems blending
447,Shout their vict’ry thro’ the skies.
447,O, we long for Thine appearing;
447,Come, O Savior, quickly come!
447,Blessed hope! Our spirits cheering
447,Take thy ransomed children home.

449,And never, never part again.

449,What! Never part again? No, never part again
449,And soon we shall with Jesus reign
449,And never, never part again.
449,2

449,And never with’ring flowers
449,And but a little space divides
449,This heav’nly land from ours.
449,3
449,Could we but stand where Moses stood
449,And view the landscape o’er
449,Not all this world’s pretended good
449,Could ever charm us more.

452,452 – What Heavenly Music
452,1
452,What heavenly music steals over the sea!
452,Entrancing the senses like sweet melody!
452,‘Tis the voice of the angels borne soft on the air;
452,For me they are singing; their welcome I hear.
452,2
452,On the banks of old Jordan, here gazing I stand
452,And earnestly longing, I stretch forth my hand;
452,Send a convoy of angels, dear Jesus, I pray!
452,Let me join that sweet music; come, take me away.
452,3
452,Though dark are the waters and rough is the wave
452,If Jesus permit, the wild surges I’ll brave;
452,For that heavenly music hath ravished me so
452,I must join in that chorus! I’ll go! let me go!
453,453 – We Have Heard
453,1
453,We have heard from the bright, the holy, land;
453,We have heard, and our hearts are glad;
453,For we were a lonely pilgrim band
453,And weary, and worn, and sad.
453,They tell us the saints have a dwelling there-
453,No longer are homeless ones;
453,And we know that the goodly land is fair
453,Where life’s pure river runs.
453,2
453,They say green fields are waving there
453,That never a blight shall know;
453,And the deserts wild are blooming fair
453,And the roses of Sharon grow.
453,There are lovely birds in the bowers green
453,Their songs are blithe and sweet;
453,And their warblings, gushing ever new
453,The angels’ harpings greet.
453,3
453,We have heard of the palms, the robes, the crowns
453,And the silvery band in white;
453,Of the city fair, with pearly gates
453,All radiant with light.
453,We have heard of the angels there, and saints
453,With their harps of gold, how they sing;
453,Of the mount with the fruitful tree of life
453,Of the leaves that healing bring.
453,4
453,The King of that country, He is fair
453,He’s the joy and light of the place;
453,In His beauty we shall behold Him there
453,And bask in His smiling face
453,We’ll be there, we’ll be there in a little while
453,We’ll join the pure and the blest;
453,We’ll have the palm, the robe, the crown
453,And forever be at rest.

454,Will you go to glory with me?
454,Hallelujah! O praise ye the Lord!
454,2
454,Don’t you see the saints ascending
454,Hear them shouting thro’ the air.
454,Jesus smiling, trumpets sounding
454,Now His glory they shall share.
455,455 – Immortal Love, Forever Full
455,1
455,Immortal Love, forever full
455,Forever flowing free
455,Forever shared, forever whole
455,A never ebbing sea!
455,2
455,We nay not climb the heavenly steeps
455,To bring the Lord Christ down;
455,In vain we search the lowest deeps
455,For him no depths can drown.
455,3
455,But warm, so tender, even yet
455,A present help is He;
455,And faith has still its Olivet
455,And love its Galilee.
455,4
455,The healing of His seamless dress
455,Is by our beds of pain;
455,We touch Him in life’s throng and press
455,And we are whole again.
455,5
455,Through Him the first fond prayers are said
455,Our lips of childhood frame;
455,The last low whispers of our dead
455,Are burdened with His name.
455,6
455,O Lord and Master of us all:
455,Whate’er our names or sign
455,We own Thy sway, we hear Thy call
455,We test our lives by Thine!
456,456 – My Lord and I
456,1
456,I have a Friend so precious
456,So very dear to me
456,He loves me with such tender love
456,He loves so faithfully;
456,I could not live apart form Him
456,I love to feel Him nigh
456,And so we dwell together
456,My Lord and I.
456,2
456,Sometimes I’m faint and weary
456,He knows that I am weak
456,And as He bids me lean on Him
456,His help I gladly seek;
456,He leads me in the paths of light
456,Beneath a sunny sky
456,And so we walk together
456,My Lord and I.
456,3
456,I tell Him all my sorrows
456,I tell Him all my joys
456,I tell Him all that pleases me
456,I tell Him what annoys;
456,He tells me what I ought to do
456,He tells me how to try
456,And so we talk together
456,My Lord and I.
456,4
456,He knows that I am longing
456,Some weary soul to win
456,And so He bids me go and speak
456,The loving word for Him;
456,He bids me tell His wondrous love
456,And why He came to die
456,And so we work together
456,My Lord and I.
457,457 – I Love to Tell the Story
457,1
457,I love to tell the story
457,of unseen things above
457,of Jesus and his glory
457,of Jesus and his love.
457,I love to tell the story
457,because I know ’tis true;
457,it satisfies my longings
457,as nothing else can do.
457,Refrain
457,I love to tell the story
457,’twill be my theme in glory
457,to tell the old, old story
457,of Jesus and his love.
457,2
457,I love to tell the story;
457,more wonderful it seems
457,than all the golden fancies
457,of all our golden dreams.
457,I love to tell the story
457,it did so much for me;
457,and that is just the reason
457,I tell it now to thee.
457,3
457,I love to tell the story;
457,’tis pleasant to repeat
457,what seems, each time I tell it
457,more wonderfully sweet.
457,I love to tell the story
457,for some have never heard
457,the message of salvation
457,from God’s own holy Word.
457,4
457,I love to tell the story
457,for those who know it best
457,seem hungering and thirsting
457,to hear it like the rest.
457,And when, in scenes of glory
457,I sing the new, new song
457,’twill be the old, old story
457,that I have loved so long.

460,460 – As Water to the Thirsty
460,1
460,As water to the thirsty
460,As beauty to the eyes
460,As strength that follows weakness
460,As truth instead of lies;
460,As song-time and springtime and summertime to be
460,So is my Lord, my living Lord
460,So is my Lord to me.
460,2
460,Like calm in place of clamor
460,Like peace that follows pain
460,Like meeting after parting
460,Like sunshine after rain;
460,Like moonlight and starlight and sunlight on the sea
460,So is my Lord, my living Lord
460,So is my Lord to me.
460,3
460,As sleep that follows fever
460,As gold instead of grey
460,As freedom after bondage
460,As sunrise to the day;
460,As home to the trav’ler and all he longs to see
460,So is my Lord, my living Lord
460,So is my Lord to me.
461,461 – Be Still, My Soul
461,1
461,Be still, my soul:
461,the Lord is on thy side;
461,Bear patiently the cross of grief or pain;
461,Leave to thy God to order and provide;
461,In every change He faithful will remain.
461,Refrain
461,Be still, my soul:
461,thy best, thy heavenly friend
461,Through thorny ways leads to a joyful end.
461,2
461,Be still, my soul:
461,thy God doth undertake
461,To guide the future as He has the past.
461,Thy hope, thy confidence let nothing shake;
461,All now mysterious shall be bright at last.
461,3
461,Be still, my soul:
461,the hour is hastening on
461,When we shall be forever with the Lord
461,When disappointment, grief, and fear are gone
461,Sorrow forgot, love’s purest joys restored.
462,462 – Blessed Assurance, Jesus is Mine!
462,1
462,Blessed assurance, Jesus is mine!
462,O what a foretaste of glory divine!
462,Heir of salvation, purchase of God
462,born of his Spirit, washed in his blood.
462,Refrain
462,This is my story, this is my song
462,praising my Savior all the day long;
462,this is my story, this is my song
462,praising my Savior all the day long.
462,2
462,Perfect submission, perfect delight
462,visions of rapture now burst on my sight;
462,angels descending bring from above
462,echoes of mercy, whispers of love.
462,3
462,Perfect submission, all is at rest;
462,I in my Savior am happy and blest
462,watching and waiting, looking above
462,filled with his goodness, lost in his love.
463,463 – Peace, Perfect Peace
463,1
463,Peace, perfect peace, in this dark world of sin?
463,The blood of Jesus whispers peace within.
463,2
463,Peace, perfect peace, by thronging duties pressed?
463,To do the will of Jesus: this is rest.
463,3
463,Peace, perfect peace, with loved ones far away?
463,In Jesus’ keeping we are safe, and they.
463,4
463,Peace, perfect peace, our future all unknown?
463,Jesus we know, and He is on the throne.

464,And face a frowning world;
464,And face a frowning world
464,And face a frowning world
464,Then I can smile at Satan’s rage
464,And face a frowning world.
465,465 – I Heard the Voice of Jesus
465,1
465,I heard the voice of Jesus say
465,“Come unto Me and rest;
465,Lay down, thou weary one, lay down
465,Thy head upon My breast.”
465,I came to Jesus as I was
465,Weary and worn and sad;
465,I found in Him a resting place
465,And He has made me glad.
465,2
465,I heard the voice of Jesus say
465,“Behold, I freely give
465,The living water; thirsty one
465,Stoop down and drink and live.”
465,I came to Jesus, and I drank
465,Of that life giving stream;
465,My thirst was quench’d, my soul revived
465,And now I live in Him.
465,3
465,I heard the voice of Jesus say
465,“I am this dark world’s light;
465,Look unto Me, thy morn shall rise
465,And all thy day be bright.”
465,I looked to Jesus, and I found
465,In Him my star, my sun;
465,And in that light of life I’ll walk
465,Till trav’ling days are done.
466,466 – Wonderful Peace
466,1
466,Far away in the depths of my spirit tonight
466,Rolls a melody sweeter than psalm;
466,In celestial like strains it unceasingly falls
466,O’er my soul like an infinite calm.
466,Refrain
466,Peace! Peace! wonderful peace
466,Coming down from the Father above;
466,Sweep over my spirit forever, I pray
466,In fathomless billows of love.
466,2
466,What a treasure I have in this wonderful peace
466,Buried deep in my inner most soul
466,So secure that no power can mine it away
466,While the years of eternity roll!
466,3
466,I believe when I rise to that city of peace
466,Where the Author of peace I shall see
466,That one strain of the song which the ransomed will sing
466,In that heavenly kingdom will be-
466,4
466,Weary soul, without gladness or comfort or rest
466,Passing down the rough pathway of time!
466,Make the Savior your friend ere the shadows grow dark;
466,O accept of this peace so sublime.
467,467 – Life Is Great! So Sing About It
467,1
467,Life is great! So sing about it
467,As we can and as we should-
467,Shop and buses, towns and people
467,Village, farmland, field and wood
467,Life is great and life is given;
467,Life is lovely, free and good.
467,2
467,Life is great! What ever happens
467,Snow or sunshine, joy or pain
467,Hardship, grief or disillusion
467,Suffering that I can’t explain
467,Life is great if someone loves me
467,Holds my hand and calls my name.
467,3
467,Love is great! The love of lovers
467,Whispered words and longing eyes;
467,Love that gazes at the cradle
467,Where a child of loving lies;
467,Love that lasts when youth has faded
467,Bends with age, but never dies.
467,4
467,Love is giving and receiving
467,Boy and girl, or friend with friend;
467,Love is bearing and forgiving
467,All the hurts that hate can send;
467,Love’s the greatest way of living
467,Hoping, trusting to the end.
467,5
467,God is great! in Christ He loved us
467,As we should, but never can-
467,Love that suffered, hoped and trusted
467,When disciples turned and ran
467,Love that broke through death forever.
467,Praise that loving, living Man!
468,468 – A Child of the King
468,1
468,My Father is rich in houses and lands
468,He holdeth the wealth of the world in His hands!
468,Of rubies and diamonds, of silver and gold
468,His coffers are full, He has riches untold.
468,Refrain
468,I’m a child of the King
468,A child of the King:
468,With Jesus my Savior
468,I’m a child of the King.
468,2
468,My Father’s own Son, the Savior of men
468,Once wandered on earth as the poorest of them;
468,But now He is pleading our pardon on high
468,That we may be His when He comes by and by.
468,3
468,I once was an outcast stranger on earth
468,A sinner by choice, an alien by birth
468,But I’ve been adopted, my name’s written down
468,An heir to a mansion, a robe and a crown.
468,4
468,A tent or a cottage, why should I care?
468,They’re building a palace for me over there;
468,Though exiled from home, yet still may I sing:
468,All glory to God, I’m a child of the King.

472,472 – A Song of Heaven and Homeland
472,1
472,Sometimes I hear strange music
472,Like none e’er heard before
472,Come floating softly earthward
472,As thro’ heav’n’s open door:
472,It seems like angel voices
472,In strains of and love
472,That swell the mighty chorus
472,Around the throne above.
472,Refrain
472,O sweet, celestial music
472,Heard from a land afar-
472,The song of Heav’n and Homeland
472,Thro’ doors God leaves ajar!
472,2
472,Now soft, and low, and restful
472,It floods my soul with peace
472,As if God’s benediction
472,Bade all earth’s troubles cease.
472,Then grander than the voices
472,Of wind, and wave, and sea-
472,It fills the dome of heaven
472,With glorious harmony.
472,3
472,This music haunts me ever
472,Like something heard in dreams-
472,It seems to catch the cadence
472,Of heav’nly winds and streams
472,My heart is filled with rapture
472,To think, some day to come
472,I’ll sing it with the angels-
472,The song of heav’n and home.

473,1

473,nearer, my God, to thee;
473,nearer, my God, to thee, nearer to thee!
473,2

473,darkness be over me, my rest a stone;
473,yet in my dreams I’d be
473,nearer, my God, to thee;
473,nearer, my God, to thee, nearer to thee!
473,3

473,all that thou sendest me, in mercy given;
473,angels to beckon me
473,nearer, my God, to thee;
473,nearer, my God, to thee, nearer to thee!
473,4

473,so by my woes to be
473,nearer, my God, to thee;
473,nearer, my God, to thee, nearer to thee!
473,5

473,still all my song shall be
473,nearer, my God, to thee;
473,nearer, my God, to thee, nearer to thee!

478,478 – Sweet Hour of Prayer
478,1
478,Sweet hour of prayer! sweet hour of prayer!
478,that calls me from a world of care
478,and bids me at my Father’s throne
478,make all my wants and wishes known.
478,In seasons of distress and grief
478,my soul has often found relief
478,and oft escaped the tempter’s snare
478,by thy return, sweet hour of prayer!
478,2
478,Sweet hour of prayer! sweet hour of prayer!
478,thy wings shall my petition bear
478,to him whose truth and faithfulness
478,engage the waiting soul to bless.
478,And since he bids me seek his face
478,believe his word, and trust his grace
478,I’ll cast on him my every care
478,and wait for thee, sweet hour of prayer!
478,3
478,Sweet hour of prayer! sweet hour of prayer!
478,May I thy consolation share
478,Till from Mount Pisgah’s lofty height
478,I view my home and take my flight.
478,In my immortal flesh I’ll rise
478,To size the everlasting prize.
478,And shout while passing through the air
478,“Farewell, farewell, sweet hour of prayer!”

480,in purer lives thy service find
480,in deeper reverence, praise.
480,2

480,beside the Syrian sea
480,the gracious calling of the Lord
480,let us, like them, without a word
480,rise up and follow thee.
480,3

480,O calm of hills above
480,where Jesus knelt to share with thee
480,the silence of eternity
480,interpreted by love!
480,4

480,till all our strivings cease;
480,take from our souls the strain and stress
480,and let our ordered lives confess
480,the beauty of thy peace.
480,5
480,Breathe through the heats of our desire
480,thy coolness and thy balm;
480,let sense be dumb, let flesh retire;
480,speak through the earthquake, wind, and fire
480,O still, small voice of calm.

488,The heaven’s serene abode.

488,Though foes were all abroad.

488,However dark His plan.
488,5
488,And light and strength and faith
488,Are opening everywhere!
488,God waited patiently until
488,I prayed the larger prayer.
