494,494 – We Would See Jesus
494,1
494,“We would see Jesus;” for the shadows lengthen
494,Across the little landscape of our life;
494,We would see Jesus, our weak faith to strengthen
494,For the last conflict, in this mortal strife.
494,2
494,“We would see Jesus,” Rock of our salvation
494,Where on our feet were set with sovereign grace;
494,Not life, nor death, with all their agitation
494,Can thence remove us, gazing on His face.
494,3
494,“We would see Jesus;” other lights are paling
494,Which for long years we did rejoice to see;
494,The blessings of this sinful world are failing;
494,We would not mourn them, in exchange for Thee.
494,4
494,“We would see Jesus;” this is all we’re needing-
494,Strength, joy and willingness come with the sight;
494,We would see Jesus, dying, risen, pleading
494,Soon to return and end this mortal night!
495,495 – Near to the Heart of God
495,1
495,There is a place of quiet rest
495,near to the heart of God;
495,a place where sin cannot molest
495,near to the heart of God.
495,Refrain
495,O Jesus, blest Redeemer
495,sent from the heart of God
495,hold us who wait before thee
495,near to the heart of God.
495,2
495,There is a place of comfort sweet
495,near to the heart of God;
495,a place where we our Savior meet
495,near to the heart of God.
495,3
495,There is place a place of full release
495,near to the heart of God;
495,a place where all is joy and peace
495,near to the heart of God.
496,496 – Eternal Love, We Have No Good
496,1
496,Eternal Love, we have no good to bring Thee
496,No single good of all our hands have wrought
496,No worthy music have we found to sing Thee
496,No jewelled word, no quick up soaring thought.
496,2
496,And yet we come; and when our faith would falter
496,Show us, O Love, the quiet place of prayer
496,The golden censer and the golden altar
496,And the great angel waiting for us there.
497,497 – O Gracious Father of Mankind
497,1
497,O gracious Father of mankind
497,Our spirits’ unseen friend;
497,High heaven’s Lord, our hearts’ dear guest
497,To Thee our prayers ascend.
497,2
497,Thou dost not wait till human speech
497,Thy gifts divine implore;
497,Our dreams, our aims, our work, our lives
497,Are prayers Thou lovest more.
497,3
497,Thou hearest these, the good and ill
497,Deep buried in each breast;
497,The secret thought, the hidden plan
497,Wrought out our unexpressed.
497,4
497,O cleanse our prayers from human dross
497,Attune our lives to Thee
497,Until we labor for those gifts
497,We ask on bended knee.
497,5
497,Our best is but Thyself in us
497,Our highest thought Thy will;
497,To hear Thy voice we need but love
497,And listen, and be still.
497,6
497,We would not bend Thy will to ours
497,But blend our wills to Thine;
497,Not dreams, our aims, our work, our lives
497,Are prayers Thou lovest more.
497,7
497,Thou seekest us in love and truth
497,More than our minds seek Thee;
497,Through open gates Thy power flows in
497,Like flood tides from the sea.
497,8
497,No more we seek Thee from afar
497,Nor ask Thee for a sign
497,Content to pray in life and love
497,And toil, till all are Thine.
498,498 – Still, Still With Thee
498,1
498,Still, still with Thee, when purple morning breaketh
498,When the bird waketh, and the shadows flee;
498,Fairer than morning, lovelier than daylight
498,Dawns the sweet consciousness, I am with Thee.
498,2
498,Alone with Thee, amid the mystic shadows
498,The solemn hush of nature newly born;
498,Alone with Thee in breathless adoration
498,In the calm dew and freshness of the morn.
498,3
498,Still, still with Thee! As to each newborn morning
498,A fresh and solemn splendor still is given
498,So does this blessed consciousness, awaking
498,Breathe each day nearness unto Thee and heaven.
498,4
498,So shall it be at last, in that bright morning
498,When the soul waketh and life’s shadows flee;
498,O in that hour, fairer than daylight dawning
498,Shall rise the glorious thought, I am with Thee.
499,499 – What a Friend We Have in Jesus
499,1
499,What a friend we have in Jesus
499,All our sins and griefs to bear!
499,What a privilege to carry
499,Everything to God in prayer!
499,Oh, what peace we often forfeit;
499,Oh, what needless pain we bear
499,All because we do not carry
499,Everything to God in prayer!
499,2
499,Have we trials and temptations?
499,Is there trouble anywhere?
499,We should never be discouraged
499,Take it to the Lord in prayer.
499,Can we find a friend so faithful
499,Who will all our sorrows share?
499,Jesus knows our every weakness
499,Take it to the Lord in prayer.
499,3
499,Are we weak and heavy laden
499,Cumbered with a load of care?
499,Precious Savior, still our refuge
499,Take it to the Lord in prayer.
499,Do your friends despise, forsake you?
499,Take it to the Lord in prayer.
499,In his arms he’ll take and shield you;
499,You will find a solace there.
500,500 – Take Time to Be Holy
500,1
500,Take time to be holy
500,speak oft with thy Lord;
500,abide in him always
500,and feed on his word.
500,Make friends of God’s children
500,help those who are weak
500,forgetting in nothing
500,his blessing to seek.
500,2
500,Take time to be holy
500,the world rushes on;
500,spend much time in secret
500,with Jesus alone.
500,By looking to Jesus
500,like him thou shalt be;
500,thy friends in thy conduct
500,his likeness shall see.
500,3
500,Take time to be holy
500,let him be thy guide
500,and run not before him
500,whatever betide.
500,In joy or in sorrow
500,still follow the Lord
500,and, looking to Jesus
500,still trust in his word.
500,4
500,Take time to be holy
500,be calm in thy soul
500,each thought and each motive
500,beneath his control.
500,Thus led by his spirit
500,to fountains of love
500,thou soon shalt be fitted
500,for service above.
501,501 – Tis the Blessed Hour of Prayer
501,1
501,‘Tis the blessed hour of prayer, when our hearts lowly bend
501,And we gather to Jesus, our Savior and Friend;
501,If we come to Him in faith, His protection to share
501,Refrain
501,What a balm for the weary! O how sweet to be there!
501,Blessed hour of prayer, Blessed hour of prayer
501,What a balm for the weary! O how sweet to be there!
501,2
501,‘Tis the blessed hour of prayer, when the Savior draws near
501,With a tender compassion His children to hear;
501,When He tells us we may cast at His feet every care
501,3
501,‘Tis the blessed hour of prayer, when the tempted and tried
501,To the Savior who loves them their sorrows confide;
501,With a sympathizing heart He removes every care;
501,4
501,‘Tis the blessed hour of prayer, trusting Him we believe
501,That the blessings we’re needing we’ll surely receive;
501,In the fullness of this trust we shall lose every care;
502,502 – Sun of My Soul
502,1
502,Sun of my soul, O Savior dear!
502,It is not night if Thou be near;
502,O may no earth-born cloud arise
502,To hide Thee from Thy servant’s eyes.
502,2
502,When soft the dews of kindly sleep
502,My weary eyelids gently steep
502,Be my last thought how sweet to rest
502,Forever on my Savior’s breast!
502,3
502,Abide with me from morn till eve
502,For without Thee I cannot live;
502,Abide with me when night is nigh
502,For without Thee I dare not die.
502,4
502,Be near and bless me when I wake
502,Ere through the world my way I take;
502,Till in the ocean of Thy love
502,I lose myself in heaven above.
503,503 – A Quiet Place
503,1
503,There is a quiet place
503,Far from the rapid pace
503,where God can soothe my troubled mind.
503,Sheltered by tree and flow’r
503,There in my quiet hour with Him
503,my cares are left behind.
503,Whether a garden small
503,Or on a mountain tall
503,New strength and courage there I find;
503,Then from this quiet place
503,I go prepared to face a new day
503,With love for all mankind.
504,504 – Lord Jesus, Think on Me
504,1
504,Lord Jesus, think on me
504,And purge away my sin;
504,From earth-born passions set me free
504,And make me pure within.
504,2
504,Lord Jesus, think on me
504,With care and woe oppressed;
504,Let me Thy loving servant be
504,And taste Thy promised rest.
504,3
504,Lord Jesus, think on me
504,Nor let me go astray;
504,Through darkness and perplexity
504,Point Thou the heavenly way.
504,4
504,Lord Jesus, think on me
504,That I may sing above
504,To Father, Spirit, and to Thee
504,The strains of praise and love.
505,505 – I Need the Prayers
505,1
505,I need the prayers of those I love
505,While trav’ling o’er life’s rugged way
505,That I may true and faithful be
505,And live for Jesus every day.
505,Refrain
505,I want my friends to pray for me
505,To bear my tempted soul above
505,And intercede with God for me;
505,I need the prayers of those I love.
505,2
505,I need the prayers of those I love
505,To help me in each trying hour
505,To bear my tempted sould to Him
505,That He may keep me by His pow’r.
505,Refrain
505,I want my friends to pray for me
505,To hold me up on wing of faith
505,That I may walk the narrow way
505,Kept by our Father’s glorious grace.
506,506 – A Mighty Fortress
506,1
506,A mighty fortress is our God
506,a bulwark never failing;
506,our helper he amid the flood
506,of mortal ills prevaling.
506,For still our ancient foe
506,doth seek to work us woe;
506,his craft and power are great
506,and armed with cruel hate
506,on earth is not his equal.
506,2
506,Did we in our own strength confide
506,our striving would be losing
506,were not the right man on our side
506,the man of God’s own choosing.
506,Dost ask who that may be?
506,Christ Jesus, it is he;
506,Lord Sabbaoth, his name
506,from age to age the same
506,and he must win the battle.
506,3
506,And though this world, with devils filled
506,should threaten to undo us
506,we will not fear, for God hath willed
506,his truth to triumph through us.
506,The Prince of Darkness grim
506,we tremble not for him;
506,his rage we can endure
506,for lo, his doom is sure;
506,one little word shall fell him.
506,4
506,That word above all earthly powers
506,no thanks to them, abideth;
506,the Spirit and the gifts are ours
506,thru him who with us sideth.
506,Let goods and kindred go
506,this mortal life also;
506,the body they may kill;
506,God’s truth abideth still;
506,his kingdom is forever.
507,507 – Moment by Moment
507,1
507,Dying with Jesus, by death reckoned mine
507,Living with Jesus, a new life divine
507,Looking to Jesus till glory doth shine
507,Moment by moment, O Lord, I am Thine.
507,Refrain
507,Moment by moment I’m kept in His love;
507,Moment by moment I’ve life from above;
507,Looking to Jesus till glory doth shine;
507,Moment by moment, O Lord, I am Thine.
507,2
507,Never a trial that He is not there
507,Never a burden that He doth not bear
507,Never a sorrow that He doth not share
507,Moment by moment I’m under His care.
507,3
507,Never a heart-ache, and never a groan
507,Never a teardrop and never a moan;
507,Never a danger but there on teh throne
507,Moment by moment He thinks of His own.
507,4
507,Never a weakness that He doth not feel
507,Never a sickness that He cannot heal;
507,Moment by moment, in woe or in weal
507,Jesus, my Savior, abides with me still.
508,508 – Anywhere With Jesus
508,1
508,Anywhere with Jesus I can safely go
508,Anywhere He leads me in this world below;
508,Anywhere without Him dearest joys would fade;
508,Anywhere with Jesus I am not afraid.
508,Refrain
508,Anywhere, anywhere! Fear I cannot know;
508,Anywhere with Jesus I can safely go.
508,2
508,Anywhere with Jesus I am not alone;
508,Other friends may fail me, He is still my own;
508,Though His hand may lead me over drearest ways
508,Anywhere with Jesus is a house of praise.
508,3
508,Anywhere with Jesus I can go to sleep
508,When the darkening shadows round about me creep
508,Knowing I shall waken nevermore to roam;
508,Anywhere with Jesus will be home, sweet home.
509,509 – How Firm a Foundation
509,1
509,How firm a foundation, ye saints of the Lord
509,is laid for your faith in his excellent word!
509,What more can he say than to you he hath said
509,to you who for refuge to Jesus have fled?
509,2
509,“Fear not, I am with thee, O be not dismayed
509,for I am thy God and will still give thee aid;
509,I’ll strengthen and help thee, and cause thee to stand
509,upheld by my righteous, omnipotent hand.”
509,3
509,“When through deep waters I call thee to go
509,the rivers of woe shall not thee overflow;
509,for I will be with thee, thy troubles to bless
509,and sanctify to thee thy deepest distress.”
509,4
509,“When through fiery trials thy pathways shall lie
509,my grace, all-sufficient, shall be thy supply;
509,the flame shall not hurt thee; I only design
509,thy dross to consume, and thy gold to refine.”
509,5
509,“The soul that on Jesus hath leaned for respose
509,I will not, I will not depart to His foes;
509,That soul, though all hell should endeavor to shake
509,I’ll never, no never, no never forsake!”
510,510 – If You But Trust in God to Guide You
510,1
510,If you but trust in God to guide you
510,And place your confidence in Him
510,You’ll find Him always there beside you
510,To give you hope and strength within.
510,For those who trust God’s changeless love
510,Build on the rock that will not move.
510,2
510,What gain is there in futile weeping
510,In helpless anger and distress?
510,If you are in His care and keeping
510,In sorrow will He love you less?
510,For He who took for you a cross
510,Will bring you safe through every loss.
510,3
510,In patient trust await His leisure
510,In cheerful hope, with heart content
510,To take whate’er your Father’s pleasure
510,And all discerning love have sent;
510,Doubt not your inmost wants are known
510,To Him who chose you for His own.
510,4
510,Sing, pray, and keep His ways unswerving
510,Offer your service faithfully
510,And trust His word; though undeserving
510,You’ll find His promise true to be.
510,God never will forsake in need
510,The soul that trusts in Him indeed.
511,511 – I Know Whom I Have Believed
511,1
511,I know not why God’s wondrous grace
511,To me He hath made known
511,Nor why, unworthy, Christ in love
511,Redeemed me for His own.
511,Refrain
511,But “I know whom I have believed
511,and am persuaded that His is able
511,To keep that which I’ve committed
511,Unto Him against that day.”
511,2
511,I know not how this saving faith
511,To me He did impart
511,Nor how believing in His word
511,Wrought peace within my heart.
511,3
511,I know not how the Spirit moves
511,Convincing men of sin
511,Revealing Jesus through the word
511,Creating faith in Him.
511,4
511,I know not when my Lord may come
511,At night or noonday fair
511,Nor if I walk the vale with Him
511,Or meet Him in the air.

512,Never forsaking, all the way through

512,Just when I need Him most
512,Jesus is near to comfort and cheer
512,Just when I need Him most.
512,3
512,Just when I need Him, Jesus is strong
512,Bearing my burdens all the day long;
512,For all my sorrow giving a song
512,Just when I need Him most.
512,Just when I need Him most
512,Just when I need Him most
512,Jesus is near to comfort and cheer
512,Just when I need Him most.
512,4

512,Answering when upon Him I call;

512,Just when I need Him most
512,Just when I need Him most
512,Jesus is near to comfort and cheer

513,513 – In Heavenly Love Abiding
513,1
513,In heavenly love abiding
513,No change my heart shall fear;
513,And safe is such confiding
513,For nothing changes here.
513,The storm may roar without me
513,My heart may low be laid;
513,But God is round about me
513,And can I be dismayed?
513,2
513,Wherever He may guide me
513,No want shall turn me back;
513,My Shepherd is besided me
513,And nothing can I lack.
513,His wisdom ever waketh
513,His sight is never dim;
513,He knows the way He taketh
513,And I will walk with Him.
513,3
513,Green pastures are before me
513,Which yet I have not seen;
513,Bright skies will soon be o’er me
513,Where darkest clouds have been.
513,My hope I cannot measure
513,My path to life is free;
513,My Savior has my teasure
513,And He will walk with me.
514,514 – Lord of Our Life
514,1
514,Lord of our life, and God of our salvation
514,Star of our night, and hope of every nation
514,Hear and receive Thy church’s supplication
514,Lord God Almighty.
514,2
514,Lord, Thou canst help when earthly armor faileth;
514,Lord, Thou canst save when deadly sin assaileth;
514,Lord, o’er Thy rock nor death nor hell prevaileth;
514,Grant us Thy peace, Lord
514,3
514,Peace in our hearts our evil thoughts assuaging;
514,Peace in Thy church, where brothers are engaging;
514,Peace, when the world its busy war is waging;
514,Send us, O Savior.
514,4
514,Grant us Thy help till foes are backward driven;
514,Grant them Thy truth that they may be forgiven;
514,Grant peace on earth, and, after we have striven
514,Peace in Thy heaven.
515,515 – The Lord Is My Light
515,1
515,The Lord is my light; then why should I fear?
515,By day and by night His presence is near;
515,He is my salvation from sorrow and sin;
515,This blessed persuasion the Spirit brings in.
515,Refrain
515,The Lord is my light, my joy, and my song;
515,By day and by night He leads me along;
515,The Lord is my light, my joy, and my song;
515,By day and by night He leads me along.
515,2
515,The Lord is my light; though clods may arise
515,Faith, stronger than sight, looks up to the skies
515,Where Jesus forever in glory doth reign:
515,Then how can I ever in darkness remain?
515,3
515,The Lord is my light, the Lord is my strength;
515,I know in His might I’ll conquer at length;
515,My weakness in mercy He covers with power
515,And, walking by faith, He upholds me each hour.
515,4
515,The lord is my light, my all and in all;
515,There is in His sight no darkness at all;
515,He is my Redeemer, my Savior and King;
515,With saints and with angels His praises I sing.
516,516 – All the Way
516,1
516,All the way my Savior leads me;
516,What have I to ask beside?
516,Can I doubt His tender mercy
516,Who through life has been my guide?
516,Heavenly peace, divinest comfort
516,Here by faith in Him to dwell;
516,For I know whate’er befall me
516,Jesus doeth all things well;
516,For I know whate’er befall me
516,Jesus doeth all things well.
516,2
516,All the way my Savior leads me;
516,Cheers each winding path I tread;
516,Gives me grace for every trial
516,Feeds me with the living bread;
516,Though my weary steps may falter
516,And my soul athirst may be
516,Gushing from the Rock before me
516,Lo, a spring of joy I see;
516,Gushing from the Rock before me
516,Lo, a spring of joy I see.
516,3
516,All the way my Savior leads me;
516,O the fullness of His love!
516,Perfect rest to me is promised
516,In my Father’s house above;
516,When I wake to life immortal
516,Wing my flight to realms of day
516,This my song through endless ages
516,Jesus led me all the way;
516,This my song through endless ages
516,Jesus led me all the way.
517,517 – My Faith Looks Up to Thee
517,1
517,My faith looks up to thee
517,thou Lamb of Calvary
517,Savior divine;
517,Now hear me while I pray
517,take all my guilt away
517,O let me from this day
517,be wholly Thine.
517,2
517,May thy rich grace impart
517,strength to my fainting heart
517,my zeal inspire!
517,As thou hast died for me
517,O may my love to thee
517,pure, warm, and changeless be
517,a living fire!
517,3
517,While life’s dark maze I tread
517,and griefs around me spread
517,be thou my guide;
517,bid darkness turn to day
517,wipe sorrow’s tears away
517,nor let me ever stray
517,from Thee aside.
518,518 – Standing on the Promises
518,1
518,Standing on the promises of Christ my King
518,Thru eternal ages let His praises ring;
518,Glory in the highest I will shout and sing
518,Standing on the promises of God.
518,Refrain
518,Standing, standing
518,Standing on the promises
518,of God my Savior;
518,Standing, standing
518,I’m standing on the promises of God.
518,2
518,Standing on the promises that cannot fail
518,When the howling storms of doubt and fear assail
518,By the living word of God I shall prevail
518,Standing on the promises of God.
518,3
518,Standing on the promises of Christ the Lord
518,Bound to Him eternally by love’s strong cord
518,Overcoming daily with the Spirit’s sword
518,Standing on the promises of God.
519,519 – Give to the Winds Your Fears
519,1
519,Give to the winds your fears;
519,In hope be undismayed:
519,God hears your sighs and coundts your tears
519,God shall lift up your head.
519,2
519,To Him commit your griefs;
519,Your ways put in His hands
519,To His sure truth adn tender care
519,Who earth adn heave commands.
519,3
519,O put your trust in God;
519,In duty’s path go on.
519,Walk in His strength with faith and hope
519,So shall your work be done.
519,4
519,Leave to His sovereign sway
519,To choose and to command;
519,So you shall, faithful, seek His way
519,how wise, how strong His hand!
520,520 – He Hideth My Soul
520,1
520,A wonderful Savior is Jesus my Lord
520,A wonderful Savior to me
520,He hideth my soul in the cleft of the rock
520,Where rivers of pleasure I see.
520,Refrain
520,He hideth my soul in the cleft of the rock
520,That shadows a dry, thirsty land;
520,he hideth my life in the depths of His love
520,And covers me there with His hand
520,And covers me there with His hand.
520,2
520,A wonderful Savior is Jesus my Lord
520,He taketh my burden away
520,He holdeth me up, and I shall not be moved
520,He giveth me strength as my day.
520,3
520,With numberless blessings each moment He crowns
520,And filled with His fullness divine
520,I sing in my rapture, Oh, Glory to God
520,For such a Redeemer as mine.
520,4
520,When clothed in His brightness, transported I rise
520,To meet Him in clouds of the sky
520,His perfect salvation, His wonderful love
520,I’ll shout with the millions on high.
521,521 – Depth of Mercy
521,1
521,Depth of mercy!–can there be
521,Mercy still reserved for me?
521,Can my God His wrath forbear?
521,Me, the chief of sinners, spare?
521,2
521,I have long withstood His grace
521,Long provoked Him to His face
521,Would not hearken to His calls
521,Grieved Him by a thousand falls.
521,3
521,Now incline me to repent;
521,Let me now my sins lament;
521,Now my foul revolt deplore
521,Weep, believe, and sin no more.
521,4
521,There for me the Savior stands
521,Shows His wounds and spreads His hands;
521,God is love! I know, I feel;
521,Jesus weeps, and loves me still.
522,522 – My Hope Is Built on Nothing Less
522,1
522,My hope is built on nothing less
522,than Jesus’ blood and righteousness.
522,I dare not trust the sweetest frame
522,but wholly lean on Jesus’ name.
522,Refrain
522,On Christ the solid rock I stand;
522,all other ground is sinking sand
522,all other ground is sinking sand.
522,2
522,When Darkness veils his lovely face
522,I rest on his unchanging grace.
522,in every high and stormy gale
522,my anchor holds within the veil.
522,3
522,His oath, his covenant, his blood
522,supports me in the whelming flood.
522,When all around my soul gives way
522,he then is all my hope and stay.
522,4
522,When He shall come with trumpet sound
522,O may I then in him be found!
522,Dressed in his righteousness alone
522,faultless to stand before the throne.
523,523 – My Faith Has Found a Resting Place
523,1
523,My faith has found a resting place
523,Not in a manmade creed;
523,I trust the ever living One
523,That He for me shall plead.
523,Refrain
523,I need no other evidence
523,I need no other plea;
523,It is enough that Jesus died
523,And rose again for me.
523,2

555,Thou mightest save our race
555,And give us life.
555,3
555,Thou are the great High Priest;
555,Thou has prepared the feast
555,Of heavenly love;
555,While in our mortal pain
555,None call on Thee in vain;
555,Help Thou does not disdain
555,Help from above.
555,4
555,Ever be Thou our Guide
555,Our Shepherd and our pride
555,Our staff and song;
555,Jesus, Thou Christ of God
555,By Thy perennial word
555,Lead us where Thou hast trod
555,Make our faith strong.
556,556 – As Saints of Old
556,1
556,As saints of old their first fruits brought
556,Of orchard, flock, and field
556,To God the giver all good
556,The source of bounteous yield;
556,So we today first fruits would bring:
556,The wealth of this good land
556,Of farm and market, shop and home
556,Of mind, and heart, and hand.
556,2
556,A world in need now summons us
556,To labor, love, and give;
556,To make our life an offering
556,To God, that all may live.
556,The Church of Christ is calling us
556,To make the dream come true:
556,A world redeemed by Christ-like love;
556,All life in Christ made new.
556,3
556,In gratitude and humble trust
556,We bring our best today
556,To serve Your cause and share Your love
556,With all along life’s way.
556,O God, who gave yourself to us
556,In Jesus Christ Your Son
556,Teach us to give ourselves each day
556,Until life’s work is done.
557,557 – Come, Ye Thankful People
557,1
557,Come, ye thankful people, come
557,Raise the song of harvest home;
557,All is safely gathered in
557,Ere the winter storms begin.
557,God our Maker doth provide
557,For our wants to be supplied;
557,Come to God’s own temple, come;
557,Raise the song of harvest home!
557,2
557,We ourselves are God’s own field
557,Fruit unto His praise to yield;
557,Wheat and tares together sown
557,Unto joy or sorrow grown;
557,First the blade and then the ear
557,Then the full corn shall appear;
557,Grant, O harvest Lord, that we
557,Wholesome grain and pure may be.
557,3
557,For the Lord our God shall come
557,And shall take His harvest home;
557,From His field shall purge away
557,All that doth offend, that day;
557,Give His angels charge at last
557,In the fire the tares to cast;
557,But the fruitful ears to store
557,In His garner evermore.
557,4
557,Then, thou church triumphant, come
557,Raise the song of harvest home;
557,All are safely gathered in
557,Free from sorrow, free from sin
557,There, forever purified
557,In God’s garner to abide;
557,Come, ten thousand angels, come
557,Raise the glorious harvest home!
558,558 – For the Fruits of His Creation
558,1
558,For the fruits of His creation, thanks be to God;
558,For the gifts to every nation, thanks be to God;
558,For the plowing, sowing, reaping
558,Silent growth while men are sleeping
558,Future needs in earth’s safe keeping, thanks be to God!
558,2
558,In the just reward of labor, God’s will is done;
558,In the hop we give our neighbor, God’s will is done;
558,In our worldwide take of caring
558,For the hungry and despairing
558,In the harvests men are sharing, God’s will is done.
558,3
558,For the harvests of His Spirit, thanks be to God;
558,For the good all men inherit, thanks be to God;
558,For the wonders that astound us
558,For the truths that still confound us
558,Most of all, that love has found us, thanks be to God!
559,559 – Now Thank We All Our God
559,1
559,Now thank we all our God
559,with heart and hands and voices
559,who wondrous things hath done
559,in whom His world rejoices;
559,Who, from our mothers’ arms
559,hath blessed us on our way
559,with countless gifts of love
559,and still is ours today.
559,2
559,O may this bounteous God
559,through all our life be near us
559,with ever joyful hearts
559,and blessed peace to cheer us;
559,and keep us still in grace
559,and guide us when perplexed;
559,and free us from all ills
559,in this world and the next.
559,3
559,All praise and thanks to God
559,the Father now be given;
559,the Son, and Him who reigns
559,with them in highest heaven;
559,the one eternal God
559,whom earth and heaven adore;
559,for thus it was, is now
559,and shall be evermore.
560,560 – Let All Things Now Living
560,1
560,Let all things now living a song of thanksgiving
560,To God the Creator triumphantly raise
560,Who fashioned and made us, protected and stayed us
560,Who guideth us on to the end of our days.
560,His banners are o’er us
560,His light goes before us
560,A pillar of fire shining forth in the night
560,‘Til shadows have vanished and darkness is banished
560,as forward we travel from light into light.
560,2
560,His law He enforces: the stars in their courses
560,The sun in His orbit, obediently shine;
560,The hills and the mountains, the rivers and fountains
560,The deeps of the ocean proclaim Him divine
560,We too should be voicing our love and rejoicing
560,With glad adoration a song let us raise
560,‘Til all things now living unite in thanksgiving
560,To God in the highest, hosanna and praise.
561,561 – We Plow the Fields
561,1
561,We plow the fields, and scatter
561,the good seed on the land
561,But it is fed and watered
561,by God’s almighty hand.
561,He sends the snow in winter
561,the warmth to swell the grain
561,The breezes and the sunshine
561,and soft refreshing rain.
561,Refrain
561,All good gifts around us
561,Are sent from heaven above;
561,Then thank the Lord, O thank the Lord
561,For all His love.
561,2
561,He only is the Maker
561,of all things near and far;
561,He paints the wayside flower
561,He lights the evening star.
561,The winds and waves obey Him
561,by Him the birds are fed;
561,Much more, to us His children
561,He gives our daily bread.
561,3
561,We thank Thee then, O Father
561,for all things bright and good
561,The seed-time and the harvest
561,our life, our health, and food.
561,Accept the gifts we to offer
561,for all Thy love imparts
561,And, what Thou most desirest
561,our humble, thankful hearts.
562,562 – Come, Sing a Song of Harvest
562,1
562,Come, sing a song of harvest, Of thanks for daily food!
562,To offer God the first-fruits is old as gratitude.
562,2
562,Long, long ago, the reapers, before they kept the feast
562,Put first-fruits in a basket, and took it to the priest.
562,3
562,Shall we, sometimes forgetful oh where creation starts
562,With science in our pockets lose wonder from our hearts?
562,4
562,May God, the great Creator, to whom all life belongs
562,Accept these gifts we offer, our service and our songs.
562,5
562,And lest the world go hungry while we ourselves are fed
562,Make each of us more ready to share our daily bread.
563,563 – Praise and Thanksgiving
563,1
563,Praise and thanksgiving let everyone bring
563,Unto our Father for every good thing.
563,All together joyfully sing!
564,564 – For Sunrise Hope and Sunset Calm
564,1
564,For sunrise hope and sunset calm
564,and all that lies between
564,For all the sweetness and the balm
564,that is and that has been
564,For comradeship for peace in strife
564,and light on darkened days;
564,For work to do and strength for life
564,we sing our hymn of praise.
564,2
564,But O, we press far, far above
564,these gifts of pure delight
564,And find in Thee, and in Thy love
564,contentment infinite.
564,O Lord, beloved, in whom are found
564,all joys of time and place
564,What will it be when joy is crowned
564,by vision of Thy face?

566,566 – Father, We Thank You
566,1
566,Father, we thank You for the light that shines all the day;
566,For the bright sky You have given most like Your heaven;
566,Father, we thank You.
566,2

566,For human skill’s exploration of Your creation;
566,Father, we thank You.
566,3

566,For Your command to call others sisters and brothers;
566,Father, we thank You.
566,4

566,Giving us hope for tomorrow through joy and sorrow;
566,Father, we thank You.
567,567 – Have Thine Own Way, Lord
567,1
567,Have thine own way, Lord! Have thine own way!
567,Thou art the potter, I am the clay.
567,Mold me and make me after thy will
567,while I am waiting, yielded and still.
567,2
567,Have thine own way, Lord! Have thine own way!
567,Search me and try me, Savior today!
567,Wash me just now, Lord, wash me just now
567,as in thy presence humbly I bow.
567,3
567,Have thine own way, Lord! Have thine own way!
567,Wounded and weary, help me I pray!
567,Power, all power, surely is thine!
567,Touch me and heal me, Savior divine!
567,4
567,Have thine own way, Lord! Have thine own way!
567,Hold o’er my being absolute sway.
567,Fill with thy Spirit till all shall see
567,Christ only, always, living in me!
568,568 – Make Me a Captive, Lord
568,1
568,Make me a captive, Lord
568,and then I shall be free;
568,Force me to render up my sword
568,and I shall conqueror be.
568,I sink in life’s alarms
568,when by myself I stand;
568,Imprison me within Thine arms
568,and strong shall be my hand.
568,2
568,My heart is weak and poor
568,until it amaster find;
568,It has no spring of action sure
568,it varies with the wind.
568,It cannot freely move till
568,Thou has wrought its chain;
568,Enslave it with Thy matchless love
568,and deathless it shall reign.
568,3
568,My will is not my own
568,till Thou hast made it Thine;
568,If it would reach a monarch’s throne
568,it must its crown resign;
568,It only stands unbent
568,amid the clashing strife
568,When on Thy bosom it has leant
568,and found in Thee its life.
569,569 – Pass Me Not, O Gentle Savior
569,1
569,Pass me not, O gentle Savior
569,hear my humble cry;
569,while on others thou art calling
569,do not pass me by.
569,Refrain
569,Savior, Savior, hear my humble cry;
569,while on others thou art calling
569,do not pass me by.
569,2
569,Let me at thy throne of mercy
569,find a sweet relief
569,kneeling there in deep contrition;
569,help my unbelief.
569,3
569,Trusting only in thy merit
569,would I seek thy face;
569,heal my wounded, broken spirit
569,save me by thy grace.
569,4
569,Thou the spring of all my comfort
569,more than life to me
569,whom have I on earth beside thee?
569,Whom in heaven but thee?
570,570 – Not I, But Christ
570,1
570,Not I, but Christ, be honored, loved, exalted;
570,Not I, but Christ, be seen, be known, be heard;
570,Not I, but Christ, in every look and action
570,Not I, but Christ, in every thought and word.
570,2
570,Not I, but Christ, to gently soothe in sorrow
570,Not I, but Christ, to wipe the falling tear;
570,Not I, but Christ, to lift the weary burden
570,Not I, but Christ, to hush away all fear.
570,3
570,Christ, only Christ! No idle words e’er falling
570,Christ, only Christ; no needless bustling sound;
570,Christ, only Christ, no self important bearing;
570,Christ, only Christ, no trace of “I” be found.
570,4
570,Not I, but Christ, my every need supplying
570,Not I, but Christ, my strength and health to be;
570,Christ, only Christ, for body, soul, and spirit
570,Christ, only Christ, here and eternally.
571,571 – What Does the Lord Require
571,1
571,What does the Lord require for praise and offering?
571,What sacrifice, desire or tribute bid you bring?
571,Do justly; Love mercy; Walk humbly with your God.
571,2
571,Rulers of men, give ear! Should you not justice show?
571,Will God your pleading hear, while crime and cruelty grow?
571,Do justly; Love mercy; Walk humbly with your God.
571,3
571,How shall our life fulfill God’s law so hard and high?
571,Let Christ endue our will with grace to fortify.
571,Then justly, in mercy we’ll humbly walk with God.
572,572 – Give of Your Best to the Master
572,1
572,Give of your best to the master
572,Give of the strength of your youth;
572,Throw your soul’s fresh, glowing ardor
572,Into the battle for truth.
572,Jesus has set the example –
572,Dauntless was He, young and brave;
572,Give Him your loyal devotion
572,Give Him the best that you have.
572,Refrain
572,Give of your best to the master
572,Give of the strength of your youth;
572,Clad in salvation’s full armor
572,Join in the battle for truth.
572,2
572,Give of your best to the Master
572,Give Him first place in your heart;
572,Give Him first place in your service
572,Consecrate every part.
572,Give, and to you shall be given –
572,God His beloved Son gave;
572,Gratefully seeking to serve Him
572,Give Him the best that you have.
572,3
572,Give of your best to the Master
572,Naught else is worthy His love;
572,He gave Himself for your ransom
572,Have up His glory above;
572,Laid down His life without murmur
572,You from sin’s ruin to save;
572,Give Him your heart’s adoration
572,Give Him the best that you have.
573,573 – Ill Go Where You Want Me to Go
573,1
573,It may not be on the mountain height
573,Or over the stormy sea
573,It may not be at the battle’s front
573,My Lord will have need of me.
573,But if, by a still, small voice he calls
573,To paths that I do not know
573,I’ll answer, dear Lord, with my hand in thine;
573,I’ll go where you want me to go.
573,Refrain
573,I’ll go where you want me to go, dear Lord
573,Over mountain or plain or sea;
573,I’ll say what you want me to say, dear Lord;
573,I’ll be what you want me to be.
573,2
573,Perhaps today there are loving words
573,Which Jesus would have me speak
573,There may be now in the paths of sin
573,Some wand’rer whom I should seek.
573,O Savior, if thou wilt be my guide
573,Tho dark and rugged the way
573,My voice shall echo the message sweet;
573,I’ll say what you want me to say.
573,3
573,There’s surely somewhere a lowly place
573,In earth’s harvest fields so wide
573,Where I may labor through life’s short day
573,For Jesus, the Crucified.
573,So trusting my all to thy tender care
573,And knowing thou lovest me
573,I’ll do thy will with a heart sincere:
573,I’ll be what you want me to be.
574,574 – O Master, Let Me Walk With Thee
574,1
574,O Master, let me walk with thee
574,in lowly paths of service free;
574,tell me thy secret; help me bear
574,the strain of toil, the fret of care.
574,2
574,Help me the slow of heart to move
574,by some clear, winning word of love;
574,teach me the wayward feet to stay
574,and guide them in the homeward way.
574,3
574,Teach me thy patience; still with thee
574,in closer, dearer company
574,in work that keeps faith sweet and strong
574,in trust that triumphs over wrong;
574,4
574,In hope that sends a shining ray
574,far down the future’s broadening way
574,in peace that only thou canst give
574,with thee, O Master, let me live.
575,575 – Let Your Heart Be Broken
575,1
575,Let your heart be broken for a world in need:
575,Feed the mouths that hunger, soothe the wounds that bleed
575,Give the cup of water and the loaf of bread
575,Be the hands of Jesus, serving in His stead.
575,2
575,Here on earth applying principles of love
575,Visible expression – God still rules above
575,Living illustration of the Living Word
575,To the minds of all who’ve Never seen or heard.
575,3
575,Blest to be a blessing privileged to care
575,Challenged by the need apparent everywhere.
575,Where mankind is wanting, fill the vacant place.
575,Be the means through which the Lord reveals His grace.
575,4
575,Add to your believing deeds that prove it true
575,Knowing Christ as Savior, make Him Master, too.
575,Follow in His footsteps, go where He has trod;
575,In the world’s great trouble risk yourself for God.
575,5
575,Let your heart be tender and your vision clear;
575,See mankind as God sees, serve Him far and near.
575,Let your heart be broken by a brother’s pain;
575,Share your rich resources, give and give again.
576,576 – Awake, Awake to Love and Work
576,1
576,Awake, awake to love and work!
576,The lark is in the sky;
576,The fields are wet with diamond dew;
576,The worlds awake to cry
576,Their blessings on the Lord of life
576,As He goes meekly by.
576,2
576,Come, let thy voice be one with theirs
576,Shout with their shout of praise;
576,See how the giant sun soars up
576,Great lord of years and days!
576,So let the love of Jesus come
576,And set thy soul ablaze.
576,3
576,To give and give, and give again
576,What God hath given thee;
576,To spend thyself nor count the cost;
576,To serve right gloriously
576,The God who gave all worlds that are
576,And all that are to be.
577,577 – In the Heart of Jesus
577,1
577,In the heart of Jesus there is love for you
577,Love most pure and tender, love most deep and true;
577,Why should you be lonely, why for friendship sigh
577,When the heart of Jesus has a full supply?
577,2
577,In the mind of Jesus there is thought for you
577,Warm as summer sunshine, sweet as morning dew;
577,Why should you be fearful, why take anxious thought
577,Since the mind of Jesus cares for those He bought?
577,3
577,In the field of Jesus there is work for you;
577,Such as even angels might rejoice to do;
577,Why stand idly sighing for some lifework grand
577,While the field of Jesus seeks your reaping hand?
577,4
577,In the home of Jesus there’s a place for you;
577,Glorious, bright, and joyous, calm and peaceful too;
577,Why then, like a wanderer, roam with weary pace
577,If the home of Jesus holds for you a place?
578,578 – So Send I You
578,1
578,So sent I you- by grace made strong to triumph
578,O’er hosts of hell, o’er darkness, death, and sin
578,My name to bear, and in that name to conquer-
578,So send I you, My victory to win.
578,2
578,So send I you- to take to souls in bondage
578,The word of truth that sets the captive fee
578,To break the bonds of sin, to loose dearth’s fetters-
578,So send I you, to bring the lost to Me.
578,3
578,So send I you- My strength to know in weakness
578,My joy in grief, my perfect peace in pain
578,To prove My power, My grace, My promised presence-
578,So send I you, eternal fruit to gain.
578,4
578,So Send I you – to bear My cross with patience
578,And then one day with joy to lay it down
578,To hear My voice, “Well done, My faithful servant –
578,Come, share My throne, My Kingdom, and My crown!”
578,As the Father hath sent Me, so send I You.”

581,581 – When the Church of Jesus
581,1
581,When the church of Jesus shuts its outer door
581,Lest the roar of traffic drown the voice of prayer:
581,May our prayers, Lord make up ten times more aware
581,That the world we banish is our Christian care.
581,2
581,If our hearts are lifted where devotion soars
581,High above this hungry suffering world of ours:
581,Lest our hymns should drug us to forget its needs
581,Forge our Christian worship into Christian deeds.
581,3
581,Lest the gifts we offer, money, talents, time
581,Serve to salve our conscience to our secret shame:
581,Lord, reprove, inspire us by the way you give;
581,Teach us, dying Savior, how true Christians live.
582,582 – Working, O Christ, With Thee
582,1
582,Working, O Christ, with Thee, working with Thee
582,Unworthy, sinful, weak, though we may be;
582,Our all to Thee we give, for Thee alone we live
582,And by Thy grace achieve, working with Thee.
582,2
582,Along the city’s waste, working with Thee
582,Our eager footsteps haste, like Thee to be;
582,The poor we gather in, the outcasts raise from sin
582,And labor souls to win, working with Thee.
582,3
582,Savior, we weary not, working with Thee
582,As hard as Thine our lot can never be;
582,Our joy and comfort this, “Thy grace sufficent is;”
582,This changes toil to bliss, working with Thee.
582,4
582,So let us labor on, working with Thee
582,Till earth to Thee is won, from sin set free;
582,Till men, from shore to shore, receive Thee, and adore
582,And join us evermore, working with Thee.

585,585 – When Christ Was Lifted From the Earth
585,1
585,When Christ was lifted from the earth
585,His arms stretched out above
585,Through every culture, every birth
585,to draw an answering love.
585,2
585,Still east and west His love extends
585,and always, near or far
585,He calls and claims us as His friends
585,and loves us as we are.
585,3
585,Where generation, class, or race
585,divides us to our shame
585,He sees not labels but a face
585,a person and a name.
585,4
585,Thus freely loved, tho’ fully known
585,may I in Christ be free
585,To welcome and accept His own
585,as Christ accepted me.
586,586 – What Joy It Is to Worship Here
586,1
586,What joy it is to worship here
586,And find ourselves at home
586,Where God, who uses every gift
586,Has room for all who come!
586,2
586,Yet are no two of us alike
586,Of all the human race
586,And we must seek a common ground
586,If we would share His grace.
587,587 – In Christ There Is No East nor West
587,1
587,In Christ there is no east nor west
587,In Him no south or north;
587,But one great fellowship of love
587,Throughout the whole wide earth.
587,2
587,In Him shall true heart everywhere
587,Their high communion find;
587,His service is the golden cord
587,Close binding all mankind.
587,3
587,Join hands, then, brothers of the faith
587,Whate’er your race may be.
587,Who serves my Father as a son
587,Is surely kin to me.
587,4
587,In Christ now meet both east and west
587,In Him meet south and north;
587,All Christly souls are one in Him
587,Throughout the whole wide earth.
588,588 – Lord of All Nations
588,1
588,Lord of all nations, grant me grace
588,To love all people, every race
588,And in each person may I see
588,My kindred loved, redeemed by Thee.
588,2
588,Break down the wall that would divide
588,Thy children, Lord, on every side.
588,My neighbor’s good let me pursue;
588,Let Christian love bind warm and true.
588,3
588,Forgive me, Lord, where I have erred
588,By loveless act and thoughtless word.
588,Make me to see the wrong I do
588,Will crucify my Lord anew.
588,4
588,Give me Thy courage, Lord, to speak
588,Whenever strong oppress the weak.
588,Should I myself the victim be
588,Help me forgive, remembering Thee.
588,5
588,With Thine own love may I be filled
588,And by Thy Holy Spirit willed
588,That all I touch, where’er I be
588,May be divinely touched by Thee.
589,589 – Holy Spirit, Gracious Guest
589,1
589,Holy Spirit, gracious guest
589,Hear and grant our heart’s request
589,For that gift supreme and best:
589,Holy heav’nly love.
589,2
589,Faith that mountains could remove
589,Tongues of earth or heaven above
589,Knowledge, all things, empty prove
589,If I have no love.
589,3
589,Though I as a martyr bleed
589,Give my goods the poor to feed
589,All is vain if love I need:
589,Therefore give me love.
589,4
589,Love is kind and suffers long
589,Love is pure and thinks no wrong
589,Love than death it self more strong:
589,Therefore give us love.
589,5
589,Prophecy will fade away
589,Melting in the light of day;
589,Love will ever with us stay:
589,Therefore give us love.
589,6
589,Faith and hope and love we see
589,Joining hand in hand agree-
589,But the greatest of the three
589,And the best is love.
590,590 – Trust and Obey
590,1
590,When we walk with the Lord
590,in the light of his word
590,what a glory he sheds on our way!
590,While we do his good will
590,he abides with us still
590,and with all who will trust and obey.
590,Refrain
590,Trust and obey, for there’s no other way
590,to be happy in Jesus, but to trust and obey.
590,2
590,Not a shadow can rise
590,not a cloud in the skies
590,but his smile quickly drives it away;
590,not a doubt nor a fear
590,not a sigh nor a tear
590,can abide while we trust and obey.
590,3
590,Not a burden we bear
590,not a sorrow we share
590,but our toil he doth richly repay;
590,not a grief or a loss
590,not a frown or a cross
590,but is blest if we trust and obey.
590,4
590,But we never can prove
590,the delights of his love
590,until all on the altar we lay;
590,for the favor he shows
590,and the joy he bestows
590,are for them who will trust and obey.
590,5
590,Then in fellowship sweet
590,we will sit at his feet
590,or we’ll walk by his side in the way;
590,what he says we will do
590,where he sends we will go;
590,never fear, only trust and obey.
591,591 – In Our Work and in Our Play
591,1
591,In our work and in our play
591,Jesus, ever with us stay;
591,May be always strive to be
591,True and faithful unto Thee.
591,Then we truthfully can sing
591,We are children of the King.
591,2
591,May we in Thy strength subdue
591,Evil tempers, words untrue
591,Thoughts impure, and deeds unkind
591,All things hateful to Thy mind.
591,Then we truthfully can sing
591,We are children of the King.
591,3
591,Children of the King are we!
591,May we loyal to Him be;
591,Try to please Him every day
591,In our work and in our play.
591,Then we truthfully can sing
591,We are children of the King.

592,1

592,what its signs of promise are.
592,Traveler, o’er yon mountain’s height
592,see that glory beaming star.
592,Watchman, does its beauteous ray
592,aught of joy or hope foretell?
592,Traveler, yes; it brings the day
592,promised day of Israel.
592,2
592,Watchman, tell us of the night
592,higher yet that star ascends.
592,Traveler, blessedness and light
592,peace and truth its course portends.
592,Watchman, will its beams alone
592,gild the spot that gave them birth?
592,Traveler, ages are its own;
592,See it bursts o’er all the earth.
592,3
592,Watchman, tell us of the night
592,for the morning seems to dawn.
592,Traveler, darkness takes its flight
592,doubt and terror are withdrawn.
592,Watchman, let your wanderings cease;
592,hasten to your quiet home.
592,Traveler, lo, the Prince of Peace
592,lo, the Son of God is come!

594,594 – Heir of the Kingdom
594,1
594,Heir of the kingdom, O why dost thou slumber?
594,Why art thou sleeping so near thy blest home?
594,Wake thee, arouse thee, and gird on thine armor
594,Speed, for the moments are hurrying on.
594,2
594,Heir of the kingdom, say, why dost thou linger?
594,How canst thou tarry in sight of the prize?
594,Up, and adorn thee, the Savior is coming;
594,Haste to receive Him descending the skies.
594,3
594,Earth’s mighty nations, in strife and commotion
594,Tremble with terror, and sink in dismay;
594,Listen, ’tis nought but the chariot’s loud rumbling;
594,Heir of the kingdom, no longer delay.
594,4
594,Stay not, O stay not for earth’s vain allurements!
594,See how its glory is passing away;
594,Break the strong fetters the foe hath bound o’er thee;
594,Heir of the kingdom, turn, turn thee away.
594,5
594,Keep the eye single, the head upward lifted;
594,Watch for the glory of earth’s coming King;
594,Lo! o’er the mountaintops light is now breaking;
594,Heirs of the kingdom, rejoice ye and sing.
595,595 – Let Every Lamp Be Burning
595,1
595,Let every lamp be burning bright
595,The darkest hour is nearing;
595,The darkest hour of earth’s long night
595,Before the Lord’s appearing.
595,Refrain
595,Then trim your lamps, my brethren dear
595,Then trim your lamps with godly fear;
595,The Master’s coming draweth near
595,Let every lamp be burning.
595,2

595,The last great message spuring
595,Wel’ll rest our living faith upon
595,His promise of returning.
595,3

595,We cannot be mistaken;
595,Though dangers rise on every side
595,We shall not be forsaken.
595,4

595,To help the world atound us;
595,Obedience bring the blessing near
595,When faith has firmly bound us.

596,1

596,Look for the way-marks passing one by one;
596,Down through the ages, past the kingdoms four—
596,Where are we standing? Look the way-marks o’er.
596,Refrain
596,Look for the way-marks, the great prophetic way-marks
596,Down through the ages, past the kingdoms four.
596,Look for the waymarks, the great prophetic way-marks;
596,The journey’s almost o’er.
596,2

596,Then Medo-Persia’s banners were unfurled;
596,And after Greece held universal sway
596,Rome seized the scepter—where are we today?
596,3
596,Down in the feet of iron and of clay
596,Weak and divided, soon to pass away;
596,What will the next great, glorious drama be?
596,Christ and His coming, and eternity.

600,600 – Hold Fast Till I Come
600,1
600,Sweet promise is given to all who believe–
600,“Behold I come quickly, Mine own to receive;
600,Hold fast till I come; the danger is great;
600,Sleep not as do others; be watchful, and wait.”
600,Refrain
600,“Hold fast till I come,” sweet promise of heaven–
600,“The kingdom restored, to you shall be given.”
600,“Come, enter My joy, sit down on the throne;
600,Bright crowns are in waiting; hold fast till I come.”
600,2
600,We’ll “watch unto prayer” with lamps burning bright;
600,He comes to all others a “thief in the night.”
600,We know He is near, but know not the day–
600,As spring shows that summer is not far away.
600,3
600,Yes! this is our hope, ’tis built on His word–
600,The glorious appearing of Jesus, our Lord;
600,Of promises all, it stands as the sum:
600,“Behold I come quickly; hold fast till I come.”

602,602 – O Brother, Be Faithful
602,1
602,O brother be faithful! soon Jesus will come
602,For whom we have waited so long;
602,O, soon we shall enter our glorious home
602,And join in the conqueror’s song.
602,O brother be faithful! for why should we prove
602,Unfaithful to Him who had shown
602,Such deep, such unbounded and infinite love
602,Who died to redeem us His own.
602,2
602,O brother be faithful! the city of gold
602,Prepared for the good and the blest
602,Is waiting its portals of pearl to unfold
602,And welcome thee into thy rest.
602,Then, brother be faithful! not long shall we stay
602,In weariness here, and forlorn
602,Time’s dark night of sorrow is wearing away
602,We haste to the glorious morn.
602,3
602,O brother be faithful! He soon will descend
602,Creation’s omnipotent King
602,While legions of angels His chariot attend
602,And palm wreaths, of victory bring.
602,O brother be faithful! and soon shalt thou hear
602,They Savior pronounce the glad word
602,Well done, faithful servant, they title is clear
602,To enter the joy of thy Lord.
602,4
602,O brother be faithful! eternity’s years
602,Shall tell for thy faithfulness now
602,When bright smiles of gladness shall scatter thy tears
602,A coronet gleam on thy brow.
602,O brother be faithful! the promise is sure
602,That waits for the faithful and tried;
602,To reign with the ransomed, immortal and pure
602,And ever with Jesus abide.

604,who are seeking salvation;

605,605 – My Soul, Be on Thy Guard
605,1
605,My soul, be on they guard!
605,Ten thousand foes arise;
605,The hosts of sin are pressing hard
605,To draw thee from the skies.
605,2
605,O watch, and fight, and pray!
605,The battle ne’er give o’er;
605,Renew it boldly every day
605,And help divine implore.
605,3

605,Nor lay thine armor down;

606,606 – Once to Every Man and Nation
606,1
606,Once to every man and nation
606,comes the moment to decide
606,In the strife of truth with falsehood
606,for the good or evil side;
606,Some great cause, some great decision
606,offering each the bloom or blight
606,And the choice goes by forever
606,’twixt that darkness and that light.
606,2
606,Then to side with truth is noble
606,when we share her wretched crust
606,Ere her cause bring fame and profit
606,and ’tis prosperous to be just;
606,Then it is the brave man chooses
606,while the coward stands aside
606,Till the multitude make virtue
606,of the faith they had denied.
606,3
606,By the light of burning martyrs
606,Christ, Thy bleeding feet we track
606,Toiling up new Calv’ries ever
606,with the cross that turns not back;
606,New occasions teach new duties
606,time makes ancient good uncouth
606,They must upward still and onward
606,who would keep abreast of truth.
606,4
606,Though the cause of evil prosper
606,yet the truth alone is strong;
606,Though her portion be the scaffold
606,and upon the throne be wrong;
606,Yet that scaffold sways the future
606,and behind the dim unknown
606,Standeth God within the shadow
606,keeping watch above His own.

607,Gird our lives that they may be

609,and shall I fear to own his cause
609,or blush to speak his name?
609,2

609,on flowery beds of ease
609,while others fought to win the prize
609,and sailed through bloody seas?
609,3

609,Must I not stem the flood?
609,Is this vile world a friend to grace
609,to help me on to God?

609,supported by thy word

609,6

609,and all thy armies shine

612,with the cross of Jesus going on before.

613,613 – Fight the Good Fight
613,1
613,Fight the good fight with all thy might;
613,Christ is thy strength, and Christ thy right;
613,Lay hold on life and it shall be
613,Thy joy and crown eternally.
613,2
613,Run the straight race through God’s good grace;
613,Lift up thine eyes, and seek His face.
613,Life with its path before us lies;
613,Christ is the way, and Christ the prize.
613,3
613,Cast care aside, lean on thy guide
613,His boundless mercy will provide;
613,Trust, and the trusting soul shall prove
613,Christ is its life, and Christ its love.
613,4
613,Faint not, nor fear, His arms are near;
613,He changeth not, and thou art dear.
613,Only believe, and thou shalt see
613,That Christ is all in all to thee.
614,614 – Sound the Battle Cry
614,1

614,See! the foe is nigh;
614,Raise the standard high
614,For the Lord;
614,Gird your armor on
614,Stand firm, every one
614,Rest your cause upon His holy word.
614,Refrain

614,rally round the banner!

614,Onward, forward, shout aloud hosanna!
614,Christ is Captain of the mighty throng.
614,2
614,Strong to meet the foe
614,Marching on we go
614,While our cause we know
614,Must prevail;
614,Shield and banner bright
614,Gleaming in the light
614,Battling for the right
614,We ne’er can fail.
614,3

614,Hear us when we call
614,Help us, one and all
614,By Thy grace;
614,When the battle’s done
614,And the victory won

614,Before Thy face.

616,616 – Soldiers of Christ, Arise
616,1
616,Soldiers of Christ,arise
616,And put your armor on
616,Strong in the strength which God supplies
616,Through His eternal Son
616,Strong in the Lord of hosts
616,And in His mighty power
616,Who in the strength of Jesus trusts
616,Is more than conqueror.
616,2
616,Stand then in His great might
616,With all His strength endued
616,But take, to arm you for the fight
616,The panoply of God;
616,That, having all things done
616,And all your conflicts passed
616,Ye may o’ercome through Christ alone
616,And stand entire at last.
616,3
616,From strength to strength go on
616,Wrestle and fight and pray
616,Tread all the powers of darkness down
616,And win the well-fought day.
616,Still let the Spirit cry
616,In all His soldiers, “Come!”
616,Till Christ the Lord who reigns on high
616,Shall take the conquerors home.
617,617 – We Are Living, We Are Dwelling
617,1
617,We are living, we are dwelling
617,In a grand and awful time
617,In an age on ages telling
617,To be living is sublime.
617,Hark! the waking up of nations
617,Gog and Magog to the fray;
617,Hark! what soundeth? Is creation
617,Groaning for her latter day?
617,2
617,Christian, rouse and arm for conflict
617,Nerve thee for the battlefield;
617,Bear the helmet of salvation
617,And the mighty gospel shield;
617,Let the breastplate, peace, be on thee
617,Take the Spirit’s sword in hand;
617,Boldly, fearlessly, go forth then
617,In Jehovah’s strength to stand.
617,3
617,And the prince of evil spirits
617,Great deceiver of the world!
617,He who at the blessed Jesus
617,Once his deadly weapons hurled
617,Cometh with unwonted power
617,Knowing that his reign will cease
617,When the kingdom shall be given
617,To the mighty Prince of Peace.
617,4
617,Christians, rouse! fight in this warfare
617,Cease not till the victory’s won;
617,Till your Captain loud proclaimeth
617,“Servant of the Lord, well done!”
617,He, alone, who thus is faithful
617,Who abideth to the end
617,Hath the promise, in the kingdom
617,An eternity to spend.

618,He with the King of glory

619,619 – Lead On, O King Eternal
619,1

619,the day of march has come;
619,henceforth in fields of conquest
619,thy tents shall be our home.

619,thy grace has made us strong;
619,and now, O King eternal
619,we lift our battle song.
619,2

619,till sin’s fierce war shall cease
619,and holiness shall whisper
619,the sweet amen of peace.
619,For not with swords loud clashing
619,nor roll of stirring drums;
619,with deeds of love and mercy
619,the heavenly kingdom comes.
619,3

619,we follow, not with fears
619,for gladness breaks like morning
619,where’er thy face appears.
619,Thy cross is lifted o’er us
619,we journey in its light;
619,the crown awaits the conquest;
619,lead on, O God of might.

623,And rejoice to follow Thee.

623,5

625,By faith, on Heaven’s table land

625,Where doubts arise and fears dismay;

625,The song of saints on higher ground.
625,4

625,And catch a gleam of glory bright;

628,628 – As Jacob With Travel Was Weary
628,1
628,As Jacob with travel was weary one day
628,At night on a stone for a pillow he lay;
628,He saw in a vision a ladder so high
628,That its foot was on earth and its top in the sky.
628,Refrain
628,Alleluia to Jesus who died on the tree
628,And has raised up a ladder of mercy for me
628,And has raised up a ladder of mercy for me.
628,2
628,Come let us ascend! All may climb it who will;
628,For the angels of Jacob are guarding it still:
628,And remember each step that by faith we passo’er
628,Some prophet or martyr has trod it before.
628,3
628,And when we arrive at the haven of rest
628,We shall hear the glad words, “Come up hither, ye blest
628,Here are regions of light, here are mansions of bliss.”
628,O who would not climb such a ladder as this?
629,629 – O Happy Band of Pilgrims
629,1
629,O happy band of pilgrims
629,If onward ye will tread
629,With Jesus as your fellow
629,To Jesus as your Head!
629,2
629,O happy if ye labor
629,As Jesus did for men;
629,O happy if ye hunger
629,As Jesus hungered then!
629,3
629,The trials that beset you
629,The sorrows ye endure
629,The manifold temptations
629,That death alone can cure
629,4
629,What are they but His jewels
629,Of right celestial worth?
629,What are they but the ladder
629,Set up to heaven on earth?
629,5
629,O happy band of pilgrims
629,Look upward to the skies
629,Where such a light affliction
629,Shall win you such a prize!
630,630 – Rise, My Soul, and Stretch Thy Wings
630,1
630,Rise, my soul, and stretch thy wings
630,thy better portion trace;
630,Rise from transitory things
630,toward heaven, thy native place;
630,Sun, and moon, and stars decay;
630,time shall soon this earth remove;
630,Rise, my soul, and haste away
630,to seats prepared above.
630,2
630,Rivers to the ocean run
630,nor stay in all their course;
630,Fire ascending seeks the sun;
630,both speed them to their source;
630,So a soul that’s born of God
630,longs to view His glorious face
630,Forward tends to His abode
630,to rest in His embrace.
630,3
630,Cease, ye pilgrims, cease to mourn;
630,press onward to the prize;
630,Soon our Savior will return
630,triumphant in the skies;
630,Yet a season, and you know
630,happy entrance will be given
630,All our sorrows left below
630,and earth exchanged for heaven.
631,631 – When on Life a Darkness Falls
631,1
631,When on life a darkness falls
631,When the mist flows chilling
631,Paths and sign posts lost in doubt
631,Loveless, unfulfilling
631,Reach us, Jesus, from Your cross
631,Though we feel forsaken;
631,Keep us through the aching night
631,Till new dawns awaken.
631,2
631,When the dreams and vows of youth
631,Painfully accuse us
631,Stab our conscience, steal our worth
631,Christ will not refuse us:
631,Peace the world cannot provide
631,Daily resurrection
631,Strong companion at our side
631,For each new direction.
631,3
631,Come and meet Him, Friend and Lord
631,Thro’ the gospel story:
631,Open door to life and peace
631,Window into glory.
631,All who seek Him, soon are found
631,Made His close relation:
631,Christ our pathway, Christ our home
631,Christ our sure foundation.
632,632 – Until Then
632,1
632,My heart can sing when I pause to remember
632,A heartache here is but a stepping stone.
632,Along a trail, thats winding always upward
632,This troubled world, is not my final home.
632,Refrain
632,But until then, my heart will go on singing
632,Until then, with joy I’ll carry on
632,Until the day my eyes behold the city
632,Until the day God calls me home.
632,2
632,The things of earth will dim and lose their value
632,If we recall they’re borrowed for awhile;
632,And things of earth that cause the heart to tremble
632,Remembered there, will only bring a smile.

633,1

633,He’ll prepare for us a place.

633,What a day of rejoicing that will be!
633,When we all see Jesus
633,We’ll sing and shout the victory!
633,2

633,Clouds will overspread the sky;
633,But when traveling days are over
633,Not a shadow, not a sigh.
633,3

633,Trusting, serving every day;
633,Just one glimpse of him in glory
633,Will the toils of life repay.
633,4
633,Onward to the prize before us!
633,Soon his beauty we’ll behold;
633,Soon the pearly gates will open;
633,We shall tread the streets of gold.

634,1
634,Come, all Christians, be committed
634,To the service of the lord;
634,Make your lives for him more fitted
634,Tune your hearts with one accord.
634,Come into His courts with gladness
634,Each his sacred vows renew
634,Turn away from sin and sadness
634,Be transformed with life anew.
634,2
634,Of your time and talents give ye
634,They are gifts from God above;
634,To be used by Christians freely
634,To proclaim His wondrous love.
634,Come again to serve the Savior
634,Tithes and off’rings with you bring.
634,In your work, with Him find favor
634,And with joy His praises sing.
634,3

634,Is required of every one;
634,Showing mercy to one another
634,Mirrors His redemptive plan.
634,In compassion He has given
634,Of His love that is divine;
634,On the cross sins were forgiven;
634,Joy and peace are fully thine.
634,4
634,Come in praise and adoration
634,All who in Christ’s name believe;
634,Worship Him with consecration
634,Grace and love you will receive.

634,And repeat the gospel story
634,Till mankind His name has heard.
635,635 – Lord of All Good

635,Use them Your holy purpose to fulfill.

635,That our whole life is offered to Your will.
635,2
635,We give our minds to understand Your ways;
635,Hands, voices, eyes to serve Your great design;
635,Hearts with the flame of your own love ablaze:
635,Thus for Your glory all our pow’rs combine.
635,3
635,Father, whose bounty all creation shows;
635,Christ, by whose willing sacrifice we live;
635,Spirit, from whom all life in fullness flows:
635,To You with grateful hearts ourselves we give.
636,636 – God, Whose Giving Knows No Ending
636,1
636,God, whose giving knows no ending
636,From Your rich and endless store:
636,Nature’s wonder, Jesus’ wisdom
636,Costly cross, grave’s shattered door.
636,Gifted by You, we turn to You
636,Off’ring up ourselves in praise:
636,Thankful song shall rise forever
636,Gracious donor of our days.
636,2
636,Skills and time are ours for pressing
636,Toward the goals of Christ, Your Son:
636,All at peace in health and freedom
636,Races joined, the church made one.
636,Now direct our daily labor
636,Lest we strive for self alone:
636,Born with talents, make us servants
636,Fit to answer at Your throne.
636,3
636,Treasure, too, You have entrusted
636,Gain through pow’rs Your grace conferred:
636,Ours to use for home and kindred
636,And to spread the Gospel Word.
636,Open wide our hands in sharing
636,As we heed Christ’s ageless call.
636,Healing, teaching, and reclaiming
636,Serving You by loving all.
637,637 – Son of God, Eternal Savior
637,1
637,Son of God, eternal Savior
637,Source of life and truth and grace
637,Work made flesh, whose birth among us
637,Hallows all our human race
637,You our head, who throned in glory
637,For Your own will ever plead:
637,Fill us with Your love and pity
637,Heal our wrongs, and help our need.
637,2
637,Bind us all as one together
637,In Your church’s sacred fold
637,Weak and healthy, poor and wealthy
637,Sad and joyful, young and old.
637,Is there want or pain or sorrow?
637,Make us all the burden share.
637,Are there spirits crushed and broken?
637,Teach us, Lord, to soothe their care.
637,3
637,As You, Lord, have lived for others
637,So may we for others live.
637,Freely have Your gifts been granted;
637,Freely may Your servants give.
637,Yours the gold and Yours the silver
637,Yours the wealth of land and sea;
637,We but stewards of Your bounty
637,Held in solemn trust will be.
637,4
637,Come, O Christ, and reign among us
637,King of love and Prince of Peace;
637,Hush the storm of strife and passion
637,Bid its cruel discords cease.
637,By Your patient years of toiling
637,By Your silent hours of pain
637,Quench our fevered thirst of pleasure
637,Stem our selfish greed of gain.
637,5
637,Son of God, eternal Savior
637,Source of life and truth and grace
637,Word made flesh, whose birth among us
637,Hallows all our human race:
637,By Your praying, by Your willing
637,That Your people should be one
637,Grant, oh, grant our hope’s fruition:
637,Here on earth Your will be done.
638,638 – The Wise May Bring Their Learning

638,To follow in His ways:
638,And these be the treasures
638,We offer to the King
638,And these are gifts that ever
638,The poorest child may bring.
638,3

638,We have to do each day;
638,We’ll try our best to please Him
638,At home, at school, at play:
638,And better are these treasures
638,To offer to the King
638,Than richest gift without them:
638,Yet these a child may bring.

641,641 – God in His Love for Us
641,1

641,Gave it a purpose in time and in space:
641,Small as a spark from the fire of creation
641,Cradle of life and the home of our race.
641,2

641,Life that sustains us in body and mind:
641,Plenty for all, if we learn how to share it
641,Riches undreamed of to fathom and find.
641,3

641,Long has earth bowed to the terror of forced;

641,Poisoned the fountain of life at its source.
641,4

641,Ours, as His stewards, to farm and defend.
641,From its pollution, misuse, and destruction
641,Good Lord, deliver us, world without end!
